------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Maori Bible: Psalms

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> ¶ Ka hari te tangata kahore nei e haere i
te whakaaro o te tangata kino, a kahore e tu i te ara o te hunga hara,
kahore ano e noho i te nohoanga o te hunga whakahi.

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> Engari ko te ture a Ihowa tana e
whakaahuareka ai; kei tona ture ona whakaaro i te ao, i te po.

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> E rite hoki ia ki te rakau i whakatokia ki
te taha o nga awa wai, e whai hua nei i te po e hua ai: e kore tona rau
e memenga; a ka pono ana mea katoa e mea ai ia.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> ¶ E kore e pera nga tangata kino; engari ka
rite ki te papapa e aia ana e te hau.

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Ae ra, e kore e tu te hunga kino i te
whakawakanga, me te hunga hara i te whakaminenga o te hunga tika.

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> E matau ana hoki a Ihowa ki te ara o te
hunga tika: ko te ara ia o te hunga kino e ngaro.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> ¶ He aha ka nana ai nga tauiwi, ka whakaaro
horihori ai nga iwi?

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> Whakatika mai ana nga kingi o te whenua,
runanga tahi ana nga ariki, ki te whawhai ki a Ihowa, ki tana tangata
hoki i whakawahi ai; me te ki ano,

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Kia motumotuhia e tatou a raua here, kia
akiritia a raua taura i a tatou.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> Ko ia kei te rangi e noho ana, ka kata ia:
ka whakahi te Ariki ki a ratou.

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> Na ka korero ia ki a ratou me te riri ano:
ka tino weriweri hoki, ka whakahorere i a ratou,

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> Ahakoa ra ka whakawahia e ahau taku kingi
ki runga ki taku maunga tapu, ki Hiona.

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> ¶ Maku e whakapuaki te kupu, kua mea a
Ihowa ki ahau, Ko koe taku tama, nonaianei koe i whakatupuria ai e ahau.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> Inoi ki ahau, a ka hoatu e ahau ki a koe
nga tauiwi hei kainga mou, me nga topito o te whenua hei nohoanga tupu
mou.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> Ka wawahi koe i a ratou ki te whiu rino,
mongamonga noa ratou i a koe, ano he oko na te kaihanga rihi.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> ¶ Na kia mahara ra, e nga kingi: kia
akona, e nga kaiwhakawa o te whenua.

<span id="an_2:11">2:11</span> Mahi atu ki a Ihowa i runga i te wehi,
kia hari me te wiri.

<span id="an_2:12">2:12</span> Kihia te tama kei riri ia, a ka mate
koutou i te ara, ka hohoro tonu hoki te mura o tona riri. Ka hari katoa
te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, i tona omanga atu i
tana tama i a Apoharama. E Ihowa, ano te tini o oku hoariri, he tokomaha
te hunga e whakatika mai ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> He tokomaha te mea ana ki toku wairua, hore
rawa he whakaoranga mona i te Atua. (Hera.

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, hei whakangungu rakau
moku, hei kororia moku, hei kaiwhakaara i toku matenga.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> ¶ I karanga toku reo ki a Ihowa: a
whakahoki kupu mai ana ia ki ahau i tona maunga tapu. (Hera.

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> I takoto ahau, i moe; i ara ake ano; na
Ihowa hoki ahau i whakamau ake.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> E kore ahau e mataku i nga mano tini o te
iwi, kua whakatika mai nei ki ahau karopoti noa.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> Whakatika, e Ihowa; whakaorangia ahau, e
toku Atua: nau hoki i patu te kauae o oku hoariri katoa; mangungu noa i
a koe nga niho o te hunga kino.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> Na Ihowa te whakaoranga: kei runga i tau
iwi tau manaaki. (Hera.

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He
himene na Rawiri. Whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e te Atua o toku tika,
ina karanga ahau: i ahau i te pouri i whakaputaina ahau e koe; kia
atawhai ki ahau, whakarongo ki taku inoi.

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> E nga tama a te tangata, kia pehea te roa o
ta koutou mea i toku kororia hei whakama, o ta koutou aroha ki te
horihori, o ta koutou whai i te teka? (Hera.

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> Otiia kia mohio koutou he mea momotu ke na
Ihowa te tangata tapu mana: e whakarongo a Ihowa ua karanga ahau ki a
ia.

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> Kia oho koutou, a kaua e hara: korerorero
ki o koutou ngakau i runga i o koutou moenga, me te ata takoto ano.
(Hera.

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Patua nga whakahere o te tika, me te okioki
ano ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> ¶ He tokomaha te mea ana, Ma wai e
whakakite te pai ki a matou? Kia ara, e Ihowa, te marama o tou mata ki
runga ki a matou.

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> Hira ake te hari i homai e koe ki roto ki
toku ngakau i to ratou i te wa i hua ai a ratou witi, ta ratou waina.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> Ka takoto marire ahau, a moe tonu iho: ko
koe anake hoki, e Ihowa, hei mea kia au toku noho.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nehiroto. He
himene na Rawiri. Tahuri tou taringa, e Ihowa, ki aku kupu, kia mohio
koe ki toku whakaaroaronga.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Whakarongo ki te reo o taku karanga, e toku
Kingi, e toku Atua, he inoi hoki taku ki a koe.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> E rongo koe ki toku reo, e Ihowa, i te ata;
i te ata ka whakatikaia atu e ahau taku inoi ki a koe, a ka titiro
matatau atu.

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> Ehara hoki koe i te Atua e pai ana ki te
hara, e kore te kino e noho ki a koe.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> E kore te hunga wairangi e tu ki tou
aroaro: e kinongia ana e koe nga kaimahi katoa i te kino.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> E ngaro i a koe te hunga korero teka; e
whakarihariha ana a Ihowa ki te tangata toto, ki te tangata hianga.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> ¶ Ko ahau ia ka haere i runga i te tini o
au atawhai ki tou whare: ka koropiko ki te ritenga o tau temepara tapu,
me te wehi ano ki a koe.

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> E Ihowa, arahina ahau i runga i tou tika,
he hoariri hoki oku; whakatikaia tau ara i mua i ahau.

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> Kahore hoki he pono i o ratou mangai; he
kino kau a roto i a ratou; he urupa puare noa o ratou korokoro; e
patipati ana o ratou arero.

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> Whakataua te hara ki a ratou, e te Atua;
kia hinga ratou i o ratou whakaaro; peia atu ratou me a ratou tini mahi
tutu; mo ratou i whakakeke ki a koe.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Na kia hari katoa te hunga e
whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe: kia hamama tonu ratou i te koa, mo ratou e
hipokina nei e koe; a kia whakamanamana ki a koe te hunga e aroha ana ki
tou ingoa.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> No te mea ka manaakitia e koe, e Ihowa,
te tangata tika; me he whakangungu rakau te manako e karapotia ai ia e
koe.

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto, he mea
Heminiti. He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kaua e whakatupehupehu mai ki
ahau, ina riri koe, kaua ano ahau e pakia ina arita mai koe.

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> E Ihowa, tohungia ahau, he ngoikore hoki
ahau: rongoatia ahau, e Ihowa, e ohooho ana hoki oku wheua.

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> E ohooho noa iho ana hoki toku wairua: ko
koe ia, e Ihowa, kia pehea atu te roa?

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> Hoki mai, e Ihowa, kia mawhiti atu toku
wairua: kia mahara ki tou aroha, a whakaorangia ahau.

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Kahore hoki he mahara ki a koe ina mate: ko
wai hei whakawhetai ki a koe i roto i te reinga?

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> Mauiui iho ahau i toku auetanga; e manu ana
toku moenga i ahau a pau noa te po; e whakamakukuria ana e ahau toku
takotoranga ki oku roimata.

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> Pakoko kau toku kanohi i te tangi; kua
koroheke haere i oku hoariri katoa.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> ¶ Mawehe atu i ahau, e nga kaimahi katoa i
te kino; kua rongo nei hoki a Ihowa i te reo o taku tangi.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Kua rongo a Ihowa ki taku inoi; ka manako a
Ihowa ki taku karakia.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> Ka whakama, ka pokaikaha noa iho oku
hoariri katoa: ka hoki ratou, ka pa whakarere atu te whakama.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> ¶ He Hikaiono na Rawiri, tana i waiata ai
ki a Ihowa mo nga kupu a Kuhu Pineamine. E Ihowa, e toku Atua, kei a koe
toku whakawhirinakitanga: kia ora ahau i te hunga katoa e aru ana i
ahau, kia mawhiti atu hoki ahau:

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> Kei haehae ia i toku wairua, ano he raiona,
a titaritari noa, i te mea kahore he kaiarai.

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, ki te mea naku tena
mahi, ki te mea he hara kei oku ringa;

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> Ki te mea i whakahokia e ahau he kino ki te
tangata kua mau nei ta maua rongo; i whakaora nei hoki ahau i te tangata
i kino noa mai ki ahau:

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> Kia arumia toku wairua e te hoariri, a kia
mau; kia takahia hoki toku ora e ia ki te whenua, kia whakatokotoria ano
toku kororia ki te puehu. (Hera.

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> E Ihowa, whakatika, kia riri koe, ara ake,
e nana nei hoki oku hoa whawhai: kia oho ake hoki koe moku; kua kiia e
koe te whakawa.

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> Tukua kia karapotia koe e te whakaminenga o
nga iwi: ma runga atu i a ratou tou hokinga atu ki runga.

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> Ko Ihowa e whakarite whakawa ana mo nga
iwi; kia rite, e Ihowa, tau whakawa moku ki taku mahi tika, ki te
tapatahi hoki o oku whakaaro.

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> Kia whakamutua te kino o te hunga kino:
whakaukia hoki te tangata tika: e whakamatautau ana hoki te Atua tika i
nga ngakau, i nga whatumanawa.

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> ¶ Kei te Atua toku whakangungu rakau,
mana e whakaora te hunga ngakau tika.

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> He kaiwhakawa tika te Atua, ae ra, he
Atua e riri ana i tenei ra, i tenei ra.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> Ki te kore tetahi e tahuri, ka whakakoia
e ia tana hoari; kua whakapikoa e ia tana kopere, a oti rawa te
whakapai.

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Oti rawa ano ana mea whakamate te
whakapai e ia; kua meinga e ia ana pere ano he ahi.

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> Nana, he kino te mea e whakamamae nei ia;
he whanoke te mea i hapu ki roto ki a ia, a whanau ake he teka.

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> I pokaia e ia he poka, he mea keri nana,
taka iho ia ki roto ki te rua i mahia e ia.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> Ka hoki tona whanoke ki tona matenga, a
ka tau iho tana tukino ki tona tumuaki.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> Ka rite ki tona tika taku whakamoemiti ki
a Ihowa: ka himene atu hoki ahau ki te ingoa o Ihowa, o te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. He
himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, e to matou Ariki, ano te nui o tou ingoa i te
whenua katoa! Paku ana i a koe tou kororia ki runga ake i nga rangi!

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> U pu i a koe te kaha o te mangai o nga
kohungahunga, o nga mea ngote u hei mea mo ou hoariri, hei pehi mo te
hoariri, mo te kairapu utu.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> ¶ Ka titiro ahau ki au rangi, ki te mahi a
ou maihao, ki te marama, ki nga whetu, i hanga nei e koe;

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> He aha te tangata i maharatia ai e koe? te
tama ranei a te tangata i tirohia ai ia e koe?

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> Nohinohi nei te wahi i whakaititia iho ai
ia e koe i te Atua, karaunatia ana ia e koe ki te kororia, ki te honore.

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Waiho iho e koe hei kingi mo nga mahi a ou
ringa; kua waiho e koe nga mea katoa i raro i ona waewae;

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> Nga hipi katoa, nga puru, me nga kirehe
katoa o te parae;

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Te manu o te rangi, me te ika o te moana, e
tere nei i nga ara o nga moana.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> E Ihowa, e to matou Ariki, ano te nui o tou
ingoa i te whenua katoa!

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Muturapena. He
himene na Rawiri. Ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te whakamoemiti ki a
Ihowa, ka korerotia e ahau au mahi whakamiharo katoa.

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> Ka koa ahau, ka whakamanamana ki a koe, ka
himene atu ki tou ingoa, e te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> I te hokinga whakamuri o oku hoariri,
tutuki ana ratou, ngaro iho i tou aroaro.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> Nau hoki i whakatika aku korero me toku
whakawa; i runga koe i te torona e noho ana, e whakarite tika ana.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> Kua whakatupehupehu koe ki nga tauiwi, huna
ana e koe te tangata kino, horoia atu ana to ratou ingoa ake ake.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Ko te hoariri, mutu pu ratou, he ngaromanga
oti tonu iho: a ko nga pa i huna e koe, ngaro whakarere to ratou
whakamaharatanga.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> Ko Ihowa ia noho tonu hei kingi ake, ake:
kua whakapaia e ia tona torona mo te whakawa.

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> A e whakarite ia mo te ao i runga i te
tika, ka whakatakoto tikanga mo nga iwi i runga i te pono.

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> Hei pa teko ano a Ihowa mo te tangata e
tukinotia ana, hei pa teko i nga wa o te he.

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> A ka whakawhirinaki ki a koe te hunga e
matau ana ki tou ingoa: no te mea e kore e whakarerea e koe, e Ihowa, te
hunga e rapu ana i a koe.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> ¶ Himene ki a Ihowa e noho nei i Hiona:
whakapuakina i waenganui i nga iwi ana mahi.

<span id="an_9:12">9:12</span> Ka whakataki toto ia, ka mahara ia ki a
ratou: kahore e wareware i a ia te karanga a te hunga iti.

<span id="an_9:13">9:13</span> Tohungia ahau, e Ihowa; titiro ki toku
mate i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, e te kaiwhakaara i ahau i nga tatau
o te mate:

<span id="an_9:14">9:14</span> Kia whakakitea katoatia ai e ahau ou
whakamoemiti i nga tatau o te tamahine o Hiona: ka hari ahau ki tau
whakaoranga.

<span id="an_9:15">9:15</span> Kua tapoko nga tauiwi ki te rua i keria e
ratou: kua mau to ratou waewae i roto i te kupenga i huna e ratou.

<span id="an_9:16">9:16</span> Kua matauria a Ihowa ki te whakawa e
whakaritea ana e ia: he mahanga mo te tangata kino te mahi a ona ringa.
(Hikaiono. Hera.

<span id="an_9:17">9:17</span> Ka hoki nga tangata kino ki te reinga,
ara nga iwi katoa e wareware ana ki te Atua.

<span id="an_9:18">9:18</span> E kore hoki e warewarea tonutia te
tangata rawakore: e kore e taka tonu ta te hunga iti i tumanako atu ai.

<span id="an_9:19">9:19</span> E ara, e Ihowa, kei riro i ta te tangata:
kia whakawakia nga tauiwi i tou aroaro.

<span id="an_9:20">9:20</span> E Ihowa, meinga ratou kia wehi: kia matau
nga tauiwi he tangata nei ano ratou. (Hera.

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> ¶ He aha koe ka tu mai ai i tawhiti, e
Ihowa? ka whakangarongaro ai i nga wa o te he?

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> E whakakake ana te tangata kino, e tukino
ana i te tangata iti: kia hopukina ratou ki nga whakaaro i whakaaro ai
ratou.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> E whakapehapeha ana hoki te tnngata kino
ki te hiahia o tona ngakau, a ko te hunga apo taonga, e whakakahore ana,
ae ra, e whakahawea ana ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> Ka mea te tangata kino, i te
whakapehapeha o tona mata, E kore e hiahiatia e ia. Kei roto i ona
whakaaro katoa e mea ana, Kahore he Atua.

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> Whanoke tonu ona ara i nga wa katoa; kei
runga noa ake au whakaritenga te kitea e ia, he mea whakatupereru e ia
ona hoariri katoa.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> E mea ana i roto i tona ngakau, e kore
ahau e whakakorikoria: kahore hoki he he moku a nga whakatupuranga
katoa.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> Ki tonu tona mangai i te kanga, i te
hianga, i te tukino: kei raro i tona arero te whanoke me te teka.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> E noho ana ia, e whanga ana i nga pa
koraha: e kohurutia ana e ia te hunga harakore i nga wahi ngaro; e
matatau ana ona kanohi ki te hunga rawakore.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> E whanga puku ana ia me he raiona i tona
kuhunga: e whanga ana kia hopukia te tangata iti: e hopukia ana e ia te
tangata iti, ua kumea ki tana. kupenga.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> Kupapa ana ia, piko ana, hinga ana te
hunga rawakore i ana mea kaha.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> E mea ana i roto i tona ngakau, Ka
wareware te Atua: e huna ana ia i tona mata, e kore ia e kite ake tonu
atu.

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> ¶ Whakatika, e Ihowa, e te Atua,
takiritia tou ringa: kaua e wareware ki te hunga iti.

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> He aha te tangata kino ka whakahawea ai
ki te Atua? kua mea ia i roto i tona ngakau, E kore tenei e whakatakina
e koe.

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> Kua kite koe; e tirohia nei hoki e koe
te whanoke me te whakatoi, a ka utua e tou ringa: e tuku ana te rawakore
i a ia ano ki a koe; ko koe hei tuara mo te pani.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> Whatiia e koe te ringa o te tangata
kino; tena ko te tangata nanakia, whakatakina tona kino, kia kahore ra
ano e kitea e koe.

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> Ko Ihowa te Kingi ake ake: kua kahore
ke nga tauiwi i tona whenua.

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> E Ihowa, kua whakarongo koe ki te
hiahia o te hunga whakaiti: mau ano o ratou ngakau e whakapai, ka tahuri
ano tou taringa ki te whakarongo:

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> Ki te whakawa mo te pani, mo te tangata
e tukinotia ana, kei whakamataku a mua ake te tangata o te whenua.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri. Ko
Ihowa taku e whakawhirinaki ai: he aha koutou ka mea ai ki toku wairua,
rere a manu atu ki to koutou maunga?

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Nana, kua whakapikoa te kopere e te hunga
kino, e whakatikaia ana a ratou pere ki te aho, hei perenga pukutanga ma
ratou ki te hunga ngakau tika.

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> Ki te wawahia nga turanga ake, me pehea
te tangata tika?

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> ¶ Kei tona temepara tapu a Ihowa, kei te
rangi te torona o Ihowa: e titiro ana ona kanohi, e whakamatautau ana
ona kamo i nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> E whakamatautau ana a Ihowa i te tangata
tika: a e kinogia ana e tona wairua te tangata kino me te tangata e
aroha ana ki te tutu.

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> Ka uaina e ia ki runga ki te hunga kino
he mahanga, he ahi, he whanariki, he awha tuaikerekere: ko te wahi tena
mo to ratou kapu.

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> No te mea he tika a Ihowa, e aroha ana ki
te tika; ka kite te hunga tika i tona kanohi.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Heminiti. He
himene na Rawiri. Whakaorangia, e Ihowa; ka mutu hoki nga tangata tapu;
ka taweke atu te hunga pono i roto i nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> E korero teka ana ratou tetahi ki tetahi;
he ngutu patipati, he ngakau rua o ratou ina korero.

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> Ka hatepea e Ihowa nga ngutu patipati
katoa, me te arero e korero whakapehapeha ana;

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> E mea nei, Ma o tatou arero tatou ka kake
ai; no tatou ano o tatou ngutu, ko wai hei ariki mo tatou?

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> Mo te tukinotanga i te hunga iti, mo te
aue a te hunga rawakore, ka whakatika ahau aianei, e ai ta Ihowa, Ka
whakanohoia ia e ahau ki te wahi e ora ai ia i nga tangata e
whakatupereru ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> He kupu parakore nga kupu a Ihowa: he
hiriwa i whakakorea nei te para i roto i te oumu whenua, he mea tuku
whitu.

<span id="an_12:7">12:7</span> Ka tiakina ratou e koe, e Ihowa, ka
whakaorangia ratou i tenei whakatupuranga ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_12:8">12:8</span> E haereere noa ana nga tangata kino i
tetahi taha, i tetahi taha, i te mea e whakateiteitia ana te kino i roto
i nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. Kia pehea te roa o tou wareware ki ahau, e Ihowa? mo ake tonu
atu ranei? Kia pehea te roa o tau hunanga i tou mata ki ahau?

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> Kia pehea te roa o toku whakaaroaronga i
roto i toku wairua, o te pouri i roto i toku ngakau i tenei ra, i tenei
ra? Kia pehea te roa o te whakakake mai a toku hoariri ki ahau?

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> Titiro mai, whakahokia mai he kupu ki
ahau, e Ihowa, e toku Atua: whakamaramatia oku kanohi, kei moe ahau i te
moe o te mate.

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> Kei mea mai toku hoariri, Kua taea ia e
ahau: kei whakamanamana oku hoariri, ina whakakorikoria ahau.

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> Ko ahau ia e whakawhirinaki ana ki tau
mahi toku: ka whakamanamana toku ngakau ki tau whakaoranga.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> Ka waiata ahau ki a Ihowa, mona i atawhai
mai ki ahau.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri.
Kua ki te wairangi i tona ngakau, Kahore he Atua. Kua pirau ratou, he
whakahouhou a ratou mahi, kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai.

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> I titiro iho a Ihowa i te rangi ki nga
tama a te tangata, kia kite me kahore tetahi e mahara ana, e rapu ana i
te Atua.

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> Kua peka ke ratou katoa kua pirau tahi:
kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai, kohore kia kotahi.

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> ¶ E kore ranei e mohio nga kaimahi katoa
o te kino? e kai nei i toku iwi, me te mea e kai taro ana, a kahore e
karanga ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> Na, i reira ratou e tuiri noa ana: kei
roto hoki te Atua i te whakatupuranga o te hunga tika.

<span id="an_14:6">14:6</span> Meinga ana e koutou te whakaaro o te
hunga iti hei whakama, no te mea ko Ihowa tona piringa.

<span id="an_14:7">14:7</span> Aue, me i puta mai te whakaoranga o
Iharaira i Hiona! Kia whakahokia e Ihowa tana iwi i te whakarau, ka
whakamanamana a Hakopa, ka hari a Iharaira.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, ko wai e
noho ki tou tapenakara? Ko wai e noho ki tou maunga tapu?

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> Ko ia he tapatahi nei te haere, he tika
te mahi, he korero pono ano i roto i tona ngakau.

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> Kahore nei e ngautuara tona arero, kahore
e kino te mahi ki tona hoa, kahore ana ingoa kino mo tona hoa.

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> E whakahengia ana te tangata kino e ona
kanohi, e whakahonoretia ana ia e ia te hunga e wehi ana ki a Ihowa.
Ahakoa mate i tana oati, kahore e whakapaheketia e ia.

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> Kahore e tuku i tana moni hei moni
whakatupu; kahore hoki e tango i te moni hei utu mate mo te tangata
harakore. Ki te penei te mahi a tetahi, e kore ia e whakakorikoria ake
ake.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> ¶ He Mikitama na Rawiri. Tiakina ahau, e
te Atua: e whakawhirinaki nei hoki ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Kua mea ahau ki a Ihowa, Ko koe toku
Ariki, kahore oku pai i tua atu i a koe.

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Ko te hunga tapu i runga i te whenua, te
hunga pai rawa, kua ahau katoa toku ahuareka ki a ratou.

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> Ka whakanuia nga mamae o te hunga e
whakawhiti ana i a Ihowa mo tetahi atua ke: e kore e ringihia e ahau a
ratou ringihanga toto, e kore ano o ratou ingoa e whakahuatia e oku
ngutu.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> Ko Ihowa te wahi i wehea mai moku, taku
kapu hoki: ko koe te kaiwhakapumau i te wahanga maku.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> Kua takoto oku aho ki nga wahi ahuareka,
ina, he wahi pai toku.

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> Ka whakapaingia e ahau a Ihowa, i
whakamahara nei i ahau: ka whakaako ano hoki oku whatumanawa i ahau i te
po.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> ¶ Kua waiho tonu e ahau a Ihowa ki toku
aroaro: kei toku ringa matau nei ia, e kore ahau e whakakorikoria.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> Koia i koa ai toku ngakau, i
whakamanamana ai toku kororia, i takoto tumanako ai ano oku kikokiko.

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> No te mea e kore e waiho e koe toku
wairua i te reinga, e kore e tukua tau Mea Tapu kia kite i te pirau.

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> Ka whakakitea mai e koe ki ahau te
huarahi o te ora; kei tou aroaro te hari nui, kei tou matau nga ahuareka
e kore e mutu.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> ¶ He inoi na Rawiri. Whakarongo ki te
tika, e Ihowa, tahuri mai ki taku karanga, kia titaha mai tou taringa ki
taku inoi, ara ki ta te ngutu tinihangakore.

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> Kia puta mai te whakaritenga o taku
whakawa i tou aroaro; tirohia mai e ou kanohi te mea rite.

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> Kua whakamatauria e koe toku ngakau; kua
tirotirohia iho ahau e koe i te po; kua whakamatau koe i ahau, a kahore
he mea i kitea e koe; e mea ana ahau kia kaua e hara toku mangai.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> Ko nga mahi ia a te tangata, ko nga kupu
a tou mangai taku mea hei pa mai i ahau i nga ara o te kaiwhakangaro.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> I whakaukia oku hikoinga ki au ara, kihai
i paheke oku waewae.

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> Kua karanga nei ahau ki a koe, no te mea
ka whakahoki kupu mai koe, e te Atua, ki ahau: whakatitahatia mai tou
taringa ki ahau, whakarongo ki taku kupu.

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> Whakaaturia tou aroha whakamiharo, ko koe
hoki, ko tou matau, te kaiwhakaora mo te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a
koe, i te hunga e whakatika mai ana.

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> ¶ Tiakina ahau, ano ko te whatu o te
kanohi, huna ahau ki raro i te taumarumarutanga o ou pakau,

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> I te hunga kino e tukino nei i ahau, i
oku hoariri whakamate e karapoti nei i ahau.

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> E kopakia ana ratou e o ratou ngako: e
korero whakapehapeha ana o ratou mangai.

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> Tenei o matou hikoinga te karapotia nei
e ratou: matatau tonu iho o ratou kanohi ki te tuku iho i a matou ki te
whenua.

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> Kei te raiona e hiahia ana ki te hopu
kai te rite, kei te kuao raiona e piri ana i nga wahi ngaro.

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> E ara, e Ihowa, haukotia tona aroaro,
turakina ia ki raro; whakaorangia toku wairua ki tau hoari i te tangata
kino;

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> I nga tangata, ma tou ringa, e Ihowa, i
nga tangata o te ao: kei tenei ora nei to ratou wahi, a e whakakiia ana
o ratou kopu e koe ki tau taonga. E kiki ana ratou i te tamariki,
whakarerea iho nga toenga o a ratou taonga ki a ratou kohungahunga.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> Ko ahau, e kite ahau i tou mata i runga
i te tika, a ka tatu toku ngakau, ina oho ake ahau, kia kite i tou ahua.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
te pononga a Ihowa, na Rawiri. Nana i whakahua nga kupu o tenei waiata
ki a Ihowa i te ra i whakaorangia ai ia i te ringa o ona hoariri katoa,
i te ringa ano o Haora. I mea ia, Ka aroha ahau ki a koe, e Ihow a, e
toku kaha.

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> Ko Ihowa toku kamaka, toku pa, toku
kaiwhakaora; toku Atua, toku tino kamaka, e whakawhirinaki ai ahau; toku
whakangungu rakau, te haona o toku whakaoranga, toku pourewa tiketike.

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Ka karanga ahau ki a Ihowa, e tika nei
kia whakamoemititia: a ka ora i oku hoariri.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a te
mate, a whakawehia ana ahau e nga waipuke o te kino.

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a te
reinga, i haukotia e nga mahanga a te mate.

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> I karanga ahau ki a Ihowa i toku
paweratanga, i hamama ki toku Atua: i whakarongo ia ki toku reo i roto i
tona temepara, i tae ano taku hamama ki tona aroaro, ki ona taringa.

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> Na ka ngaueue te whenua, ka ru, wiri ana
nga putake o nga maunga, ngaueue ana i tona riri.

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> I kake he paowa i ona pongaponga, a kai
ana te kapura a tona mangai, ngiha ana nga waro.

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> I whakapingoretia e ia nga rangi, a heke
iho ana, a i raro te pouri matotoru i ona waewae.

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> I eke ia ki runga ki te kerupa, a rere
ana: ae, i rere omaki ia i runga i nga parirau o te hau.

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> I meinga e ia te pouri hei wahi ngaro
mona, hei teneti i tetahi taha ona, i tetahi taha; ko te pouritanga o
nga wai, ko nga kapua matotoru o te rangi.

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> I rere atu ona kapua metotoru i te
wherikotanga o tona aroaro: te whatu, me nga waro kapura.

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> I papa ano te whatitiri a Ihowa i nga
rangi, a puaki ana te reo o te Runga Rawa; he whatu, he waro kapura.

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> I kokiritia e ia ana pere, a marara ana
ratou: ae, i koperea hoki e ia te tini uira, a whati ana ratou.

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> Katahi ka kitea nga takere o nga wai, a
ka takoto kau nga putake o te ao i tau whakatupehupehutanga, e Ihowa, i
te whengunga o te manawa o ou pongaponga.

<span id="an_18:16">18:16</span> I tono karere mai ia i runga, ka mau ki
ahau; toia ake ahau e ia i roto i nga wai maha.

<span id="an_18:17">18:17</span> Nana ahau i ora ai i toku hoariri kaha,
i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau; he kaha rawa hoki ratou i ahau.

<span id="an_18:18">18:18</span> I huakina tatatia ahau e ratou i te ra
o toku matenga; ko Ihowa ia toku whakawhirinakitanga.

<span id="an_18:19">18:19</span> I whakaputaina ahau e ia ki te wahi
nui, i whakaorangia ahau e ia; he ahuareka nona ki ahau.

<span id="an_18:20">18:20</span> ¶ Rite tonu ki taku mahi tika ta Ihowa
utu ki ahau: rite tonu ki te ma o oku ringa tana i whakahoki ai ki ahau.

<span id="an_18:21">18:21</span> Moku i pupuri i nga ara o Ihowa, a
kihai i he, i whakarere i toku Atua.

<span id="an_18:22">18:22</span> Kei mua tonu hoki i ahau ana
whakaritenga katoa, kihai ano i whakamataratia atu i ahau ana tikanga.

<span id="an_18:23">18:23</span> Tapatahi tonu hoki toku whakaaro ki
tona aroaro, a i tiaki ahau i ahau kei kino.

<span id="an_18:24">18:24</span> Na ka homai e Ihowa he utu ki ahau,
rite tonu ki toku tika, ki te ma o oku ringa i tona aroaro.

<span id="an_18:25">18:25</span> He tangata atawhai, ka atawhai hoki
koe; he tangata tika, ka tika hoki koe.

<span id="an_18:26">18:26</span> He tangata ma, ka ma hoki koe; he
tangata whakakeke, ka whakakeke hoki koe.

<span id="an_18:27">18:27</span> E whakaorangia hoki e koe te iwi ngakau
mamae; ka whakahokia ano e koe ki raro nga kanohi whakakake.

<span id="an_18:28">18:28</span> Mau hoki e whakau taku rama: ma Ihowa,
ma toku Atua, e whakamarama toku pouri.

<span id="an_18:29">18:29</span> ¶ Nau hoki ahau i rere ai na waenganui
atu i te ropu: na toku Atua hoki i pekea ai e ahau te taiepa.

<span id="an_18:30">18:30</span> Tena ko te Atua, tika tonu tona ara:
kua oti tana kupu te whakamatau; he whakangungu rakau ia ki te hunga
katoa e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_18:31">18:31</span> Ko wai oti te Atua, ki te kahore a
Ihowa? Ko wai hoki he kamaka, ki te kahore to tatou Atua?

<span id="an_18:32">18:32</span> Ko te Atua, nana ahau i whitiki ki te
kaha, i mea kia tino tika toku ara.

<span id="an_18:33">18:33</span> Ko ia hei mea i oku waewae kia rite ki
o te hata: mana hoki ahau e whakatu ki runga ki oku wahi tiketike.

<span id="an_18:34">18:34</span> Ko ia hei whakaako i oku ringa ki te
whawhai, a whati ana te kopere parahi i oku ringa.

<span id="an_18:35">18:35</span> Kua homai ano e koe ki ahau te
whakangungu rakau o tau whakaoranga: puritia ana ahau e tou ringa matau
whakanuia ana e tou whakaaro mahakai.

<span id="an_18:36">18:36</span> I whakanuia e koe oku takahanga i raro
i ahau; te paheke oku waewae.

<span id="an_18:37">18:37</span> Ka arumia e ahau oku hoariri, mau iho i
ahau; e kore ahau e tahuri mai, a ngaro noa ratou.

<span id="an_18:38">18:38</span> Maru ana ratou i ahau, te kaha te
whakatika: hinga ana ki raro i oku waewae.

<span id="an_18:39">18:39</span> Nau hoki ahau i whitiki ki te kaha mo
te whawhai: piko ana i a koe ki raro i ahau te hunga e whakatika mai ana
ki ahau.

<span id="an_18:40">18:40</span> Kua meinga e koe kia tahuri mai nga
tuara o oku hoariri ki ahau, kia hautopea ai e ahau te hunga e kino ana
ki ahau.

<span id="an_18:41">18:41</span> I karanga ratou, heoi kahore he
kaiwhakaora: ki a Ihowa, otira kihai i whakahoki kupu ki a ratou.

<span id="an_18:42">18:42</span> Na ka tukia ratou e ahau a rite noa
ratou ki te puehu e puhia ana e te hau: akiritia atu ana ratou ki waho,
ano he paru no te huarahi.

<span id="an_18:43">18:43</span> Kua whakaorangia ahau e koe i nga
ngangautanga a te iwi; kua meinga e koe hei rangatira mo nga tauiwi: hei
apa moku te iwi kahore i matauria e ahau.

<span id="an_18:44">18:44</span> Kia rongo kau te taringa ki ahau, ka
kakama tonu mai ratou ki ahau; ko nga tangata iwi ke ngohe kau ki ahau.

<span id="an_18:45">18:45</span> Ka memeha haere nga tangata iwi ke: ka
puta wehi mai hoki i roto i o ratou kuhunga.

<span id="an_18:46">18:46</span> E ora ana a Ihowa; kia whakapaingia
hoki toku kamaka, kia whakanuia te Atua o toku whakaoranga:

<span id="an_18:47">18:47</span> Ko te Atua, mana nei e rapu he utu
moku, mana e pehi nga iwi ki raro i ahau.

<span id="an_18:48">18:48</span> Mana ahau e mawhiti ai i oku hoariri,
ae ra, mau ahau e mea kia teitei ake i te hunga e whakatika mai ana ki
ahau; ka whakaorangia ahau e koe i te tangata tutu.

<span id="an_18:49">18:49</span> Mo konei ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe,
e Ihowa, i waenganui i nga tauiwi: ka himene ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_18:50">18:50</span> He nui nei tana whakaora i tana kingi;
e whakaputa aroha ana ki tana tangata i whakawahi ai, ki a Rawiri ratou
ko ona uri ake ake.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. E korerotia ana e nga rangi te kororia o te Atua; a e
whakaaturia ana e te kikorangi te mahi a ona ringa.

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> E puaki ana te reo o tena rangi, o tena
rangi, e whakaatu mohiotanga ana hoki tena po, tena po.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> Kahore he hamumu, kahore he kupu, kahore
e rangona to ratou reo.

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> Kua puta ta ratou aho ki te whenua katoa,
a ratou kupu, a te pito ra ano o te ao. Whakaturia ana e ia ki reira te
tapenakara mo te ra;

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> A e puta ana ia me he tane marena hou i
tona whare moenga, whakai ana ia, pera ana me te tangata kaha e mea ana
ki te oma whakataetae.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> Ko tona putanga kei tetahi pito o te
rangi, a whawhe noa ke tetahi pito: kahore hoki tetahi mea e ngaro i
tona mahana.

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> ¶ Tapatahi tonu te ture a Ihowa, he mea
whakatahuri i te wairua: pono tonu nga whakaatu a Ihowa, e
whakawhaiwhakaaro ana i te kuare.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> He tika nga ako a Ihowa, e whakahari ana
i te ngakau, he ma te whakahau a Ihowa, e whakamarama ana i nga kanohi.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> He ma te wehi ki a Ihowa, pumau tonu ake
ake, he pono nga whakaritenga a Ihowa, tika kau ano.

<span id="an_19:10">19:10</span> Engari ena e hiahiatia ana i te koura,
ae, i te tino koura ahakoa maha: reka atu i te honi, i te
maturuturutanga iho o nga honikoma.

<span id="an_19:11">19:11</span> Na ena ano tau pononga i whakatupato;
he nui te utu ki te puritia.

<span id="an_19:12">19:12</span> Ko wai e matau ana ki ona he?
Whakamakia oku hara puku.

<span id="an_19:13">19:13</span> Puritia ano tau pononga kei riro i nga
hara whakakake hei rangatira moku: ko reira ahau tu tika ai, a ka watea
i te he nui.

<span id="an_19:14">19:14</span> Kia manakohia nga kupu a toku mangai:
me nga whakaaro o toku ngakau i tou aroaro, e Ihowa, e toku kamaka, e
toku kaihoko.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. Ma Ihowa e whakahoki he kupu ki a koe i te ra o te he; ma te
ingoa o te Atua o Hakopa koe e tiaki;

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> Mana e tono mai he awhina mou i te wahi
tapu, e whakau hoki koe i Hiona;

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Mana e mahara ki au whakahere katoa, e
manako ki au tahunga tinana. (Hera.

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> Mana e homai ki a koe ta tou ngakau e mea
ai, e whakamana katoa hoki tau e wawata ai.

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> Ka hari matou ki tau whakaoranga, ka
whakatu hoki i o matou kara i runga i te ingoa o to matou Atua: ma Ihowa
e whakarite au inoi katoa.

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> ¶ Katahi ahau ka matau e whakaora ana a
Ihowa i tana tangata i whakawahi ai, ka whakahoki kupu ia ki a ia i tona
rangi tapu, me te kaha ano tona ringa matau ki te whakaora.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> Ko ta etahi he hariata, ko ta etahi he
hoiho: ko tatou ia ka whakahua i te ingoa o Ihowa, o to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> Kua piko ratou, kua hinga: ko tatou ia
kua ara, kua tu ki runga.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> Whakaorangia, e Ihowa: kia whakahoki kupu
mai te Kingi ina karanga matou.

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. Ka hari te kingi ki tou kaha, e Ihowa; ano te nui o tona
whakamanamana ki tau whakaoranga!

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> Kua homai e koe ki a ia ta tona ngakau i
hiahia ai; kihai ano i kaiponuhia e koe ta ona ngutu i inoi ai. (Hera.

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> Kei mua nei hoki koe i a ia e homai ana i
nga manaakitanga o te pai; karaunatia ana e koe tona matenga ki te tino
koura.

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> He ora tana i inoi ai i a koe, a kua
homai e koe ki a ia, he roa noa atu nga ra ake ake.

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> He nui tona kororia i tau whakaoranga:
uhia ana ia e koe ki te honore, ki te kororia.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> Nau hoki ia i mea kia manaakitia rawatia
ake ake: whakaharitia ana ia e koe ki te koa o tou mata.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> ¶ E whakawhirinaki ana hoki te kingi ki a
Ihowa; e kore ano ia e whakangaueuetia, he atawhai hoki no te Runga
Rawa.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> Ka mau i tou ringa ou hoariri katoa: ka
mau i tou ringa matau te hunga e kino ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> Ka meinga ratou e koe, kia rite ki te
oumu kapura i te wa e riri ai koe: e horomia ratou e Ihowa ina weriweri
ia, a ma te kapura ratou e kai.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> Ka whakamotitia e koe o ratou hua i
runga i te whenua, o ratou uri i waenganui o nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> He kino hoki ta ratou i whakatakoto ai
mou, he mahi nanakia ta ratou i whakaaro ai, kihai nei i taea e ratou.

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> Mo reira ka meinga e koe kia tahuri o
ratou tuara, ina whakatihaia e koe au pere i runga i au aho ki o ratou
mata.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Kia whakanuia koe, e Ihowa, i runga i
tou kaha: ka waiata matou, ka himene ki tou nui.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Airete
Hahara. He himene na Rawiri. E toku Atua, e toku Atua, he aha koe i
whakarere ai i ahau? he aha koe i matara atu ai ki te whakaora i ahau i
nga kupu hoki o taku hamama?

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> E toku Atua, e karanga nei ahau i te
awatea, heoi kahore koe e rongo, i te po ano kahore ahau e wahangu.

<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> Otiia he tapu koe, kei nga whakamoemiti a
Iharaira tou nohoanga.

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> I whakawhirinaki o matou matua ki a koe,
i whakawhirinaki, a whakaorangia ana e koe.

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> I karanga ratou ki a koe, a kua ora; i
whakawhirinaki ki a koe, a kihai i whakama.

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> Ko ahau ia he toke, ehara i te tangata: e
tawaia ana e te tangata, e whakahaweatia ana e te iwi.

<span id="an_22:7">22:7</span> Kataina iho ahau e te hunga katoa e kite
ana i ahau, ko ana o ratou ngutu, ruru ana o ratou matenga, e ki mai
ana,

<span id="an_22:8">22:8</span> Tukua atu koe ki a Ihowa, mana ia e
whakaora: mana ia e whakaora, e pai ana hoki ia ki a ia.

<span id="an_22:9">22:9</span> Nau ia ahau i whakawhanau mai i roto i te
kopu, i mea hoki kia tumanako, i ahau i nga u o toku whaea.

<span id="an_22:10">22:10</span> He mea whakarere atu ahau ki runga ki a
koe no te kopu mai; ko koe toku Atua no te kopu mai ano o toku whaea.

<span id="an_22:11">22:11</span> ¶ Kei mamao atu i ahau, e tata ana hoki
te he, kahore hoki he kaiawhina.

<span id="an_22:12">22:12</span> He tini nga puru e karapoti nei i ahau:
e whakapaea ana ahau e nga mea kaha o Pahana.

<span id="an_22:13">22:13</span> E hamama ana o ratou mangai ki ahau,
ano he raiona e haehae ana, e hamama ana.

<span id="an_22:14">22:14</span> Kua ringihia ahau, ano he wai, kua
takoki katoa oku iwi; me te ware pi toku ngakau, e rewa ana i waenganui
i oku whekau.

<span id="an_22:15">22:15</span> Kua maroke toku kaha, ano he maramara
rihi, piri tonu toku arero ki oku kauae; kua whakatakotoria ano ahau e
koe ki te puehu o te mate.

<span id="an_22:16">22:16</span> Kua karapotia nei hoki ahau e te
kirehe, kua muia e te whakaminenga o nga tangata hara: kua pokaia e
ratou oku ringa me oku waewae.

<span id="an_22:17">22:17</span> E taea e ahau te tatau oku iwi katoa: e
titiro mai ana ratou, e matakitaki ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_22:18">22:18</span> E wehewehea ana oku kakahu mo ratou, e
maka rota ana mo toku weruweru.

<span id="an_22:19">22:19</span> Kaua ra ia koe e matara atu, e Ihowa; e
toku kaha, hohoro mai hei awhina moku.

<span id="an_22:20">22:20</span> Whakaorangia toku wairua i te hoari,
taku hoki e matenui nei i te kuri.

<span id="an_22:21">22:21</span> Whakaorangia ahau i te mangai o te
raiona: ae, i nga haona o nga kau maka kua whakahokia mai e koe he kupu
ki ahau.

<span id="an_22:22">22:22</span> ¶ Ka korerotia e ahau tou ingoa ki oku
teina, ka whakamoemititia koe e ahau i waenganui i te whakaminenga.

<span id="an_22:23">22:23</span> E te hunga e wehi ana ki a Ihowa,
whakamoemiti ki a ia; whakakororiatia ia, e te uri katoa o Hakopa, kia
wehi hoki ki a ia, e te uri katoa o Iharaira.

<span id="an_22:24">22:24</span> Kihai hoki ia i whakahawea, kihai i
whakarihariha ki te aue o te ngakau mamae; kihai ano i huna i tona mata
ki a ia, engari i tana karangatanga ki a ia i whakarongo ia.

<span id="an_22:25">22:25</span> Ko koe taku e whakamoemiti ai i
waenganui o te whakaminenga nui, ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi
ki te aroaro o te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_22:26">22:26</span> Ka kai te hunga mahaki, a ka makona: ka
whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa te hunga e rapu ana ki a ia; kia ora tonu o
koutou ngakau, ake, ake.

<span id="an_22:27">22:27</span> E mahara nga pito katoa o te whenua, a
ka tahuri ki a Ihowa: ka koropiko ano nga hapu katoa o nga iwi ki tou
aroaro.

<span id="an_22:28">22:28</span> No Ihowa hokite rangatiratanga, ko ia
ano te kawana i waenganui o nga iwi.

<span id="an_22:29">22:29</span> Ka kai, a ka koropiko nga tangata
tetere katoa o te whenua: ka tuohu ki tona aroaro te hunga katoa e heke
ana ki te puehu; tae no ki te tangata kahore e ora i a ia tona wairua.

<span id="an_22:30">22:30</span> Tera e mahi tetahi uri ki a ia; ka
waiho ki te Ariki hei whakatupuranga.

<span id="an_22:31">22:31</span> E haere mai ratou, e kauwhau i tona
tika ki te iwi e whanau a mua, he meatanga tenei nana.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Ko Ihowa toku
hepara; e kore ahau e hapa.

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> Ko ia hei mea kia takoto ahau ki nga wahi
tarutaru hou: e arahi ana ia i ahau ki te taha o nga wai ata rere.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Ko ia hei whakahoki ake i toku wairua: e
arahi ana ia i ahau i nga ara o te tika, he whakaaro ki tona ingoa.

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> Ae, ahakoa haere ahau i te awaawa o te
atarangi o te mate, kahore he kino e wehi ai ahau: no te mea kei toku
taha koe; ko tau rakau, ko tau tokotoko, ko ena hei oranga ngakau moku.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> E taka ana e koe he tepu ki toku aroaro i
te tirohanga a oku hoariri, e whakawahia ana e koe toku matenga ki te
hinu, purena tonu taku kapu.

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> He pono e aru i ahau te pai me te atawhai
i nga ra katoa e ora ai ahau, a ka noho ahau ki te whare o Ihowa ake
tonu atu.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. No Ihowa te
whenua, me ona tini mea, te ao, me nga tangata e noho ana i runga.

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> He mea whakatu hoki nana ki runga ki nga
moana, he mea whakau ki runga ki nga roma.

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> ¶ Ko wai e eke ki te maunga o Ihowa? Ko
wai e tu ki tona wahi tapu?

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> Ko te tangata he ma nei nga ringa, he
harakore tona ngakau, kahore nei i ara tona wairua ki te horihori, a
kahore i oati teka.

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Ka riro i a ia te manaaki a Ihowa, me te
tika a te Atua o tona whakaoranga.

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Ko te whakatupuranga tenei o te hunga e
rapu ana ki a ia, e rapu nei i tou mate, e Hakopa. (Hera.

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> ¶ Kia ara o koutou matenga, e nga tatau,
ara ake, e nga tatau onamata; a ka tomo te Kingi o te kororia.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> Ko wai tenei Kingi kororia? Ko Ihowa, ko
te kaha, ko te marohirohi, ko Ihowa, ko te marohirohi ki te whawhai.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> Kia ara o koutou matenga, e nga tatau,
kia ara ake, e nga tatau onamata, a ka tomo te Kingi o te kororia.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> Ko wai tenei Kingi kororia? Ko Ihowa o
nga mano, ko ia te Kingi kororia. (Hera.

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka ara nei toku wairua ki a
koe, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> E toku Atua, ko koe toku
whakawhirinakitanga: kei whakama ahau, aua oku hoariri e tukua kia
whakaputa ki ahau.

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> Ae, aua tetahi o te hunga e tatari ana ki
a koe e tukua kia whakama: kia whakama te hunga e tinihanga noa ana.

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> Whakakitea ki ahau au ara, e Ihowa;
whakaakona ahau ki au huarahi.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> Arahina ahau i tou pono, whakaakona hoki
ahau: ko koe hoki te Atua o toku whakaoranga; pau noa te ra i ahau e
tatari nei ki a koe.

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> E Ihowa, kia mahara ki au mahi tohu, ki
au mahi aroha; nonamata riro hoki ena.

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> Kaua e maharatia nga hara o toku
tamarikitanga, me oku kino: mahara mai koe ki ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite ki
tau mahi tohu, kia whakaaro ki tou pai.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> ¶ He pai, he tika a Ihowa, a ka
whakaakona e ia te hunga hara ki te huarahi.

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> Ka arahina e ia te hunga mahaki i runga i
te whakawa: ka akona hoki e ia te hunga mahaki ki tana ara.

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> He mahi tohu, he pono nga ara katoa o
Ihowa ki te hunga e pupuri ana i tana kawenata, i ana whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> Kia mahara ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa, a
murua toku kino, he nui nei hoki.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> Ko wai te tangata e wehi ana ki a
Ihowa? Ka whakaako ia i a ia ki te ara e pai ai ia.

<span id="an_25:13">25:13</span> Ka noho tona wairua i runga i te pai, a
ka riro te whenua i tona uri.

<span id="an_25:14">25:14</span> Kei te hunga e wehi ana i a ia te mea
ngaro a Ihowa; a mana e whakakite ki a ratou tana kawenata.

<span id="an_25:15">25:15</span> ¶ E tau tonu ana oku kanohi ki a Ihowa;
mana hoki e unu ake oku waewae i te kupenga.

<span id="an_25:16">25:16</span> Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki ahau;
he mokemoke hoki ahau, e mamae ana te ngakau.

<span id="an_25:17">25:17</span> Kua whakanuia nga whakapawera o toku
ngakau: whakaputaina ahau i roto i nga mea e pehi nei i ahau.

<span id="an_25:18">25:18</span> Tirohia toku mate me toku mamae, a
murua katoatia oku hara.

<span id="an_25:19">25:19</span> Tirohia mai oku hoariri, he tokomaha
hoki ratou: a he nanakia te kino e kino nei ratou ki ahau.

<span id="an_25:20">25:20</span> Tiakina toku wairua, a whakaorangia
ahau: kei whakama ahau; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_25:21">25:21</span> Tukua ma te ngakau tapatahi, ma te tika
ahau e tiaki; e tumanako ana hoki ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_25:22">25:22</span> Hokona, e te Atua, a Iharaira i roto i
ona whakapawera katoa.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Whakawakia ahau, e Ihowa,
kua haere nei hoki ahau i te tapatahitanga o toku ngakau: kua
whakawhirinaki ano ki a Ihowa, na, e kore e paheke.

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> Tirohia iho ahau, e Ihowa, whakamatauria
ahau, kia kitea oku whatumanawa me toku ngakau.

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> Kei mua hoki tou atawhai i oku kanohi;
kua haere nei ahau i tou pono.

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> Kahore ahau i noho tahi ki nga tangata
horihori; e kore ano ahau e tomo tahi me nga tangata tinihanga.

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> Kino tonu ahau ki te whakaminenga o nga
kaimahi i te he, e kore ano ahau e noho tahi ki te hunga kino.

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> ¶ Ka horoia e ahau oku ringa ki te
harakore, ka taiawhio ai i tau aata, e Ihowa;

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> A ka rangona toku reo e whakamoemiti ana,
e whakapuaki ana i au mahi whakamiharo katoa.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> E Ihowa, kua aroha nei ahau ki tou whare
nohoanga, ki te wahi e nohoia ana e tou kororia.

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> Kei huia toku wairua ki roto ki te hunga
hara, me toku ora ki roto ki te hunga toto.

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> He mahi nanakia hoki ta o ratou ringa;
ki tonu o ratou matau i te utu whakapati.

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> Ko ahau ia, ka haere i runga i toku
tapatahi: hokona ahau, tohungia hoki ahau.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> E tu ana toku waewae i te wahi tika: ka
whakapaingia a Ihowa e ahau i roto i nga whakaminenga.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ko Ihowa toku marama, toku
whakaoranga; kia wehi ahau i a wai? Ko Ihowa te kaha o toku ora; ko wai
e mataku ai ahau?

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> I te whakatatanga mai o te hunga kino, o
oku hoariri, o oku hoa whainga, ki te kai i oku kikokiko, tutuki ana
ratou, hinga ana.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Ahakoa whakapae noa te ope i ahau e kore
toku ngakau e wehi: ahakoa ara noa te pakanga ki ahau, ka au tonu ia
ahau.

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> Kotahi taku mea i inoi ai i a Ihowa, ko
taku tena e rapu ai: kia noho i te whare o Ihowa i nga ra katoa e ora ai
ahau, kia kite ai i te ataahua o Ihowa, kia ui ai i roto i tona
temepara.

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Ka huna hoki ahau e ia ki tona teneti i
te ra o te he, ka huna ki te wahi ngaro i tona tapenakara, ka hapainga
ahau ki runga ki te kohatu.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> Na, aianei ka teitei toku mahunga ki
runga ake i oku hoariri, e karapoti nei i ahau; a ka patua e ahau i roto
i tona tapenakara he whakahere hari; ka waiata ahau, ae ka himene ki a
Ihowa.

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> ¶ Whakarongo mai ki toku reo, e Ihowa, ua
karanga ahau, tohungia ahau, whakahokia mai hoki he kupu ki ahau.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> I a koe i mea, Rapua e koutou toku mata;
ka mea toku ngakau ki a koe, ka rapu ahau i tou mata, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Kaua tou mata e huna ki ahau, kaua tau
pononga e peia atu ua riri koe: ko koe toku kaiawhina, kei mahue ahau i
a koe, kei whakarerea e koe e te Atua o toku whakaoranga.

<span id="an_27:10">27:10</span> Ki te whakarerea ahau e toku papa, e
toku whaea, ko Ihowa hei tukunga atu moku.

<span id="an_27:11">27:11</span> E Ihowa, whakaakona ahau ki tau ara;
arahina ahau i te ara tika, he hoariri hoki oku.

<span id="an_27:12">27:12</span> Kaua ahau e tukua ki te hiahia o oku
hoariri; kua whakatika mai hoki ki ahau he kaiwhakapae teka, me te hunga
manawa nanakia.

<span id="an_27:13">27:13</span> Kua ngohe ahau, me i kaua ahau i
whakapono, tera ahau e kite i te pai o te Atua i te whenua o te ora.

<span id="an_27:14">27:14</span> Taria a Ihowa: kia maia, a kia kaha tou
ngakau; ina, taria a Ihowa.

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka karanga ahau ki a koe, e
Ihowa, e toku kohatu, kaua e wahangu ki ahau; ki te wahangu hoki koe ki
ahau, ka rite ahau ki te hunga e heke atu ana ki te poka.

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Whakarongo ki toku reo inoi, ua karanga
ahau ki a koe, ina totoro oku ringa ki tou ahurewa tapu.

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> Kaua ahau e kumea tahitia me te hunga he;
me nga kaimahi i te kino, he marie a ratou kupu ki o ratou hoa, he kino
ia kei roto i o ratou ngakau.

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> Kia rite ki a ratou mahi tau e hoatu ai
ki a ratou, ki te kino ano o a ratou hanga: kia rite ki nga mahi a o
ratou ringa tau e hoatu ai ki a ratou, whakahokia ta ratou utu ki a
ratou.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> Na kahore nei ratou e whakaaro ki nga
mahi a Ihowa, ki nga meatanga a ona ringa, mo reira ka whakahoroa iho
ratou e ia, e kore ano e whakaturia ake.

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa mona i
whakarongo mai ki toku reo inoi.

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> Ko Ihowa toku kaha, toku whakangungu
rakau; i whakawhirinaki toku ngakau ki a ia, a awhinatia ana ahau; koia
i hari ai toku ngakau, i whakamoemiti ai hoki taku waiata ki a ia.

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> Ko Ihowa to ratou kaha, ko ia ano te kaha
whakaora o tana tangata i whakawahi ai.

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> Whakaorangia tau iwi, manaakitia tou
kainga tupu: whangainga ratou, whakaarahia ake ake.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Hoatu ki a Ihowa,
e nga tama a te hunga nunui, hoatu ki a Ihowa te kororia me te kaha.

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> Hoatu ki a Ihowa te kororia e rite ana mo
tona ingoa, koropiko ki a Ihowa i roto i te ataahua o te tapu.

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> Kei runga te reo o Ihowa i nga wai: e
papa ana te whatitiri a te Atua o te kororia: kei runga a Ihowa i nga
wai maha.

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> Kaha tonu te reo o Ihowa; kororia tonu te
reo o Ihowa.

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Mongamonga noa nga hita i te reo o Ihowa;
ina, mongamonga noa i a Ihowa nga hita o Repanona.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> Ko ia hei mea i a ratou kia mokowhiti,
ano he kuao: a Repanona raua ko Hiriona, ano he kuao kau maka.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> E wehewehe ana te reo o Ihowa i nga mura
ahi.

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> Wiri ana te koraha i te reo o Ihowa: wiri
ana i a Ihowa te koraha o Karehe.

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> Whanau ana nga hata i te reo o Ihowa,
tihorea ana nga ngahere kia tahanga: i tona temepara ko te kupu a te
katoa, Kororia.

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> I noho a Ihowa hei kingi i runga i te
Waipuke; ae, ka noho a Ihowa hei kingi, ake ake.

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> Ka homai e Ihowa he kaha ki tana hunga;
he rongo mau ta Ihowa manaaki mo tana hunga.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> ¶ He hemene, he waiata mo te tainga o te
kawa o te whare. Na Rawiri. Ka whakanui ahau i a koe, e Ihowa; nau hoki
ahau i hapai ake, a kihai i tukua oku hoariri kia hari ki ahau.

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, i karanga ahau ki a
koe, a kore ake toku mate i a koe.

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> E Ihowa, nau i whakaputa ake toku wairua
i te reinga; nau ahau i whakaora kei heke ki te poka.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> Himene ki a Ihowa, e tana hunga tapu,
whakawhetai hoki ki tona ingoa tapu.

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> He iti hoki te wahi e riri ai ia; he
oranga ki te manakohia e ia: e tau iho te tangi i te ahiahi, a i te ata
he hari.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> ¶ I mea ahau i toku wa i kake ai, E kore
ahau e whakangaueuetia a muri ake nei.

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> He manakohanga nau, e Ihowa, i u ai i a
koe te tu o toku maunga; i huna e koe tou mata a raru iho ahau.

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> E Ihowa, i karanga ahau ki a koe, i inoi
hoki ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> He aha te pai o oku toto ina heke ahau ki
te poka? Ma te puehu koia koe e whakamoemiti? mana oti e whakapuaki tou
pono?

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> Whakarongo, e Ihowa, tohungia hoki
ahau: e Ihowa, ko koe hei awhina moku.

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> Kua puta ke i a koe taku tangi hei
kanikani: kua wewete i toku kakahu taratara, a whitikiria ana ahau e koe
ki te koa;

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> Hei mea e himene ai toku kororia ki a
koe, kore ake e wahangu. E Ihowa, e toku Atua, ka whakawhetai ahau ki a
koe ake ake.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. E Ihowa, ko koe taku e whakawhirinaki nei; kei whakama ahau ake
ake: whakaorangia ahau, he tika nei hoki koe.

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Anga mai tou taringa ki ahau; hohoro te
whakaora i ahau: kia ai koe hei kohatu kaha moku, hei whare tiaki moku.

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> Ko koe hoki toku kohatu, toku pa: na kia
mahara ki tou ingoa, a arahina ahau, tohutohungia hoki ahau.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> Kapohia ahau i roto i te kupenga i huna e
ratou moku; ko koe hoki toku kaha.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> Tenei toku wairua te tukua atu nei e ahau
ki tou ringa; nau ahau i hoki e Ihowa, e te Atua o te pono.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> E kino ana ahau ki te hunga e whakaaro
ana ki nga mea tekateka noa; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> Ka whakamanamana ahau, ka hari ki tou
atawhai; mou i titiro ki taku tangi; i matau hoki ki toku wairua i nga
wa o te he;

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> Kahore ahau i kopia e koe ki roto ki te
ringa o te hoariri: kua whakaturia e koe oku waewae ki te wahi nui.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> ¶ Tohungia ahau, e Ihowa, kei te he hoki
ahau, pakoko kau toku mata i te pouri, toku wairua me toku kopu.

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Ka hemo nei hoki toku ora i te tangi,
me oku tau i te aue; poto iho toku kaha i toku he, kurupopo ana oku iwi.

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> He tawainga ahau na oku hoariri katoa;
ko te tino mahi ia tena a oku hoa noho tata, he mea wehi ahau na nga
tangata i mohio ki ahau: ko te hunga i kite i ahau i waho, rere ana i
ahau.

<span id="an_31:12">31:12</span> Kua warewaretia ahau me te tupapaku kua
ngaro atu i te ngakau; kua rite ki te oko pakaru.

<span id="an_31:13">31:13</span> I rongo hoki ahau i te ngautuara a te
tini; i karapotia ahau e te wehi: i a ratou e runanga ana ki te he moku,
i mea kia whakamatea ahau.

<span id="an_31:14">31:14</span> Ko ahau ia i whakawhirinaki ki a koe, e
Ihowa: i mea, Ko koe toku Atua.

<span id="an_31:15">31:15</span> Kei tou ringa oku taima, whakaorangia
ahau i nga ringa o oku hoariri, i te hunga e tukino ana i ahau.

<span id="an_31:16">31:16</span> Kia whiti tou mata ki tau pononga;
whakaorangia ahau, he mahi tohu hoki tau.

<span id="an_31:17">31:17</span> Kei whakama ahau, e Ihowa; kua karanga
hoki ahau ki a koe: kia whakama te hunga kino, kia takoto puku i te
reinga.

<span id="an_31:18">31:18</span> Whakamutua te korero a nga ngutu teka,
he kino nei a ratou korero mo te tangata tika, na to ratou whakapehapeha
hoki, na to ratou whakahihi.

<span id="an_31:19">31:19</span> ¶ Ano te nui o tau pai kua rongoatia
nei e koe mo te hunga e wehi ana ki a koe; i mahia nei e koe mo te hunga
e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe i te aroaro o nga tama a te tangata!

<span id="an_31:20">31:20</span> Ka huna ratou e koe ki te wahi ngaro i
tou aroaro i nga rauhanga a te tangata; ka huna ratou e koe ki roto ki
te teneti, kei taea e te ngangau a nga arero.

<span id="an_31:21">31:21</span> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, mona i mea
kia miharotia tana mahi tohu ki ahau i te pa kaha.

<span id="an_31:22">31:22</span> I ki hoki ahau i toku potatutatunga,
Kua motuhia mai ahau i mua i ou kanohi: ahakoa ra i rongo koe ki toku
reo inoi i taku karangatanga ki a koe.

<span id="an_31:23">31:23</span> Arohaina a Ihowa, e tana hunga tapu
katoa: e tiakina ana e Ihowa te hunga pono, a he nui tana utu ki te
kaimahi whakapehapeha.

<span id="an_31:24">31:24</span> Kia maia, kia kaha o koutou ngakau, e
te hunga katoa e tumanako ana ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri: he Makiri. Ka hari te
tangata kua oti tana he te muru, tona hara te hipoki.

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Ka hari te tangata kahore nei e whakairia
e Ihowa he hara ki a ia, a kahore he hianga i tona wairua.

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> I ahau kihai i kuihi, ngahengahe kau oku
iwi i taku auetanga i te ra roa.

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> No tou ringa i taimaha ki ahau i te ao, i
te po; kua whakaputaina ketia toku makukuranga, ano na te maroketanga o
te raumati. (Hera.

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> I whakina e ahau toku hara ki a koe,
kihai hoki i huna i toku kino: i mea ahau, Ka whakina aku mahi tutu ki a
Ihowa; a murua ana e koe te kino o toku hara. (Hera.

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> Mo konei ka inoi ki a koe nga tangata
tapu katoa i te wa e kitea ai koe: he pono ka ngawha nga wai nui, e kore
e tata ki a ia.

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> ¶ Ko koe toku piringa; mau ahau e
whakaora i te pouri, mau ahau e karapoti ki nga waiata whakaora. (Hera.

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Ka tohutohungia koe e ahau, ka whakaakona
koe ki te ara e haere ai koe; ma toku kanohi koe e arahi.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> Kei rite koutou ki te hoiho, ki te muera
ranei, kahore nei he matauranga; he mea kuku nei o raua kauae ki te
paraire, ki te moka hei pupuri mai; ki te kore hoki, e kore e tata ki a
koe.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> He tini nga mea whakapouri mo te
tangata hara: ko te tangata ia e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa, ka
karapotia e te atawhai.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> Kia koa ki a Ihowa, whakamanamana, e te
hunga tika: kia hari, hamama, e te hunga ngakau tika katoa.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> ¶ Kia hari ki a Ihowa, e te hunga tika:
he mea ataahua te whakamoemiti ma te hunga kore he.

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> Whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa i runga i te
hapa; himene ki a ia i runga i te hatere kotahi tekau nei nga aho.

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> Waiatatia ki a ia he waiata hou: kia tika
te whakatangi, kia nui te reo.

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> No te mea he tika te kupu a Ihowa, a kei
runga i te pono ana mahi katoa.

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> E paingia ana e ia te tika me te whakawa:
ki tonu te whenua i te atawhai a Ihowa.

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> Na te kupu a Ihowa nga rangi i hanga; ko
nga mano katoa hoki o reira na te ha o tona mangai.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> He mea huihui e ia nga wai o te moana,
ano he puranga; he mea whawhao e ia te rire ki nga pakoro.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> Kia wehi te whenua katoa ki a Ihowa; kia
ohooho nga tangata katoa o te ao ki a ia.

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> I ki hoki ia, a kua oti: i whakahau, a tu
tonu iho.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> E whakataka ana e Ihowa te whakaaro o
nga tauiwi: e whakakahoretia ana e ia nga meatanga a nga iwi.

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> Ko te whakaaro o Ihowa, tu tonu ake
ake; ko nga meatanga a tona ngakau kei tena whakatupuranga, kei tena
whakatupuranga.

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> ¶ Ka hari te iwi no ratou nei Atua a
Ihowa, te iwi kua whiriwhiria e ia hei taonga tupu mona.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> E titiro iho ana a Ihowa i te rangi: e
kite ana ia i nga tama katoa a te tangata.

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Kei tona wahi nohoanga ia e matakitaki
iho ana ki nga tangata katoa o te whenua.

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> Nana i hanga nga ngakau o ratou katoa,
e mohiotia ana e ia a ratou mahi katoa.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> E kore tetahi kingi e ora i te nui o te
ope, e kore e ora te marohirohi i te nui o te kaha.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> He mea teka te hoiho hei whakaora;
ehara ano tona kaha nui i te mea e mawhiti ai.

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> Nana, kei runga i te hunga e wehi ana i
a ia te kanohi o Ihowa, kei te hunga e tumanako ana ki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> Hei whakaora i o ratou wairua kei mate,
hei mea i a ratou kia ora i te wa o te hemokai.

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Kua tatari nei o tatou wairua ki a
Ihowa; ko ia to tatou kaiawhina, to tatou whakangungu rakau.

<span id="an_33:21">33:21</span> Hari tonu to tatou ngakau ki a ia; no
tatou hoki i whakawhirinaki ki tona ingoa tapu.

<span id="an_33:22">33:22</span> E Ihowa, hei runga i a matou tau mahi
tohu; kia rite hoki ki ta matou tumanako ki a koe.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri, i tona ahua i rere ke ra i
te aroaro o Apimereke; na pei ana ia, a haere ana. Ka whakapaingia e
ahau a Ihowa i nga wa katoa; he whakamoemiti tonu ta toku mangai ki a
ia.

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> Ka whakamanamana toku wairua ki a Ihowa:
ka rongo te hunga mahaki, a ka hari.

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Kia whakanui tahi tatou i a Ihowa, kia
whakateitei tahi hoki i tona ingoa.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> I rapu ahau i a Ihowa, a rongo mai ana ia
ki ahau, whakaorangia ana ahau e ia i oku wehi katoa.

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> I titiro ratou ki a ia, a kua marama: a
kahore rawa he whakama o o ratou mata.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> I karanga tenei tangata iti, a whakarongo
ana a Ihowa, whakaora ana i a ia i ona whakapawera katoa.

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> E noho ana te anahera a Ihowa i tetahi
taha, i tetahi taha, o te hunga e wehi ana i a ia, a e whakaora ana i a
ratou.

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Whakamatauria, kia kite ai koutou i te
pai o Ihowa: ka hari te tangata e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> Kia wehi ki a Ihowa, e tona hunga tapu: e
kore hoki e hapa nga tangata e wehi ana i a ia.

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> E hapa ana nga kuao raiona, e mate ana
i te kai: ko te hunga ia e rapu ana ki a Ihowa, e kore e hapa i tetahi
mea pai.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> ¶ Haere mai, e nga tamariki, whakarongo
ki ahau: maku koutou e ako kia wehi ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> Ko wai te tangata e hiahia ana ki te
ora, e whai ana kia maha nga ra, kia kite i te pai?

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> Tiakina tou arero kei kino, ou ngutu
kei korero hianga.

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> Mawehe atu i te kino, mahia te pai;
rapua te ata noho, whaia hoki.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> E tau ana nga kanohi o Ihowa ki te
hunga tika; me ona taringa ki ta ratou karanga.

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> E he ana te mata o Ihowa ki nga kaimahi
i te kino, hei hatepe i a ratou i te whenua kei maharatia.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> I karanga te hunga tika, a i whakarongo
a Ihowa, whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i o ratou whakapawera katoa.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> E tata ana a Ihowa ki te hunga ngakau
maru: ka whakaorangia ano e ia te hunga wairua iro.

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> He tini nga mate o te tangata tika:
otiia e whakaorangia ana ia e Ihowa i roto i era katoa.

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> E tiakina ana e ia ona wheua katoa: e
kore tetahi e whati.

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> Ka mate i te kino te tangata hara; a ka
he te hunga e kino ana ki te tangata tika.

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> E hokona ana e Ihowa te wairua o ana
pononga, e kore ano e he tetahi o te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. E ngana, e Ihowa, ki te
hunga e tohe ana ki ahau: whawhaitia te hunga e whawhai nei ki ahau.

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> Kia mau ki te whakangungu rakau, ki te
puapua; whakatika hei awhina moku

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> Unuhia te tao, araia te ara o te hunga e
whai nei i ahau: ki mai ki toku wairua, Ko ahau tou whakaoranga.

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> Kia whakama, kia numinumi te hunga e whai
ana kia whakamatea ahau: kia whakahokia ki muri, kia whakapoauautia te
hunga e whakatakoto ana i te kino moku.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> Kia rite ratou ki te papapa e puhia ana e
te hau; kia aia haeretia e te anahera a Ihowa.

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> Kia pouri to ratou ara, kia pahekeheke:
kia whaia ratou e te anahera a Ihowa.

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> Kahore hoki he rawa i huna ai e ratou te
poka o ta ratou kupenga moku; he mea keri takekore kia mate ai ahau.

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> Kia rokohanga poauautia ia e te
ngaromanga; kia mau ano ko ia i tana kupenga i huna ai: kia taka ia ki
taua tino ngaromanga.

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> A ka koa toku wairua ki a Ihowa, ka hari
ki tana whakaoranga.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> Ka ki katoa oku wheua, E Ihowa, ko wai
te rite mou, mo te kaiwhakaora o te iti i te tangata e kaha ake ana i a
ia, ae o te iti, o te rawakore i tona kaipahua?

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> ¶ Whakatika ana nga kaiwhakapae teka:
whakawakia ana ahau mo nga mea kihai nei ahau i matau atu.

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Utua ana e ratou taku pai ki te kino, a
whakatupu pani ana toku wairua.

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> Tena ko ahau, i a ratou e mate ana, he
kahu taratara toku, waikauwere ana toku wairua, kihai i kai: a hoki mai
ana taku inoi ki toku uma.

<span id="an_35:14">35:14</span> Ko toku ahua me te mea he hoa ia, he
teina noku: kupapa noa iho ahau, ano he tangata e tangi ana ki tona
whaea.

<span id="an_35:15">35:15</span> I toku paheketanga ia koa ana ratou,
huihui ana; huihui ana nga tangata kino noa iho hei hoariri moku, kihai
ano ahau i mohio; haehae ana ratou i ahau, kihai hoki i mutu.

<span id="an_35:16">35:16</span> Rite tonu ki nga kaiwhakakata o nga
hakari, tetea ana o ratou niho ki ahau.

<span id="an_35:17">35:17</span> ¶ E te Ariki, kia pehea te roa o tau
titiro kau mai? Whakaorangia toku wairua i a ratou whakangaromanga, taku
e aroha nei, i nga raiona.

<span id="an_35:18">35:18</span> Ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe i roto i
te whakaminenga nui, ka whakamoemiti ki a koe i roto i te iwi maha.

<span id="an_35:19">35:19</span> Kei hari pokanoa ki ahau oku hoariri;
kei whakakini te kanohi o te hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_35:20">35:20</span> Ehara hoki ta ratou i te korero mo te
rangimarie; heoi kei te whakatakoto kupu tinihanga ratou mo te hunga ata
noho o te whenua.

<span id="an_35:21">35:21</span> Ina, hamama ana o ratou mangai ki ahau,
e ki ana, Ha, ha, kua kite to matou kanohi.

<span id="an_35:22">35:22</span> Kua kite koe, e Ihowa: kaua ra e
wahangu; e te Ariki, kei matara i ahau.

<span id="an_35:23">35:23</span> Oho ake, e ara ki te whakarite i toku
whakawa, ki taku tautohe, e toku Atua, e toku Ariki.

<span id="an_35:24">35:24</span> Kia rite ki tou tika te whakarite moku,
e Ihowa, e toku Atua: kei koa ano ratou ki ahau.

<span id="an_35:25">35:25</span> Kei mea ratou i roto i o ratou ngakau,
Ha, ko ta matou tena i pai ai: kei mea ratou, Kua horomia ia e tatou.

<span id="an_35:26">35:26</span> Kia whakama, kia numinumi ngatahi, te
hunga e koa ana ina he ahau: kia whakakakahuria ki te whakama, ki te
numinumi, te hunga e whakakake ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_35:27">35:27</span> Kia hamama i te hari, kia koa te hunga
e pai ana ki taku mahi tika: ae, kia mea tonu, kia whakanuia a Ihowa e
whakapai nei ki te ora o tana pononga.

<span id="an_35:28">35:28</span> A ka korerotia e toku arero tau mahi
tika, me te whakamoemiti ki a koe i te ra roa.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na te pononga
a Ihowa, na Rawiri. E mea ana te mahi kino a te tangata hara i roto i
toku ngakau, Kahore he wehi ki te Atua i mua i ona kanohi.

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> E whakapai ana hoki ona kanohi ake ki a
ia ano, e kore e kitea tona hara, e kore e kinongia.

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> He kino nga kupu a tona mangai he
rauhanga hoki, kua mahue i a ia te mahara, te mahi i te pai.

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> He mahi nanakia tana e whakaaro ai i
runga i tona moenga; ehara i te pai te ara e turia ana e ia, kahore ona
whakarihariha ki te kino.

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> ¶ Kei nga rangi, e Ihowa, tau mahi tohu:
tutuki noa atu tou pono ki nga kapua.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> Rite tonu tou tika ki nga maunga o te
Atua; he rire nui au whakaritenga: ko koe, e Ihowa, te kaiwhakaora i te
tangata, i te kararehe.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Ano te pai o tou aroha, e te Atua: ka
okioki nga tama a te tangata i raro i te taumarumarutanga iho o ou
pakau.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Ka makona ratou i nga mea momona o tou
whare: ka whakainumia ano e koe ki te awa o au mea whakahari.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> Kei a koe hoki te puna o te ora; ma tou
marama ka kite ai matou i te marama.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> Kia roa tou aroha ki te hunga e matau
ana ki a koe, tou tika hoki ki te hunga ngakau tika.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> Kei puta mai ki ahau te waewae
whakapakari; kei aia atu ahau e te ringa o te hunga hara.

<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> Hinga iho i reira nga kaimahi i te
kino: kua turakina iho, te ahei te ara ake.

<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Kaua e mamae ki te hunga
kino, kaua e hae ki nga kaimahi i te he.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> No te mea ka hohoro ratou te kotia, te
peratia me te tarutaru, a ka memenga me he otaota hou.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> Whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, mahia te pai;
e noho ki te whenua, a e aru i muri i te pono.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> Whakaahuareka ki a Ihowa, a ka homai e ia
ki a koe ta tou ngakau i hiahia ai.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> Tukua tou ara ki a Ihowa; whakawhirinaki
hoki ki a ia, a mana e mahi.

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> Mana hoki e whakaputa tou tika, ano he
marama, ou ritenga me te mea ko te ra e tu ana.

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> ¶ Okioki ki a Ihowa, tatari marie ki a
ia: kei mamae ki te tangata e tere ana i tona ara, ki te tangata e taea
ana e ia nga whakaaro kino.

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> Kati te riri, whakarerea hoki te arita;
kei mamae koe, kei takina kia mahi i te kino.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> No te mea ka hatepea atu te hunga kino:
ko te hunga ia e tatari ana ki a Ihowa, ka riro i a ratou te whenua.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Kia potopoto ake nei hoki, a ka kore
noa iho te hunga kino: ae ra, ka ata tirohia e koe tona wahi, a kore kau
noa iho ia.

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> Na ka riro te whenua i te hunga mahaki;
a ka hari ratou i te roa o te ata noho.

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> E whakangarahu ana te tangata kino mo
te tangata tika: pakiri ana ona niho ki a ia.

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> Ka kata te Ariki ki a ia, no te mea ka
kite ia e tata ana tona ra.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> Kua unuhia te hoari e te hunga kino,
kua piko ta ratou kopere, hei turaki i te ware, i te rawakore, hei
kohuru i te hunga e tika ana, i te ara.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> Ka tapoko ta ratou hoari ki o ratou
ngakau: a ka whatiia a ratou kopere.

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> Engari te wahi iti a te tangata tika i
nga taonga o nga tangata kino tokomaha.

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> Ka whatiia hoki nga ringa o te hunga
kino: u tonu ia i a Ihowa te hunga tika.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> E matau ana a Ihowa ki nga ra o te
hunga tika: a ka pumau to ratou kainga ake ake.

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> E kore ratou e whakama i te wa o te he,
ka makona ano ratou i nga ra o te hemokai.

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> Ka ngaro ia te hunga kino, a ka rite
nga hoariri o Ihowa ki te momona o te tarutaru: ka mahea atu ratou; ka
mahea atu me he paowa.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> ¶ E tango ana te tangata kino i te
taonga tarewa, kahore hoki ana utu: ko te tangata tika ia he aroha tona,
he homai.

<span id="an_37:22">37:22</span> Ka riro hoki te whenua i ana e manaaki
ai; ka hatepea ano ana e kanga ai.

<span id="an_37:23">37:23</span> Ka u i a Ihowa nga hikoinga o te
tangata tika; e paingia ana hoki e ia tona ara.

<span id="an_37:24">37:24</span> Ahakoa hinga, e kore e tino takoto
rawa; ka u hoki ia i te ringa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_37:25">37:25</span> He tamariki ahau i mua, a kua koroheke
nei, heoi, kahore ahau i kite i te tangata tika e whakarerea ana, i ona
uri hoki e pinono taro ana.

<span id="an_37:26">37:26</span> I te ra roa he atawhai tonu tana, he
ohaoha: ka manaakitia hoki ona uri.

<span id="an_37:27">37:27</span> Whakarerea te kino, mahia te pai, ka
noho tonu ai.

<span id="an_37:28">37:28</span> E aroha ana hoki a Ihowa ki te ritenga
pai: e kore ano e whakarere i tana hunga tapu; e tiakina tonutia ana
ratou ake ake; ka hatepea atu ia nga uri o te hunga kino.

<span id="an_37:29">37:29</span> Ka riro te whenua i te hunga tika, ka
nohoia hoki a reira e ratou ake ake.

<span id="an_37:30">37:30</span> He kupu mohio ta te mangai o te tangata
tika; he ritenga pai ta tona arero e korero ai.

<span id="an_37:31">37:31</span> Kei tona ngakau te ture a tona Atua; e
kore e paheke tetahi o ona hikoinga.

<span id="an_37:32">37:32</span> E tau ana te titiro a te tangata kino
ki te tangata tika, a e whai ana kia whakamatea ia.

<span id="an_37:33">37:33</span> E kore a Ihowa e whakarere i a ia ki
tona ringa: e kore ano ia e whakatau he ki a ia ina whakawakia.

<span id="an_37:34">37:34</span> ¶ Taria a Ihowa, kia mau ki tana ara, a
ka whakanuia koe e ia, ka whakawhiwhia hoki ki te whenua: e hatepea atu
te hunga kino, ka kite koe.

<span id="an_37:35">37:35</span> I kite ahau i te tangata kino e kake
ana, e tautorotoro ana me te rakau matomato i tona oneone tupu.

<span id="an_37:36">37:36</span> Heoi, pahure noa ake tetahi, a kore kau
noa iho; ae, i rapua ia e ahau, a kihai i kitea.

<span id="an_37:37">37:37</span> Waitohutia te tangata tika, tirohia iho
te tangata kore he: no te mea he marie te tukunga iho ki taua tangata.

<span id="an_37:38">37:38</span> Tena ko te hunga kino, ka ngaro ngatahi
atu ratou: te tukunga iho ki te hunga kino, ka hatepea atu ratou.

<span id="an_37:39">37:39</span> Na Ihowa ia te whakaoranga o te hunga
tika: ko ia to ratou pa kaha i te wa o te he.

<span id="an_37:40">37:40</span> Ma Ihowa ratou e awhina, ko ia hoki hei
tauarai mo ratou: ko ia hei tauarai mo ratou i te hunga kino, ka
whakaorangia ratou e ia, mo ratou ka whakawhirinaki ki a ia.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, hei whakamahara. E
Ihowa, kaua e whakatupehupehu mai ki ahau ina riri koe, kaua ano ahau e
pakia ina arita koe.

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> Titi tonu hoki au pere ki ahau: kaha rawa
te pehi a tou ringa i ahau.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> Kahore he wahi ora o oku kikokiko, na tou
riri hoki: kahore ano e ata takoto oku wheua, noku i hara nei.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> Kua taupokina iho hoki toku matenga e oku
kino: ano he pikaunga taimaha e pehi rawa ana i ahau.

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> E piro ana oku whiunga, kua pirau i taku
mahi poauau.

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> E whakawiria ana ahau, piko rawa; e tangi
haere ana i te roa o te ra.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Kei te tahuna hoki toku hope, kapi tonu:
kahore hoki he wahi ora o oku kikokiko.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> Kua kore oku kaha, maru rawa ahau: hamama
ana taku aue i te mamae o toku ngakau.

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> E te Ariki, kei tou aroaro oku hiahia
katoa; kahore hoki e ngaro i a koe taku aue.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> Kihakiha kau toku ngakau, kua hemo toku
kaha: me te marama o oku kanohi, kua kore hoki ena oku.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> Matara noa atu i toku mate te turanga
mai o nga tangata i aroha mai ki ahau, o oku hoa hoki; i tawhiti ano oku
whanaunga e tu ke mai ana.

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> ¶ E whakatakoto mahanga ana moku te
hunga e whai ana i ahau kia whakamatea; he nanakia ano nga kupu a te
hunga e rapu ana i te he moku; he whakaaro tinihanga ano a ratou a pau
noa te ra.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> Ko ahau ia, i rite ki te turi, kihai i
rongo, ki te tangata wahangu, kahore nei e hamamu tona mangai.

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> Na rite tonu ahau ki te tangata kahore
nei e rongo, kahore nei he whakatupehupehu i tona mangai.

<span id="an_38:15">38:15</span> E tumanako nei hoki ahau ki a koe, e
Ihowa: ka whakahoki kupu mai ano koe, e te Ariki, e toku Atua.

<span id="an_38:16">38:16</span> I mea hoki ahau, Kei koa mai ratou ki
ahau: ka paheke toku waewae, ka whakahihi ratou ki ahau.

<span id="an_38:17">38:17</span> Ko ahau hoki, meake kopa, a kei inua
tonu i ahau toku pouri.

<span id="an_38:18">38:18</span> Ka whaki hoki ahau i toku kino, ka
pouri mo toku hara.

<span id="an_38:19">38:19</span> Ko oku hoariri ia hauhau tonu, kaha
tonu; kua tokomaha ano te hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_38:20">38:20</span> He hoariri ano ki ahau te hunga e utu
ana i te pai ki te kino: moku e whai ana i te pai.

<span id="an_38:21">38:21</span> Kaua ahau e whakarerea, e Ihowa, e toku
Atua; kei mamao atu koe i ahau.

<span id="an_38:22">38:22</span> Hohoro ki te awhina i ahau, e te Ariki,
e toku whakaoranga.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a
Ierutunu. He himene na Rawiri. I mea ahau, Ka ata whakaaro ahau ki oku
