ara, kei hara toku arero; ka tiakina toku mangai, paraire rawa, i te mea
kei toku aroaro te tangata kino.

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> I whakamoroki ahau, i wahangu, kihai i
puaki taku kupu, ahakoa pai; a ka oho toku mamae.

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> Werawera ana toku ngakau i roto i ahau; i
ahau e whakaaro ana ka ka te ahi, a ka korero toku arero.

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> E Ihowa, meinga ahau kia matau ki toku
mutunga, ki te maha hoki o oku ra, e hia ranei: kia matau ai ahau he mea
memeha noa ahau.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Nana, he whanuitanga ringa oku ra kua
homai nei e koe; he kahore noa iho ano oku tau i tou aroaro: ahakoa u
noa te tu o nga tangata katoa, he mea memeha kau. (Hera.

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> He pono kei roto i te atarangi te tangata
e kopikopiko noa ana; he pono e ohorere noa ana ratou: e ami ana ia i te
taonga, a kahore e matau ma wai ranei e kohi.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> ¶ Na he aha taku e tatari atu nei, e te
Ariki? Ko koe taku e tumanako ai.

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> Whakaorangia ahau i aku mahi tutu katoa:
kaua ahau e waiho hei tawainga ma te wairangi.

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> Wahangu ana ahau, kihai i kuihi toku
mangai: he meatanga hoki tenei nau.

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> Nekehia atu i ahau tau whiu: ka ngaro
ahau i te pakinga a tou ringa.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> Ka pakia e koe te tangata, ka
whakatupehupehutia mo te hara, ka meinga e koe tona ataahua kia memeha,
kia pera me te purehurehu: he pono he mea teka noa nga tangata katoa.
(Hera.

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Whakarongo ki taku inoi, e Ihowa, kia
titaha mai tou taringa ki taku karanga; kei wahangu koe ki oku roimata:
he heke hoki ahau nau, he manene, he pera me oku matua katoa.

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> Kia ata hanga ki ahau, kia ta ai toku
manawa, keiwha haere atu ahau i konei, a ka kahore noa iho.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. I tatari marie ahau ki a Ihowa: a anga ana ia ki ahau,
whakarongo ana ki taku karanga.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> Na kei te tango ake ia i ahau i te poka
whakamataku, i te paru taoruoru; kei te whakatu i oku waewae ki runga ki
te kohatu, kei te whakau i oku hikoinga.

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> A homai ana e ia he waiata hou ki toku
mangai, he whakamoemiti ki to tatou Atua: he tokomaha e kite, a ka wehi
ka whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> Ka hari te tangata kua waiho nei e ia a
Ihowa hei whakawhirinakitanga mona: a kahore e tahuri ki te hunga
whakakake, ki te hunga hoki e peka ana ki te teka.

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> E Ihowa, e toku Atua, he tini au mahi
whakamiharo i mahia e koe, me ou whakaaro ki a matou; e kore e taea te
korero whakatepe atu ki a koe: me i mea ahau kia whakakitea, kia
korerotia, e kore e taea te tatau.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> ¶ Kihai i matenuitia e koe te patunga
tapu, me te whakahere; pokaia ana e koe oku taringa: kihai koe i mea mai
ki te tahunga tinana, ki te whakahere hara.

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> Na ko taku meatanga atu, Na kua tae mai
ahau: kei roto i te pukapuka te tuhituhi moku.

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> Ko taku pai ko te mea i tau e pai ai, e
toku Atua: ae ra, kei toku ngakau tau ture.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> Kua kauwhautia e ahau te tika i roto i te
whakaminenga nui: nana, kihai i kopia oku ngutu, tena koe te matau ana,
e Ihowa.

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> Kihai i huna e ahau tou tika i roto i
toku ngakau; kua korerotia e ahau tou pono me tau whakaoranga: kihai i
hunga e ahau tou aroha me tou pono i te whakaminenga nui.

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> ¶ Kei kaiponuhia tou aroha ki ahau, e
Ihowa: ma tou atawhai me tou pono ahau e tiaki i nga wa katoa.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> Ta te mea kua karapotia ahau e nga kino
e kore e taea te tatau: mau pu ahau i oku kino, te ahei te titiro ake;
he tini ke i nga makawe o toku matenga: a hemo iho toku ngakau.

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> Kia pai, e Ihowa, ki te whakaora i
ahau; e Ihowa, hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Kia whakama, kia pororaru ngatahi te
hunga e rapu ana i toku wairua kia whakamatea: kia whakahokia ki muri,
kia whakama te hunga e hiahia ana kia he ahau.

<span id="an_40:15">40:15</span> Kia huna, hei utu mo to ratou whakama
te hunga e mea mai ana ki ahau, Ha, ha.

<span id="an_40:16">40:16</span> Kia hari, kia koa ki a koe te hunga
katoa e rapu ana i a koe; kia mea tonu te hunga e pai ana ki tau
whakaoranga, Kia whakanuia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_40:17">40:17</span> Ko ahau ia, he iti, he rawakore; heoi e
whakaaro ana te Ariki ki ahau: ko koe toku awhina, toku kaiwhakaora;
kaua ra e whakaroa, e toku Atua.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. Ka hari te tangata e whakaaro ana ki te rawakore; e whakaorangia
ia e Ihowa i te ra o te he.

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> Ma Ihowa ia e tiaki, e whakaora; ka
whakaharitia ia i runga i te whenua: e kore ano e tukua e koe ki nga
hiahia o ona hoariri.

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> Ma Ihowa ia e whakakaha, i a ia e
whakaruhi ana i runga i te moenga: mau ano e whakapai katoa tona moenga
i a ia e mate ana.

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> I mea ahau, E Ihowa, tohungia ahau;
rongoatia toku wairua; kua hara hoki ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> ¶ He kino te korero a oku hoariri moku, e
mea ana, A hea ranei ia mate ai, pirau ai tona ingoa?

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> A ki te haere mai ia kia kite i ahau, ka
korero horihori ia: e ami ana tona ngakau i te kino mana; i tona putanga
ki waho, korerotia ana e ia.

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> E komuhumuhu ana moku te hunga katoa e
kino ana ki ahau; e whakatakoto ana i te kino moku.

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> E ai ta ratou, E piri ana te mate kino ki
a ia; a ka takoto nei ia, heoi ano tona aranga ake.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> Ae, ko toku hoa ake ano, i whakawhirinaki
ai ahau, i kai nei i taku taro, kua hiki ake tona rekereke ki ahau.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, kia aroha ki ahau:
a whakaarahia ahau, kia utua ai ratou e ahau.

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Na konei ahau i matau ai e pai ana koe
ki ahau, no te mea kahore toku hoariri e whakamanamana ki ahau.

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> Ko ahau ia, ko koe e whakamau ake ana i
ahau i runga i toku ngakau tapatahi: e whakatu ake ana hoki i ahau ki
tou aroaro ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_41:13">41:13</span> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua o
Iharaira inamata riro ano, ake tonu atu ano hoki. Amine, ae Amine.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Makiri, ma
nga tama a Koraha. Rite tonu ki te hata e kihakiha nei ki nga manga wai
toku ngakau e kihakiha nei ki a koe, e te Atua.

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> E hiainu ana toku wairua ki te Atua, ki
te Atua ora: a hea ahau tae ai, puta ai ki te aroaro o te Atua?

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> Ko oku roimata taku kai i te ao, i te po,
i a ratou e mea tonu mai nei ki ahau, Kei hea tou Atua?

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> Ka mahara ahau ki enei mea; me te wai
toku ngakau e maringi ana i roto i ahau: i haere hoki ahau i roto i te
huihui, i haere tahi matou ki te whare o te Atua, he hari te reo, he
whakamoemiti, me te huihui e mea hakari ana.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? i
ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua; tera ano ahau e
whakawhetai ki a ia, mo te ora o tona mata.

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> ¶ E toku Atua, kua piko toku wairua i
roto i ahau: koia ahau ka mahara ai ki a koe i te whenua o Horano, o nga
Heremoni, i Maunga Mitara.

<span id="an_42:7">42:7</span> Rara ana tetahi rire ki tetahi rire i te
haruru o au awhiowhio wai: tika ana au ngaru katoa me au tuatea i runga
i ahau.

<span id="an_42:8">42:8</span> Ahakoa ra e whakahaua mai ano e Ihowa
tona atawhai i te awatea; a he waiata taku ki a ia i te po, he inoi ki
te Atua o toku ora.

<span id="an_42:9">42:9</span> Ka mea ahau ki te Atua, E toku kohatu, he
aha koe i wareware ai ki ahau? He aha ahau ka haere pouri ai i te tukino
a te hoariri?

<span id="an_42:10">42:10</span> Ano he hoari i roto i oku wheua te
tawai a oku hoariri: i a ratou e mea mai nei ki ahau i nga ra katoa, Kei
hea tou Atua?

<span id="an_42:11">42:11</span> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? He
aha koe i ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua: tera ano ahau e
whakawhetai ki a ia, ko te ora nei ia o toku mata, ko toku Atua.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> ¶ E te Atua, whakaritea taku whakawa,
whakatikaia aku korero ki te iwi atuakore: whakaorangia ahau i te
tangata tinihanga e mahi nei i te he.

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> Ko koe hoki te Atua o toku kaha: he aha
ahau ka panga nei e koe? He aha ahau ka haere pouri ai i te tukino a te
hoariri?

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> Tukua mai tou marama me tou pono hei
arahi i ahau: hei kawe i ahau ki tou maunga tapu, ki ou tapenakara.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> A ka haere ahau ki te aata a te Atua, ki
te Atua, ki toku hari nui: ae, ka whakamoemiti ki a koe, e te Atua, e
toku Atua, i runga i te hapa.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> He aha koe i piko ai, e toku wairua? He
aha koe i ohorere ai i roto i ahau? Tumanako ki te Atua: tera ano ahau e
whakawhetai ki a ia, ko te ora nei ia o toku mata, ko toku Atua.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ma nga tama a
Koraha. He Makiri. E te Atua, kua rongo o matou taringa, kua korerotia
ki a matou e o matou matua, nga mahi i mahia e koe i o ratou ra, i nga
ra o mua.

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> Nau nga tauiwi i pana ki tou ringa, nau
ratou i whakato: nau nga iwi i whiu, a whakamararatia ana ratou.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> Ehara hoki i te mea, na ta ratou hoari i
whiwhi ai ratou ki te whenua, ehara to ratou takakau i te mea i ora ai
ratou: engari na tou matau, na tou takakau hoki, na te marama ano o tou
mata, he pai hoki nou ki a ratou.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> E te Atua, ko koe toku Kingi: whakahaua
he whakaora mo Hakapa.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Mau ka turaki ai matou i o matou hoariri;
ma tou ingoa ka takahia ai e matou te hunga e whakatika ana ki a matou.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> E kore hoki ahau e whakawhirinaki ki taku
kopere: e kore ano taku hoari e whakaora i ahau.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Nau hoki matou i ora ai i o matou
hoariri: nau ano i whakama ai te hunga i kino ki a matou.

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> Ko te Atua ta matou e whakamanamana ai i
te roa o te ra: ka whakamoemiti ano matou ki tou ingoa ake ake. (Hera.

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> ¶ Otira kua panga nei matou e koe, kua
meinga kia whakama: kahore hoki koe kia haere tahi me a matou taua.

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Kua meinga matou kia hoki whakamuri mai
i te hoariri; kei te pahua ano i etahi ma ratou te hunga e kino ana ki a
matou.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Kua hoatu matou e koe, ano he hipi e
kainga ana: kua marara ki roto ki nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> E hokona ana e koe tau iwi, a hore he
utu: kahore hoki koe e whiwhi rawa i te utu mo ratou.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> E meinga ana matou e koe hei tawainga
ma o matou hoa kainga; hei whakahaweatanga, hei whakakatanga mai ma te
hunga i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha o matou.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> E meinga ana matou e koe hei whakatauki
ma nga tauiwi; hei rurutanga matenga ma nga iwi.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> Kei mua tonu i ahau toku whakama; kua
taupokina ahau e te pawera o toku mata;

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> I te reo o te kaitawai, o te
kaikohukohu; i te hoariri, i te kairapu utu.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> ¶ Kua pa katoa tenei ki a matou; heoi
kahore matou i wareware ki a koe, kihai ano i teka ki tau kawenata.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> Kahore to matou ngakau i tahuri
whakamuri; kihai ano o matou hikoinga i peka ke i tau ara;

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> I maru ai matou i a koe i te wahi o nga
tarakona; a taupoki rawa ki te atarangi o te mate.

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Mehemea kua wareware matou ki te ingoa
o to matou Atua, kua totoro ranei o matou ringa ki te atua ke;

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> E kore ranei tenei e ata tirohia e te
Atua? E matau ana hoki ia ki nga mea ngaro o te ngakau.

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> Mou nei hoki matou i patua ai i te ra
roa nei: kiia iho matou he hipi e patua ana.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> E ara, he aha koe ka moe ai, e te
Ariki? Whakatika, kaua matou e panga tonutia.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> He aha koe ka huna ai i tou mata? ka
wareware ai ki to matou mamae, ki to matou tukinotanga?

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> Kua piko nei hoki to matou wairua ki
raro ki te puehu; piri rawa to matou kopu ki te whenua.

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> E ara, hei awhina i a matou; kia mahara
ki tou aroha, a hokona matou.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Homhanimi
ma nga tama a Koraha. He Makiri, he waiata aroha. E pupuke ake ana te
mea pai i roto i toku ngakau: ka korerotia e ahau aku i tito ai mo te
kingi: he pene toku arero na te kaituhituhi hohoro.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Engari koe he ataahua i nga tama a te
tangata: kua ringihia ou ngutu ki te ahuareka, na reira i manaakitia ai
koe e te Atua ake ake.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Whitikiria tau hoari ki tou huwha, e te
Nui Rawa, tou kororia me tou honore.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Aratakina hoki tou hoiho i runga i tou
honore, i te kaha, hei mea hoki mo te pono, mo te mahaki, mo te tika, a
ma tou matau koe e whakaako ki nga mea whakamataku.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> He koi au pere; ka hinga nga iwi ki raro
i a koe; kei roto ratou i te ngakau o nga hoariri o te kingi.

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> ¶ He pumau, e te Atua, tou torona ake
ake: he hepeta tika te hepeta o tou kingitanga.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> Kua aroha koe ki te tika, kua kino ki te
hara: na reira, nui atu i to ou hoa te whakawahinga a te Atua, a tou
Atua i a koe ki te hinu o te hari.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> Ko tou kakahu katoa he kakara maira, he
aroe, he kahia; ko nga mea aho, whakatangitangi o nga whare rei nana koe
i whakaahuareka.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Kei roto i au wahine honore nga tamahine
kingi; kei tou matau te kuini e tu ana, no Opira te koura.

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> ¶ Whakarongo, e ko, titiro, tahuri iho
tou taringa: a kia wareware koe ki tou iwi, ki te whare ano o tou papa.

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> Penei ka matenuitia e te kingi tou
ataahua: ko ia hoki tou Ariki; a me koropiko ki a ia.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> Ko reira ano te tamahine o Taira me te
ohaoha: ka whai ano nga tangata taonga o te iwi kia manakohia e koe.

<span id="an_45:13">45:13</span> Kei roto te tamahine a te kingi, he
kororia kau, he mea whakairo ki te koura tona kakahu.

<span id="an_45:14">45:14</span> He mea whakapaipai ki te ngira tona
kakahu e kawea ai ia ki te kingi: ka arahina ki a koe nga wahine, ona
takahoa e whai ana i a ia.

<span id="an_45:15">45:15</span> He hari, he koa ina kawea mai ratou; ka
tomo ki te whare o te kingi.

<span id="an_45:16">45:16</span> Ko au tamariki hei whakakapi mo ou
matua: ka meinga ano ratou e koe hei kawana mo te whenua katoa.

<span id="an_45:17">45:17</span> Ka meinga e ahau tou ingoa kia
maharatia e nga whakatupuranga katoa: e whakamoemititia ai koe e nga iwi
a ake ake.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ma nga tama a
Koraha. He waiata Aramoto. Ko te Atua to tatou piringa, to tatou kaha;
he kaiawhina e tino tata ana i nga wa o te he.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> Na reira kore ake to tatou wehi, ahakoa
nekehia te whenua, ahakoa kahakina nga maunga ki waenga moana;

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Ahakoa rara, taupatupatu noa ona wai,
ahakoa wiri nga maunga i tona huamo. (Hera.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> He awa tena ko ona manga hei whakahari i
te pa o te Atua, i te wahi tapu o nga tapenakara o te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> Kei waenganui ona te Atua, e kore ia e
whakakorikoria: ma te Atua ia e awhina i te putanga ano o te ata.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> ¶ I nana nga tauiwi, i whakakorikoria nga
rangatiratanga; puaki ana tona reo, rewa ana te whenua.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> Kei a tatou a Ihowa o nga mano, ko te
Atua o Hakopa to tatou piringa. (Hera.

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> Haere mai, tirohia nga mahi a Ihowa, nga
whakangaromanga i whakaputaina e ia ki te whenua.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> E whakamutua ana e ia nga whainga a te
pito ra ano o te whenua: whati ana i a ia te kopere, poro pu te tao,
tahuna ake e ia te hariata ki te kapura.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> Kia ata noho, a kia matau ko ahau te
Atua; e whakanuia ahau i waenganui i nga tauiwi, e whakanuia ahau i te
whenua.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> Kei a tatou a Ihowa o nga mano: ko te
Atua o Hakopa to tatou piringa. (Hera.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma
nga tama a Koraha. Pakia o koutou ringa, e nga iwi katoa: hamama ki te
Atua, kia hari te reo.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> No te mea he wehi a Ihowa, te Runga Rawa,
he kingi nui ia no te whenua katoa.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Mana e riro ai nga iwi ki raro i a tatou,
me nga tautangata ki raro ki o tatou waewae.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> Mana e whiriwhiri to tatou nohoanga mo
tatou, te mea pai rawa o Hakopa, o tana i aroha ai. (Hera.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> ¶ Kua kake atu te Atua i roto i te
hamama, a Ihowa i roto i te tangi o te tetere.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> Himene ki te Atua, himene atu; himene ki
to tatou Kingi, himene atu.

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> Ko te Atua hoki te Kingi o te whenua
katoa: himene atu i runga i te mohio.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> Ko te Atua te Kingi o nga tauiwi: e noho
ana te Atua i runga i te torona o tona tapu.

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> Kua huihui nga rangatira o nga iwi, hei
iwi mo te Atua o Aperahama: na te Atua hoki nga whakangungu rakau o te
whenua; kua whakanuia rawatia ia.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> ¶ He waiata, he himene ma nga tama a
Koraha. He nui a Ihowa, kia nui hoki te whakamoemiti ki a ia i te pa o
to tatou Atua, i te maunga o tona tapu.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Ataahua ana te tairanga o Maunga Hiona,
ko ta te ao katoa e koa ai: kei te taha ki te raki te pa o te Kingi nui.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> E matauria ana te Atua i roto i ona whare
papai hei piringa.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> Na, huihui tahi mai ana nga kingi haere
tahi atu ana ratou.

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> I kite ratou, miharo iho: raruraru ana,
hohoro tonu atu.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Pa ana te wehi ki a ratou i reira, te
mamae, ano he wahine e whanau ana.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> E wahia ana e koe nga kaipuke o Tarahihi
ki te marangai.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> ¶ Rite tonu ki ta matou i rongo ai, ta
matou i kite ai i roto i te pa o Ihowa o nga mano, i te pa o to tatou
Atua: ma te Atua e whakapumau ake ake. (Hera.

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> I whakaaroaro matou ki tou atawhai, e te
Atua, i waenganui o tou temepara.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> E te Atua, rite tahi ki tou ingoa te
whakamoemiti mou, tae noa atu ki nga pito o te whenua: ki tonu tou matau
i te tika.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> Kia hari a Maunga Hiona, kia koa nga
tamahine a Hura i au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> Taiawhiotia a Hiona, haere, a kopiko
noa mai: taua ona pourewa.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> Maharatia ona pekerangi, tirohia ona
whare papai; hei korerotanga ma koutou ki enei ake whakatupuranga.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> Ko tenei Atua hoki te Atua mo tatou ake
ake: ko ia hei kaiarahi i a tatou a mate noa.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma
nga tama a Koraha. Whakarongo ki tenei, e nga iwi katoa: tahuri mai o
koutou taringa, e nga tangata katoa o te ao.

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> E nga tangata iti, koutou ko nga tangata
rahi, e te tangata taonga korua ko te rawakore.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> Ka whakapuakina he matauranga e toku
mangai: a he ata ngarahu te whakaaro o toku ngakau.

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> Ka titaha toku taringa ki te kupu
whakarite; ka puaki taku pepeha i runga i te hapa.

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> Kia wehi ahau ki te aha i nga ra o te
kino, ina karapotia ahau e te kino kei oku rekereke?

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> ¶ Ko te hunga e whakawhirinaki ana ki o
ratou taonga, e whakamanamana ana ki te nui o o ratou rawa;

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> E kore tetahi o ratou e ahei te hoko i
tona teina, te hoatu ranei i tetahi utu mona ki te Atua;

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> He nui hoki te utu mo to ratou wairua, a
me whakarere atu ake ake;

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> Kia ora tonu ai ia ake ake: kia kaua e
kite i te pirau.

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> E kite ana hoki ia e matemate ana nga
tangata whakaaro nui, e ngaro ngatahi ana te poauau me te whakaarokore,
a mahue iho o ratou taonga ki etahi atu.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> Ki to ratou whakaaro puku, tera e pumau
tonu o ratou whare me o ratou nohoanga, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa:
huaina iho o ratou whenua ki o ratou ingoa.

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> Heoi kahore te tangata e noho tonu i
roto i te honore: ko tona rite kei nga kararehe ka moti nei.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> Ko to ratou ara tenei, ara ko to ratou
poauau: heoi e whakapai ana to ratou uri ki a ratou korero. (Hera.

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Kei te hipi te rite: ko te wahi mo
ratou ko te reinga; ko te mate hei hepara mo ratou, hei rangatira ano te
hunga tika mo ratou i te ata; ko to ratou ataahua ma te reinga e
whakamoti, kia kore ai he whare mona.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> ¶ Ma te Atua ia toku wairua e hoko mai
i te reinga: ko ia hoki hei tukunga atu moku. (Hera.

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> Kaua e wehi ua whai taonga te tangata,
ina nui haere te kororia o tona whare;

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> Kahore hoki ana mea e mau atu ai ia ina
mate; e kore tona kororia e tuku iho i muri i a ia.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> Whakapai noa ia i tona wairua i a ia e
ora ana; a ka whakamoemititia koe ua pai au mahi ki a koe ano.

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> Ka haere ia ki te whakatupuranga o ona
tupuna: e kore rawa ratou e kite i te marama.

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> Ko te tangata e whakahonoretia ana, a
kahore e whai whakaaro, kei nga kararehe ka moti nei tona rite.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. Kua puaki te kupu a
te Atua, a te Atua tonu, a Ihowa, a karangatia ana e ia te whenua i te
putanga mai o te ra, tae noa ki tona torengitanga.

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> Kua tiaho mai te Atua i roto i Hiona, i
te tino o te ataahua.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> Ka haere mai to tatou Atua, e kore ano e
wahangu: ka kai te kapura i tona aroaro, a ka hukerikeri te awha ki
tetahi taha ona, ki tetahi taha.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> Ka karangatia e ia nga rangi i runga, me
te whenua hoki, ki te whakaritenga mo tona iwi.

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> Huihuia mai ki ahau taku hunga tapu, te
hunga i whakarite kawenata ki ahau i runga i te patunga tapu.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> A ma nga rangi e whakakite tona tika: ko
te Atua ake nei hoki te kaiwhakawa. (Hera.

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> ¶ Whakarongo, e toku iwi, a ka korero
ahau; e Iharaira, ka whakaatu ahau ki a koe; ko ahau te Atua, ko tou
Atua.

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> E kore ahau e riri ki a koe mo au patunga
tapu; a kei toku aroaro tonu au tahunga tinana.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> E kore ahau e tango i tetahi puru i roto
i tou whare, i etahi koati toa ranei i roto i au taiepa.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> Naku nei hoki nga kirehe katoa o te
ngahere, nga kararehe i runga i te mano o nga pukepuke.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> E matau ana ahau ki nga manu katoa o
nga maunga; naku ano nga kirehe o te parae.

<span id="an_50:12">50:12</span> Me he matekai toku, e kore ahau e
korero ki a koe: naku nei hoki te ao, me ona tini mea.

<span id="an_50:13">50:13</span> E kai koia ahau i te kikokiko o nga
puru, e inu ranei i te toto o nga koati?

<span id="an_50:14">50:14</span> Ko te whakawhetai hei patunga tapu mau
ki te Atua; whakamana hoki au kupu taurangi ki te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_50:15">50:15</span> A karanga ki ahau i te ra o te he: maku
koe e whakaora, a ka whakakororiatia ahau e koe.

<span id="an_50:16">50:16</span> ¶ Ki te tangata hara ia ka mea te Atua,
He aha mau te whakapuaki i aku tikanga, te whakahua ranei i taku
kawenata e tou mangai?

<span id="an_50:17">50:17</span> Kua kino nei hoki koe ki te ako, a e
akiri ana i aku kupu ki muri i a koe.

<span id="an_50:18">50:18</span> I tou kitenga i te tahae, na whakaae
ana koe ki a ia; a whai tahi ana me te hunga puremu.

<span id="an_50:19">50:19</span> Kua tukua e koe tou mangai ki te kino;
a e tito hianga ana tou arero.

<span id="an_50:20">50:20</span> Noho ana koe, ka korero kino ki tou
teina: ngautuara tonu iho koe ki te tama a tou whaea.

<span id="an_50:21">50:21</span> Ko au mahi enei, a wahangu tonu ahau; i
mea koe he pena pu ahau me koe: otira ka riria koe e ahau, ka
whakararangitia ano aua mea ki tou aroaro.

<span id="an_50:22">50:22</span> Na whakaaroa tenei, e te hunga kua
wareware ki te Atua; kei haehaea koutou e ahau, a kahore he kaiwhakaora.

<span id="an_50:23">50:23</span> Ko te whakamoemiti te patunga tapu e
whai kororia ai ahau: ko te tangata hoki he tika nei tona ara ka
whakakitea e ahau ki a ia te whakaoranga a te Atua.

<span id="an_51:1">51:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri, i te taenga o Natana poropiti ki a ia, mo tona haerenga ki a
Patehepa. Tohungia ahau, e te Atua, kia rite ki tou atawhai: kia rite ki
tou aroha nui te murunga o oku he.

<span id="an_51:2">51:2</span> Horoia rawatia toku kino: kia ma hoki
toku hara.

<span id="an_51:3">51:3</span> E whaki ana hoki ahau i aku mahi tutu:
kei toku aroaro tonu toku hara.

<span id="an_51:4">51:4</span> He hara ki a koe, ki a koe anake, toku; i
meatia ano tenei he ki tou aroaro; kia tika ai koe i tau korerotanga,
kia ma ai hoki ina whakawa.

<span id="an_51:5">51:5</span> Na i whakaahuatia ahau i roto i te kino,
i runga ano i te hara toku whakahaputanga ki roto ki toku whaea.

<span id="an_51:6">51:6</span> Na ko tau e matenui ai ko te pono i nga
wahi o roto, a ka whakaakona oku wahi ngaro e koe ki te whakaaro nui.

<span id="an_51:7">51:7</span> ¶ Purea ahau ki te hihopa, a ka ma ahau;
horoia ahau, a ka ma ke atu i te hukarere.

<span id="an_51:8">51:8</span> Meinga kia rongo ahau i te hari, i te
koa, a ka whakamanamana nga iwi i whatiia nei e koe.

<span id="an_51:9">51:9</span> Huna tou mata ki oku hara; a murua
katoatia oku kino.

<span id="an_51:10">51:10</span> Hanga, e te Atua, he ngakau ma ki roto
ki ahau: whakahoutia hoki ki roto ki ahau he wairua tika.

<span id="an_51:11">51:11</span> Kaua ahau e maka i tou aroaro; kaua
hoki tou wairua tapu e tangohia i ahau.

<span id="an_51:12">51:12</span> Whakahokia mai ki ahau te hari o tau
whakaoranga: tautokona hoki ahau ki te wairua kakama.

<span id="an_51:13">51:13</span> Ko reira ahau whakaako ai i au ara ki
te hunga tutu; a ka tahuri te hunga hara ki a koe.

<span id="an_51:14">51:14</span> ¶ Whakaorangia ahau i te hara toto, e
te Atua, e te Atua o toku whakaoranga, a ka waiatatia au mahi tika e
toku arero.

<span id="an_51:15">51:15</span> Whakatuwheratia oku ngutu, e te Ariki;
a ka puaki i toku mangai te whakamoemiti ki a koe.

<span id="an_51:16">51:16</span> Kahore nei hoki koe e aro ki te patunga
tapu; penei kua hoatu e ahau: kahore koe e ahuareka ki te tahunga
tinana.

<span id="an_51:17">51:17</span> Ko nga patunga tapu ma te Atua he
wairua maru: e kore koe e whakahawea e te Atua, ki te ngakau maru, ki te
ngakau iro.

<span id="an_51:18">51:18</span> Kia pai koe ki te atawhai i Hiona:
hanga nga taiepa o Hiruharama.

<span id="an_51:19">51:19</span> Ko reira koe pai ai ki nga patunga tapu
o te tika, ki nga tahunga tinana, he mea whakaeke katoa: ko reira ratou
whakaeke ai i nga puru ki runga ki tou aata.

<span id="an_52:1">52:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Makiri; na
Rawiri, i a Roeke Eromi i haere, i whakaatu ki a Haora, i mea ki a ia,
Kua tae a Rawiri ki te whare o Ahimereke. He aha koe ka whakapakari ai
ki te kino, e te tangata nui? He pumau tonu te atawhai o te Atua.

<span id="an_52:2">52:2</span> E whakatakoto ana tou arero i nga mea
nanakia, e mahi hianga ana, ano he heu koi.

<span id="an_52:3">52:3</span> E arohaina rawatia ana e koe te kino i te
pai, te teka i te korero tika. (Hera.

<span id="an_52:4">52:4</span> E te arero hianga, e arohaina ana e koe
nga kupu horomiti katoa.

<span id="an_52:5">52:5</span> Ka whakangaro hoki te Atua i a koe ake
tonu atu; ka tangohia atu koe e ia, ka takiritia atu i tou nohoanga, ka
hutia atu hoki koe i te whenua o te ora. (Hera.

<span id="an_52:6">52:6</span> ¶ E kite hoki te hunga tika, a ka wehi;
ka kata hoki ki a ia, ka mea,

<span id="an_52:7">52:7</span> Inana, ko te tangata tenei kihai nei i
waiho e ia te Atua hei kaha mona; otiia, whakawhirinaki ana ki te tini o
ana taonga, whakapakari ana i runga i tana mahi kino.

<span id="an_52:8">52:8</span> Ko ahau ia, e rite ana ki te oriwa
matomato i roto i te whare o te Atua: ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki te mahi
tohu a te Atua ake ake.

<span id="an_52:9">52:9</span> Ka whakamoemiti tonu ahau ki a koe, nau
hoki tenei i mea: ka tumanako ano ki tou ingoa; he mea pai hoki, ki te
aroaro o tau hunga tapu.

<span id="an_53:1">53:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Maharata. He
Makiri, na Rawiri. Kua ki te wairangi i roto i tona ngakau, Kahore he
Atua. Kua pirau ratou, he kino whakahouhou ta ratou mahi; kahore tetahi
e mahi ana i te pai.

<span id="an_53:2">53:2</span> I titiro iho te Atua i te rangi ki nga
tama a te tangata, kia kite me kahore tetahi e mahara ana, e rapu ana i
te Atua.

<span id="an_53:3">53:3</span> Kua hoki ki muri ratou katoa, kua pirau
tahi: kahore tetahi e mahi ana i te pai, kahore kia kotahi.

<span id="an_53:4">53:4</span> E kore ranei e mohio nga kaimahi i te
kino? e kai nei i toku iwi, me te mea e kai taro ana; a kahore e karanga
ki te Atua.

<span id="an_53:5">53:5</span> Wehi noa iho ratou i reira, i te wahi
kahore he wehi, no te mea kua titaria e te Atua nga wheua o te tangata i
whakapaea ai koe: kua whakama ratou i a koe; no te mea kua whakahaweatia
ratou e te Atua

<span id="an_53:6">53:6</span> Aue, me i puta mai te whakaoranga o
Iharaira i Hiona! Kia whakahokia mai e te Atua tana iwi i te whakarau,
ka whakamanamana a Hakopa, ka hari a Iharaira.

<span id="an_54:1">54:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He
Makiri, na Rawiri i te haerenga o nga Tiwhi ki a Haora, ki ai, He teka
ianei kei a matou a Rawiri e piri ana? E te Atua, kia whakaorangia ahau
e tou ingoa; kia whakawakia hoki ahau e tou kaha.

<span id="an_54:2">54:2</span> E te Atua, whakarongo ki taku inoi,
tahuri mai tou taringa ki nga kupu a toku mangai.

<span id="an_54:3">54:3</span> No te mea kua whakatika mai nga tangata
iwi ki ki ahau, a e whaia ana toku wairua e te hunga tukino: kahore i
waiho e ratou te Atua ki to ratou aroaro. (Hera.

<span id="an_54:4">54:4</span> ¶ Tenei te Atua hei kaiawhina moku; kei
roto te Ariki i te hunga e tautoko ake ana i toku wairua.

<span id="an_54:5">54:5</span> Mana e utu te kino o oku hoariri: huna
ratou, he pono nei hoki koe.

<span id="an_54:6">54:6</span> Ka kakama ahau ki te mea patunga tapu ki
a koe, ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa: he mea pai hoki.

<span id="an_54:7">54:7</span> Kua whakaorangia hoki ahau e ia i roto i
nga he katoa: a kua titiro toku kanohi ki te mea e hiahia ana ahau ki
oku hoariri.

<span id="an_55:1">55:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi Nekinoto. He
Makiri, na Rawiri. E te Atua, tahuri mai tou taringa ki taku inoi: kei
whakangaro atu koe, ina tangi ahau.

<span id="an_55:2">55:2</span> Anga mai ki ahau, whakahokia mai he kupu
ki ahau: pokaikaha noa iho ahau i ahau e tangi nei, e hamama nei;

<span id="an_55:3">55:3</span> I te reo hoki o te hoariri, i te tukino a
te tangata kino: no te mea e utaina ana e ratou he hara ki runga ki
ahau, a e kino ana ki ahau, e riri ana.

<span id="an_55:4">55:4</span> Mamae pu toku ngakau i roto i ahau: kua
taka ki runga ki ahau nga wehi whakamate.

<span id="an_55:5">55:5</span> Kua pa ki ahau te wehi me te wiri: a
pokia iho ahau e te whakamataku.

<span id="an_55:6">55:6</span> Na ko taku meatanga, Aue, te whai pakau
ahau me he kukupa; penei ka rere atu ahau, a ka whai okiokinga.

<span id="an_55:7">55:7</span> Katahi ahau ka rere ki tawhiti; a noho
rawa atu i te koraha. (Hera.

<span id="an_55:8">55:8</span> Ka hohoro toku rere atu i te hau, i te
awha.

<span id="an_55:9">55:9</span> ¶ Whakangaromia, e te Ariki, wehia o
ratou arero; kua kitea hoki e ahau te tukino me te tutu o roto o te pa.

<span id="an_55:10">55:10</span> Haereere ana ratou i te ao, i te po, i
runga i ona taiepa, a tawhio noa: he kino kei roto, he hianga.

<span id="an_55:11">55:11</span> He hara kei waenganui ona: kahore ona
ara e mahue i te tinihanga, i te hianga.

<span id="an_55:12">55:12</span> Ehara hoki i te hoariri nana ahau i
tawai; penei e taea e ahau te whakaririka: ehara hoki i te hoa whawhai
noku i whakakake ki ahau; penei kua piri ahau, kei kitea e ia.

<span id="an_55:13">55:13</span> Nau ia, na te tangata i rite ki ahau,
na toku takahoa, na taku i mohio ai.

<span id="an_55:14">55:14</span> Ahuareka tonu ta taua korerorero; haere
tahi ana hoki taua i roto i te ropu ki te whare o te Atua.

<span id="an_55:15">55:15</span> Kia mau ohorere ratou i te mate, kia
heke ora ki te reinga: he hara hoki kei o ratou nohoanga, kei waenganui
i a ratou.

<span id="an_55:16">55:16</span> ¶ Ko ahau, ka karanga ahau ki te Atua:
a ma Ihowa ahau e whakaora.

<span id="an_55:17">55:17</span> I te ahiahi, i te ata, i te
poutumarotanga, ka inoi ahau, ka tangi: a ka whakarongo ia ki toku reo.

<span id="an_55:18">55:18</span> Whakaorangia ana e ia toku wairua i
runga i te rangimarie i ahau e whakaekea ana: he tokomaha hoki oku hoa
whawhai.

<span id="an_55:19">55:19</span> Ka whakarongo te Atua, no tua iho nei
tona nohoanga, a ka whakahoki i ta ratou. (Hera.) Ko te hunga kahore o
ratou whakawhitiwhitinga, a kahore o ratou wehi ki te Atua.

<span id="an_55:20">55:20</span> Kua totoro ona ringa ki te hunga kua
mau nei ta ratou rongo ki a ia; kua whakataka e ia tana kawenata.

<span id="an_55:21">55:21</span> Maeneene atu tona mangai i te pata, he
whawhai ia kei roto i tona ngakau: ngawari atu ana kupu i te hinu,
kahore, he hoari kua oti te unu.

<span id="an_55:22">55:22</span> Maka ki runga ki a Ihowa tau pikaunga,
a mana koe e whakau ake: e kore e tukua e ia te hunga tika kia
whakangaueuetia ake ake.

<span id="an_55:23">55:23</span> Mau ia ratou e mea, e te Atua, kia heke
ki te poka o te pirau: e kore nga tangata toto, nga tangata hianga e
tutuki ki te hawhe o o ratou ra; ko ahau ia, ka whakawhirinaki ki a koe.

<span id="an_56:1">56:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Ionata ereme
rehokime. Na Rawiri. He Mikitama, i a ia ka mau i nga Pirihitini ki
Kata. Tohungia ahau e te Atua, ka horomia hoki ahau e te tangata: e
tukino ana ia ki ahau i te ra roa nei, i a ia e ngangare tonu nei.

<span id="an_56:2">56:2</span> E whai ana oku hoariri i te ra roa nei,
kia horomia ahau; he tokomaha nei hoki e whakahi ana, e whawhai mai ana
ki ahau.

<span id="an_56:3">56:3</span> Ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki a koe i te wa e
mataku ai ahau.

<span id="an_56:4">56:4</span> Ma te Atua ahau ka whakamoemiti ki tana
kupu: e whakawhirinaki ana ahau ki te Atua, e kore ahau e wehi. He aha
ta te kikokiko e mea ai ki ahau?

<span id="an_56:5">56:5</span> E whakariroia ketia ana e ratou aku kupu
i nga ra katoa; heoi ano ta ratou e whakaaro ai ko te kino moku.

<span id="an_56:6">56:6</span> E huihui ana ratou, e piri ana: e titiro
matatau ana ki oku hikoinga, i a ratou e whanga nei ki toku wairua.

<span id="an_56:7">56:7</span> Ma te he koia ratou ka mawhiti ai? kia
riri koe, e te Atua, whakataka iho hoki nga iwi.

<span id="an_56:8">56:8</span> ¶ E taua ana e koe oku kopikopikotanga:
rongoatia oku roimata ki roto ki tau ipu: kahore ianei i tau pukapuka?

<span id="an_56:9">56:9</span> I te ra e karanga ai ahau ka hoki
whakamuri oku hoariri: e matau ana ahau ki tenei, kei ahau hoki te Atua.

<span id="an_56:10">56:10</span> Ma te Atua ahau ka whakamoemiti ai ki
tana kupu; ma Ihowa ahau ka whakamoemiti ai ki tana kupu.

<span id="an_56:11">56:11</span> E whakawhirinaki ana ahau ki te Atua: e
kore ahau e wehi. He aha ta te tangata e mea ai ki ahau?

<span id="an_56:12">56:12</span> Kei ahau nga kupu taurangi ki a koe, e
te Atua: me tuku e ahau nga whakamoemiti ki a koe.

<span id="an_56:13">56:13</span> Nau hoki toku wairua i whakaora kei
mata: e kore ianei koe e whakau i oku waewae kei paheke, kia haere ai
ahau i te aroaro o te Atua i roto i te marama o te hunga ora.

<span id="an_57:1">57:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He
Mikitama. Na Rawiri, i tona rerenga i a Haora i a ia nei i roto i te
ana. Tohungia ahau, e te Atua, tohungia ahau, e whakawhirinaki ana hoki
toku wairua ki a koe: ae, ka piri ahau ki raro ki te taumarumarut anga o
ou pakau, kia pahemo ra ano enei mate.

<span id="an_57:2">57:2</span> Ka karanga ahau ki te Atua, ki te Runga
Rawa, ki te Atua e oti ai aku mea katoa.

<span id="an_57:3">57:3</span> Ka unga mai e ia he kaiwhakaora moku i te
rangi, ina tawai te tangata e mea ana kia horomia ahau; (Hera.) ka unga
mai e te Atua tana mahi tohu me tona pono.

<span id="an_57:4">57:4</span> Kei waenganui toku wairua i nga raiona: e
takoto ana ahau i waenganui i te hunga e kaia ana e te ahi; i nga tama
hoki a te tangata, he tao nei o ratou niho, he pere, he hoari koi ano o
ratou arero.

<span id="an_57:5">57:5</span> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga
ake i nga rangi: hei runga atu i te whenua katoa tou kororia.

<span id="an_57:6">57:6</span> Kua whakatakotoria e ratou he kupenga mo
oku takahanga, kua piko toku wairua: kua keria e ratou he poka ki toku
aroaro, a taka iho ko ratou ano ki roto. (Hera.

<span id="an_57:7">57:7</span> ¶ Pamau tonu toku ngakau, e te Atua,
pumau tonu toku ngakau: ka waiata ahau, ae, ka himene ahau.

<span id="an_57:8">57:8</span> E ara, e toku kororia; e ara, e te
hatere, e te hapa: ka ara wawe ano ahau.

<span id="an_57:9">57:9</span> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, e te
Ariki, i waenganui i nga iwi; ka himene ki a koe i waenganui i nga
tauiwi.

<span id="an_57:10">57:10</span> He nui hoki tau mahi tohu, a tutuki noa
ki nga rangi, me tou pono a tutuki noa ki nga kapua.

<span id="an_57:11">57:11</span> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga
i nga rangi: hei runga i te whenua katoa tou kororia.

<span id="an_58:1">58:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He
Mikitama. Na Rawiri. He korero puku ranei ta koutou i te pono? he tika
ranei ta koutou whakarite, e nga tama a te tangata?

<span id="an_58:2">58:2</span> He pono, e mahia ana e koutou te he i
roto i te ngakau, e paunatia ana e koutou te tutu a o koutou ringa i
runga i te whenua.

<span id="an_58:3">58:3</span> He tangata ke te hunga hara no te kopu
mai ano; whanau kau kua kotiti ke, kua korero teka.

<span id="an_58:4">58:4</span> Ko to ratou paihana he rite ki to te
nakahi, kei te neke turi e puru nei i tona taringa;

<span id="an_58:5">58:5</span> E kore nei e whakarongo ki te reo o te
kaiwhakawai, ahakoa tino matau ia ki te whakawai.

<span id="an_58:6">58:6</span> ¶ Whatiia, e te Atua, o ratou niho i roto
i o ratou mangai: kowhakia, e Ihowa, nga niho nunui o nga kuao raiona.

<span id="an_58:7">58:7</span> Kia mimiti ratou, ano he wai e heke atu
ana: ka whakatikaia ana pere, kia rite ki te mea kua poutoa.

<span id="an_58:8">58:8</span> Kia memeha haere, a kia pahure, ano he
ngata: kia rite ki te mea mate roto a te wahine, kahore nei i kite i te
ra.

<span id="an_58:9">58:9</span> E kore e tukua kia rongo a koutou kohua i
nga tataramoa, ka kahakina ratou e ia i roto i te awhiowhio, te mea
kaiota, te mea e wera ana.

<span id="an_58:10">58:10</span> Ka hari te tangata tika ua kite i te
utu: ka horoia e ia ona waewae ki nga toto o te tangata hara.

<span id="an_58:11">58:11</span> A ka mea te tangata, Koia, ka whai utu
te tangata tika: ina, he Atua ano tenei e whakawa ana i te whenua.

<span id="an_59:1">59:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He
Mikitama na Rawiri, i a Haora i tono tangata hei tiaki mo te whare, hei
whakamate mona. Whakaorangia ahau, e toku Atua, i oku hoariri:
whakateiteitia ake ahau i te hunga e whakatika ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_59:2">59:2</span> Whakaorangia ahau i nga kaimahi i te
kino: kia ora ahau i te hunga toto.

<span id="an_59:3">59:3</span> Kei te whanga nei hoki ratou mo toku
wairua: e whakamine ana te hunga kaha ki te whawhai ki ahau; kahore nei
oku tutu, kahore oku hara, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_59:4">59:4</span> Hore oku kino, oma ana ratou, kei te
takatu: e ara hei awhina moku, titiro mai hoki.

<span id="an_59:5">59:5</span> Ae ra, maranga, e Ihowa, e te Atua o nga
mano, e te Atua o Iharaira, tirohia iho nga tauiwi katoa: kaua e
tohungia tetahi o te hunga kino, e poka ke nei. (Hera.

<span id="an_59:6">59:6</span> Ka hoki mai ratou i te ahiahi, kei te
tau, ano he kuri, taiawhiotia ana e ratou te pa.

<span id="an_59:7">59:7</span> Nana, kei te kupa o ratou mangai, he
hoari kei o ratou ngutu: ki ta ratou, ko wai e rongo?

<span id="an_59:8">59:8</span> ¶ Ko tau ia, e Ihowa, he kata ki a ratou:
hei tawainga mau nga tauiwi katoa.

<span id="an_59:9">59:9</span> E toku kaha, ka tatari ahau ki a koe: ko
te Atua hoki toku pa.

<span id="an_59:10">59:10</span> Kei mua i ahau toku Atua aroha: ma te
Atua ahau ka kite i taku i hiahia ai ki oku hoariri.

<span id="an_59:11">59:11</span> Kaua ratou e whakamatea, kei wareware
toku iwi: kia whakamararatia ratou e tou kaha; whakataka iho ratou, e te
Ariki, e to matou whakangungu rakau.

<span id="an_59:12">59:12</span> Mo te hara o to ratou mangai, mo nga
kupu a o ratou ngutu, hopukia ratou i runga i to ratou whakakake, mo ta
ratou korero, he kanga, he teka.

<span id="an_59:13">59:13</span> Whakamotitia i runga i te riri, kia
kahore ai ratou: a kia matau ratou ko te Atua te Kawana o Hakopa puta
noa ki nga pito o te whenua. (Hera.

<span id="an_59:14">59:14</span> I te ahiahi tukua ratou kia hoki, tukua
ratou kia tau, ano he kuri, kia taiawhio ratou i te pa.

<span id="an_59:15">59:15</span> Ka kopikopiko noa ratou ki te rapu kai,
a ka tauwhanga i te po roa ina kore ratou e makona.

<span id="an_59:16">59:16</span> Ko ahau ia, ka waiatatia e ahau tou
kaha; ae, i te ata ka hamamatia e ahau tau mahi toku: ko koe hoki toku
pa, toku piringa i te ra o toku pouri.

<span id="an_59:17">59:17</span> Ka himene ahau ki a koe, e toku kaha:
ko te Atua nei hoki toku pa, toku Atua aroha.

<span id="an_60:1">60:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Huhana Erutu.
He Mikitama, na Rawiri, hei whakaako. No tana whawhaitanga ki a
Aramanaharaima raua ko Aramatopa. Na hoki ana a Ioapa, a patua ana e ia
a Eroma ki te Raorao Tote, kotahi tekau ma rua mano. E te Atua, kua pa
nga matou e koe, kua oti matou te whakamarara e koe, kua riri koe;
tahuri mai ano ki a matou.

<span id="an_60:2">60:2</span> Wiri ana te whenua i a koe: kua ngatata i
a koe: whakakapia ona wahi pakaru; e ru ana hoki.

<span id="an_60:3">60:3</span> He mea pakeke kua whakakitea e koe ki tau
iwi, kua oti matou te whakainu e koe ki te waina e wiri ai.

<span id="an_60:4">60:4</span> Kua homai e koe he kara ki te hunga e
wehi ana i a koe: kia whakakitea hei mea mo te pono. (Hera.

<span id="an_60:5">60:5</span> Hei mea e mawhiti ai au e aroha ai: ma
tou matau e whakaora, whakahokia mai hoki he kupu ki ahau.

<span id="an_60:6">60:6</span> ¶ Kua korero te Atua i runga i tona tapu;
ka hari ahau, ka kotikoti i Hekeme, ka roherohe hoki i te raorao o
Hukota.

<span id="an_60:7">60:7</span> Noku Kireara, noku ano a Manahi, ko
Eparaima ano hoki te kaha o toku matenga; ko Hura taku kaiwhakatakoto
ture;

<span id="an_60:8">60:8</span> Ko Moapa taku oko horoi; ka maka e ahau
toku hu ki runga ki Eroma: e Pirihitia, ko ahau hei whakamanamana mau.

<span id="an_60:9">60:9</span> Ma wai ahau e kawe ki te pa kaha? Na wai
ahau i arahi ki Eroma?

<span id="an_60:10">60:10</span> He teka ranei, e te Atua, kua panga
matou e koe? kahore hoki koe, e te Atua, e haere tahi me a matou taua.

<span id="an_60:11">60:11</span> Homai he awhina mo matou ki o matou
hoariri: he teka noa hoki te awhina a te tangata.

<span id="an_60:12">60:12</span> Ma te Atua tatou ka toa ai: mana hoki e
takahi ki raro o tatou hoa whawhai.

<span id="an_61:1">61:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekina. Na
Rawiri. Whakarongo, e te Atua, ki taku karanga: tahuri mai ki taku inoi.

<span id="an_61:2">61:2</span> Ka karanga ahau ki a koe i te pito o te
whenua, ina pehia toku ngakau: arahina ahau ki te kohatu e tiketike ake
ana i ahau.

<span id="an_61:3">61:3</span> He piringa hoki koe moku: he pa kaha i te
hoariri.

<span id="an_61:4">61:4</span> Ka noho ahau ki tou tapenakara ake ake,
ka okioki ki ou pakau hei piringa. (Hera.

<span id="an_61:5">61:5</span> ¶ Kua rongo nei hoki koe, e te Atua, i
aku kupu tauranga kua homai e koe te wahi o te hunga e wehi ana ki tou
ingoa.

<span id="an_61:6">61:6</span> Ka whakaraneatia e koe nga ra o te kingi;
ona tau ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_61:7">61:7</span> E noho ia i te aroaro o te Atua ake ake:
whakaritea mai he aroha, he pono, hei tiaki i a ia.

<span id="an_61:8">61:8</span> Penei ka himene ahau ki tou ingoa ake
ake: ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi i tenei ra, i tenei ra.

<span id="an_62:1">62:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a
Ierutonu. He himene na Rawiri. Ko te Atua anake taku e tatari nei: kei a
ia te whakaoranga moku.

<span id="an_62:2">62:2</span> Ko ia anake toku kohatu, toku
whakaoranga, toku pa hoki, e kore e nui toku ngaueuetanga.

<span id="an_62:3">62:3</span> Kia pehea te roa o ta koutou tatau ki te
tangata, kia whakamatea ai e koutou, e koutou katoa, ka rite ki te
taiepa e tungou ana, ki te wawa ka tata te hinga?

<span id="an_62:4">62:4</span> Heoi ano ta ratou e runanga ai ko te
turaki i a ia i tona wahi teitei: e ahuareka ana ki te teka; e manaaki
ana o ratou mangai, a e kanga ana a roto i a ratou. (Hera.

<span id="an_62:5">62:5</span> Tatari, e toku wairua, ki te Atua anaki;
ko ia taku e tumanako nei.

<span id="an_62:6">62:6</span> Ko ia anake toku kohatu, toku
whakaoranga, toku pa hoki; e kore ahau e whakangaueuetia.

<span id="an_62:7">62:7</span> Kei te Atua te whakaoranga moku, te
kororia ano moku; kei te Atua te kohatu o toku kaha, toku piringa.

<span id="an_62:8">62:8</span> ¶ Whakawhirinaki ki a ia i nga wa katoa,
e te iwi, ringihia to koutou ngakau ki tona aroaro: hei piringa mo tatou
te Atua (Hera.

<span id="an_62:9">62:9</span> He pono he mea memeha noa nga ware, he
teka noa nga rangatira; ki te paunatia ratou, mama noa ake ratou tahi i
te horihori.

<span id="an_62:10">62:10</span> Kaua e whakawhirinaki ki te tukino, kei
wairangi hoki ki te pahua: ki te tini haere nga taonga, kei whakamanawa
to koutou ngakau ki reira.

<span id="an_62:11">62:11</span> Kotahi korerotanga a te Atua, ka rua
oku rongonga i tenei, no te Atua te kaha.

<span id="an_62:12">62:12</span> Nau ano, e te Ariki, te mahi tohu: rite
tonu hoki ki tana mahi tau utu ki te tangata.

<span id="an_63:1">63:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri, i a ia i te koraha
o Hura. E te Atua, noku koe Atua; ka moata taku rapu i a koe. E hiainu
ana toku wairua ki a koe, e hiahia ana oku kikokiko ki a koe, i te
whenua maroke, ruha noa, kahore nei he wai.

<span id="an_63:2">63:2</span> Koia i titiro atu ai ahau ki a koe i te
wahi tapu, kia kite ai i tou kaha, i tou kororia.

<span id="an_63:3">63:3</span> ¶ Pai atu tou aroha i te ora: mo reira ka
whakamoemiti oku ngutu ki a koe.

<span id="an_63:4">63:4</span> Ina, ka whakapai ahau ki a koe i ahau ano
e ora nei; ka totoro atu oku ringa i runga i tou ingoa.

<span id="an_63:5">63:5</span> Ka makona toku wairua, ano i te hinu
wheua, i te ngako, a ka hari oku ngutu ina whakamoemiti toku mangai ki a
koe.

<span id="an_63:6">63:6</span> Ina mahara ahau ki a koe i runga i toku
moenga, ina whakaaro ki a koe i nga mataaratanga o te po.

<span id="an_63:7">63:7</span> ¶ Ko koe hoki toku kaiawhina: na ka hari
ahau ki te taumarumarutanga iho o ou pakau.

<span id="an_63:8">63:8</span> Piri tonu toku wairua ki a koe: e tautoko
ake ana tou matau i ahau.

<span id="an_63:9">63:9</span> Ko te hunga e whai ana i toku wairua kia
whakangaromia, ka riro ratou ki nga wahi o raro rawa o te whenua.

<span id="an_63:10">63:10</span> Ka tukua atu ratou ki te kaha o te
hoari: hei wahi ratou ma nga pokiha.

<span id="an_63:11">63:11</span> Tena ko te kingi, ka hari ia ki te
Atua; ka whakamanamana nga tangata katoa ko ia nei ta ratou oati: a ka
purua te mangai o te hunga katoa e korero teka ana.

<span id="an_64:1">64:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene na
Rawiri. Whakarongo ki toku reo, e te Atua, ina inoi atu ahau: tiakina
toku ora i te wehi o te hoariri.

<span id="an_64:2">64:2</span> Huna ahau i te whakaaro ngaro o te hunga
kino, i te ngangau a nga kaimahi i te he;

<span id="an_64:3">64:3</span> Kua whakakoi nei i o ratou arero, ano he
hoari, kua whakatika nei i a ratou pere, ara i nga kupu kikino,

<span id="an_64:4">64:4</span> Hei koperenga pukutanga ma ratou ki te
tangata tika; kitea rawatia ake kua kopere ki a ia, kahore hoki he wehi.

<span id="an_64:5">64:5</span> E whakamaia ana ratou i a ratou ano ki te
mea kino; e runanga ana kia whakatakotoria pukutia he rore, e mea ana,
Ko wai e kite i a ratou?

<span id="an_64:6">64:6</span> E rapu hara ana ratou; e mea ana, Kua ata
rapu marie tatou: taea noatia te hohonutanga o te whakaaro o ia tangata,
a ko te ngakau he hohonu.

<span id="an_64:7">64:7</span> ¶ Ma te Atua ia e kopere he pere ki a
ratou kitea rawatia ake kua tu ratou.

<span id="an_64:8">64:8</span> Heoi ka meinga ratou kia tapatu, ko to
ratou arero ake ano ka tu atu ki a ratou; a ka ruru i to ratou matenga
te hunga katoa e kite i a ratou.

<span id="an_64:9">64:9</span> Ka wehi ano hoki nga tangata katoa, ka
whakapuaki i te mahi a te Atua: ka ata maharatia hoki e ratou tana mahi.

<span id="an_64:10">64:10</span> Ka koa te tangata tika ki a Ihowa, ka
whakawhirinaki hoki ki a ia: ka whakamanamana ano te hunga ngakau tika
katoa.

<span id="an_65:1">65:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he
waiata na Rawiri. E taria ana koe, e te Atua, e te whakamoemiti i Hiona:
a ka whakamana te kupu taurangi ki a koe.

<span id="an_65:2">65:2</span> E te kaiwhakarongo inoi, e haere nga
kikokiko katoa ki a koe.

<span id="an_65:3">65:3</span> E kaha ake ana i ahau nga kino: a matou
mahi tutu, mau ena e hipoki.

<span id="an_65:4">65:4</span> Ka hari te tangata e whiriwhiria e koe, e
meatia e koe kia tata atu ki a koe, kia noho i roto i ou marae: ka
makona matou i te pai o tou whare, o tou temepara tapu.

<span id="an_65:5">65:5</span> He mea whakawehi, he tapu, tau utu kupu
ki a matou, e te Atua o to matou whakaoranga, e te okiokinga o nga pito
katoa o te whenua, o te hunga hoki i tawhiti i runga o te moana;

<span id="an_65:6">65:6</span> ¶ E whakau nei i nga maunga, he kaha hoki
nona; tona whitiki nei he kaha.

<span id="an_65:7">65:7</span> E whakamarie nei i te haruru o nga moana,
i te haruru o o ratou ngaru, i te ngangau hoki o nga iwi.

<span id="an_65:8">65:8</span> Ka wehi ano ki au tohu te hunga e noho
ana i nga pito rawa: hari ana i a koe nga putake o te ata, o te ahiahi.

<span id="an_65:9">65:9</span> E tirotirohia ana e koe te whenua, e
whakamakukuria ana, e whakamomonatia nuitia ana e koe; ki tonu te awa o
te Atua i te wai: oti rawa ake te whakapai e koe, kua rite mai i a koe
he witi mo aua wahi.

<span id="an_65:10">65:10</span> Makuku rawa i a koe ona moa, pe ana i a
koe ona tupuke: e whakangawaritia ana e koe ki nga ua: e manaakitia ana
e koe tona pihinga ake.

<span id="an_65:11">65:11</span> E karaunatia ana e koe te tau ki tou
pai; e maturuturu ana hoki te momonatanga o ou ara.

<span id="an_65:12">65:12</span> E maturuturu ana ki nga wahi kai o te
koraha: a whitikiria ana nga pukepuke ki te koa.

<span id="an_65:13">65:13</span> He hipi te kakahu o nga wahi kai; ngaro
ana nga raorao i te witi; hamama ana ratou i te hari, waiata ana.

<span id="an_66:1">66:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he
waiata. Hamama, e te whenua katoa, ki te Atua:

<span id="an_66:2">66:2</span> Himenetia te kororia o tona ingoa, kia
whai kororia te whakamoemiti ki a ia.

<span id="an_66:3">66:3</span> Mea atu ki te Atua, Ano te wehi o au
mahi! Ma te nui o tou kaha e ngohengohe ai ou hoariri ki a koe.

<span id="an_66:4">66:4</span> E koropiko katoa te whenua ki a koe; ka
himene ki a koe; ka himene ratou ki tou ingoa. (Hera.

<span id="an_66:5">66:5</span> Haere mai kia kite i nga mahi a te Atua:
mataku rawa tana mahi ki nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_66:6">66:6</span> Nana i mea te moana hei tuawhenua: haere
a waewae ana ratou ra roto i te awa; hari ana matou ki a ia i reira.

<span id="an_66:7">66:7</span> Ko tona kawanatanga tuturu tonu i runga i
tona kaha; e titiro ana ona kanohi ki nga tauiwi; kei whakakake te hunga
tutu. (Hera.

<span id="an_66:8">66:8</span> ¶ Whakapaingia to tatou Atua, e nga iwi;
kia rangona te reo whakamoemiti ki a ia.

<span id="an_66:9">66:9</span> Nana nei hoki i mau ai to tatou wairua ki
te ora, kahore hoki e tukua e ia o tatou waewae kia nekehia.

<span id="an_66:10">66:10</span> Kua whakamatauria hoki matou e koe, e
te Atua: whakarewaia ana matou e koe, ano he hiriwa e whakarewaia ana.

<span id="an_66:11">66:11</span> Kua kawea nei matou e koe ki roto ki te
kupenga: whakapikaua ana e koe te mea whakamamae ki o matou hope.

<span id="an_66:12">66:12</span> I meinga ano e koe o matou upoko kia
ekengia hoihotia e te tangata; i ra roto matou i te kapura, i te wai:
heoi whakaputaina mai ana matou e koe ki te wahi momona.

<span id="an_66:13">66:13</span> ¶ Ka tomo ahau me nga tahunga tinana ki
tou whare; ka whakamana ahau i aku kupu taurangi ki a koe,

<span id="an_66:14">66:14</span> Era i puaki i oku ngutu, i korerotia e
toku mangai i ahau e pouri ana.

<span id="an_66:15">66:15</span> Ka whakaekea e ahau mau nga mea momona
hei tahunga tinana, ngatahi ano me te mea kakara o nga hipi toa; ka
tukua e ahau he puru, he koati. (Hera.

<span id="an_66:16">66:16</span> Haere mai, whakarongo, e koutou katoa e
wehi ana ki te Atua, a maku e whakapuaki tana i mea ai ki toku wairua.

<span id="an_66:17">66:17</span> I tangi toku mangai ki a ia: i
whakanuia ano ia e toku arero.

<span id="an_66:18">66:18</span> Ki te whakaaroa e toku ngakau te he, e
kore te Ariki e whakarongo mai.

<span id="an_66:19">66:19</span> Nei ra he pono kua whakarongo te Atua,
kua tahuri ia ki toku reo inoi.

<span id="an_66:20">66:20</span> Kia whakapaingia te Atua, kihai nei i
whakapeau ke i taku inoi, i tana atawhai hoki ki ahau.

<span id="an_67:1">67:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekinoto. He
himene, he waiata. Ma te Atua tatou e atawhai, mana tatou e manaaki;
mana e mea kia tiaho tona mata ki a tatou; (Hera.

<span id="an_67:2">67:2</span> Kia matauria ai tau ara ki runga ki te
whenua, tau whakaoranga i roto i nga tauiwi katoa.

<span id="an_67:3">67:3</span> Kia whakamoemiti nga iwi ki a koe, e te
Atua, kia whakamoemiti nga iwi katoa ki a koe.

<span id="an_67:4">67:4</span> Kia koa nga tauiwi, kia waiata i te hari:
no te mea ka tika tau whakawa mo nga iwi, a ka kawana koe i nga tauiwi o
te whenua. (Hera.

<span id="an_67:5">67:5</span> Kia whakamoemiti nga iwi ki a koe, e te
Atua, kia whakamoemiti nga iwi katoa ki a koe.

<span id="an_67:6">67:6</span> Kua tuku mai nei te whenua i ona hua; a
ka manaaki te Atua, to tatou Atua, i a tatou.

<span id="an_67:7">67:7</span> Ka manaaki te Atua i a tatou; a ka wehi
nga pito katoa o te whenua i a ia.

<span id="an_68:1">68:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene, he
waiata na Rawiri. Kia ara te Atua, kia marara ona hoariri: kia whati
hoki i tona aroaro te hunga e kino ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_68:2">68:2</span> Aia atu ratou, peratia me te paowa e aia
ana: kia rite ki te ware pi e rewa ana i te kapura te ngaromanga o te
hunga kino i te aroaro o te Atua.

<span id="an_68:3">68:3</span> Kia koa ia te hunga tika; kia hari i te
aroaro o te Atua: ae ra, kia tino hari pu ratou.

<span id="an_68:4">68:4</span> Waiata ki te Atua, himenetia tona ingoa;
opehia ake he huanui mo tana hariata i nga koraha; tona ingoa ko IHA;
kia hari hoki ki tona aroaro.

<span id="an_68:5">68:5</span> Hei matua mo nga pani, hei kaiwhakarite
mo nga pouaru, te Atua i tona nohoanga tapu.

<span id="an_68:6">68:6</span> E whakanohoia ana e te Atua te mokemoke
ki te whare; e whakaputaina ana e ia nga herehere ki te ora: ko te hunga
tutu ia e noho i te wahi waikore.

<span id="an_68:7">68:7</span> ¶ E te Atua, i tou haerenga atu i mua i
tau iwi: i tou haerenga i te koraha; (Hera.

<span id="an_68:8">68:8</span> I wiri te whenua, i tuturu iho ano nga
rangi i te aroaro o te Atua; me taua Hinai ano i te aroaro o te Atua, o
te Atua o Iharaira.

<span id="an_68:9">68:9</span> I taia mai, e koe, e te Atua, he ua nui;
a i tou kainga e ruwha ana ka whakaukia e koe.

<span id="an_68:10">68:10</span> I noho tau whakaminenga ki reira: na
tou pai, e te Atua, i mea kai ai koe ma nga rawakore.

<span id="an_68:11">68:11</span> Ka homai e Ihowa te kupu: he ope nui
nga wahine whakapuaki.

<span id="an_68:12">68:12</span> Whati rawa nga kingi o nga taua: a ko
te wahine i noho i te whare, kei te tuwha i nga parakete.

<span id="an_68:13">68:13</span> I a koutou ka takoto noa i nga
takotoranga hipi, he rite ki nga pakau o te kukupa kua paparuatia nei ki
te hiriwa, ona hou ki te koura whero.

<span id="an_68:14">68:14</span> I te whakamararatanga a te Kaha Rawa i
nga kingi i reira, koia ano kei te hukarere o Taramono te ma.

<span id="an_68:15">68:15</span> ¶ He maunga Atua a Maunga Pahana; he
maunga tiketike a Maunga Pahana.

<span id="an_68:16">68:16</span> He aha koutou ka titiro titaha ai, e
nga maunga tiketike, ki te maunga i hiahiatia nei e te Atua kia nohoia e
ia? ae, ka nohoia e Ihowa ake ake.

<span id="an_68:17">68:17</span> Ko nga hariata a te Atua, e rua tekau
mano, mano mano iho; kei roto i a ratou te Ariki, me te mea ko Hinai, ko
te wahi tapu.

<span id="an_68:18">68:18</span> Kua kake koe ki runga, kua whakaraua e
koe te whakarau: kua riro i a koe he ohaoha mo te tangata; ae, mo te
hunga tutu ano, kia noho ai a Ihowa, te Atua ki a ratou.

<span id="an_68:19">68:19</span> Kia whakapaingia te Ariki, e whakawaha
nei i ta tatou pikaunga i tenei ra, i tenei ra, te Atua o to tatou
whakaoranga. (Hera.

<span id="an_68:20">68:20</span> Ko to tatou Atua te Atua o te
whakaoranga: na Ihowa ano, na te Ariki, nga putanga ake i te mate.

<span id="an_68:21">68:21</span> Ka maru ia i te Atua te matenga o ona
hoariri: me te tumuaki huruhuru o te tangata e haere tonu ana i ana
kino.

<span id="an_68:22">68:22</span> ¶ I mea te Ariki, Ka whakahokia mai e
ahau i Pahana, ka whakahokia mai e ahau taku iwi i nga rire o te moana:

<span id="an_68:23">68:23</span> Kia toua ai tou waewae ki te toto, kia
whiwhi ai te arero o au kuri ki tana wahi o ou hoariri.

<span id="an_68:24">68:24</span> I kite ratou, e te Atua, i ou haerenga,
i nga haerenga o toku Atua, o toku Kingi, i te wahi tapu.

<span id="an_68:25">68:25</span> Ko nga kaiwaiata i haere i mua, i muri
ko nga kaiwhakatangi, i waenganui o nga kotiro e patupatu ana i nga
timipera.

<span id="an_68:26">68:26</span> Whakapaingia te Atua i roto i nga
whakaminenga, te Ariki hoki, e nga mea i puta mai i te matapuna o
Iharaira.

<span id="an_68:27">68:27</span> Kei reira a Pineamine, te whakaotinga,
to ratou ariki, nga rangatira o Hura, me to ratou ropu, nga rangatira o
Hepurona, me nga rangatira o Napatari.

<span id="an_68:28">68:28</span> Kua oti he kaha mou te whakahau iho e
tou Atua: whakaukia, e te Atua, tau i mea ai mo matou.

<span id="an_68:29">68:29</span> Ka maua mai e nga kingi he hakari ki a
koe, mo tou temepara i Hiruharama.

<span id="an_68:30">68:30</span> Riria te kirehe o nga kakaho, te huinga
puru, me nga kuao kau a nga iwi, me te takahi i nga pihi hiriwa ki raro:
whakamararatia nga iwi e ahuareka ana ki te whainga.

<span id="an_68:31">68:31</span> E puta mai nga rangatira i Ihipa: meake
hohoro te totoro o nga ringa o Etiopia ki te Atua.

<span id="an_68:32">68:32</span> ¶ Waiata ki te Atua, e nga
rangatiratanga o te whenua: himene ki te Ariki: (Hera.

<span id="an_68:33">68:33</span> Ki a ia, ko tona hariata nei ko nga
rangi o nga rangi, nonamata: na, ka puaki tona reo, he reo kaha.

<span id="an_68:34">68:34</span> Waiho te kaha i te Atua, kei runga nei
i a Iharaira tana mahi rangatira: kei nga kapua hoki tona kaha.

<span id="an_68:35">68:35</span> Ka wehingia koe, e te Atua, i roto i ou
wahi tapu: ko te Atua o Iharaira te kaihomai i te kaha, i te mana, ki
tona iwi. Whakapaingia te Atua.

<span id="an_69:1">69:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Hohanimi. Na
Rawiri. Whakaorangia ahau e te Atua, ka tae mai hoki nga wai ki roto ki
toku wairua.

<span id="an_69:2">69:2</span> Ka tapoko ahau ki te oru hohonu, ki te
wahi kahore nei he tunga: kua tae ahau ki nga wai hohonu, ngaro iho ahau
i nga waipuke.

<span id="an_69:3">69:3</span> Kua ruwha ahau i taku tangi; kua maroke
toku korokoro: pakoko kau oku kanohi i ahau e tatari nei ki toku Atua.

<span id="an_69:4">69:4</span> Tini ke i nga makawe o toku matenga te
hunga e kino noa ana ki ahau: he kaha rawa te hunga e mauahara noa ana
ki ahau, e mea nei kia whakamatea ahau; utua ana e ahau i reira nga mea
kihai i tangohia e ahau.

<span id="an_69:5">69:5</span> E te Atua, e matau ana koe ki toku
kuware; kahore hoki oku he e ngaro i a koe.

<span id="an_69:6">69:6</span> E te Ariki, e Ihowa o nga mano kaua te
hunga e tatari ana ki a koe e whakama i ahau: e te Atua o Iharaira, kei
numinumi kau i ahau te hunga e rapu ana i a koe.

<span id="an_69:7">69:7</span> Mou hoki ahau i waiho ai hei tawainga:
ngaro iho toku mata i te whakama.

<span id="an_69:8">69:8</span> He tangata ke ahau ki oku hoa ake: hei
tautangata ki nga tama a toku whaea.

<span id="an_69:9">69:9</span> Ka pau hoki ahau i te aroha ki tou whare:
kua tau ano ki ahau nga tawai a te hunga e tawai ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_69:10">69:10</span> I ahau i tangi, i whakatiki hei whiu i
toku wairua, ka waiho tena hei tawainga moku.

<span id="an_69:11">69:11</span> I kakahu hoki ahau i te kakahu taratara
moku, a i waiho hei whakatauki ma ratou.

<span id="an_69:12">69:12</span> Kei te korero kino moku te hunga e noho
ana i te kuwaha: waiatatia ana ahau e te hunga haurangi waina.

<span id="an_69:13">69:13</span> ¶ Ko ahau ia, ki a koe taku inoi, e
Ihowa, i te wa e manakohia ai: whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e te
Atua, i runga i te nui o tou aroha, o te pono o tau whakaoranga.

<span id="an_69:14">69:14</span> Whakaorangia ahau i roto i te oru, kei
toremi: kia ora ahau i te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, i nga wai hohonu ano
hoki.

<span id="an_69:15">69:15</span> Kei ngaro ahau i te waipuke, kei
horomia e te rire; kei kopia ano te waha o te poka ki runga ki ahau.

<span id="an_69:16">69:16</span> E Ihowa whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau;
he pai hoki tou atawhai: tahuri mai ki ahau, kia rite ki te nui o au
arohatanga.

<span id="an_69:17">69:17</span> A kaua e huna tou mata ki tau pononga;
e pouri ana hoki ahau: hohoro te whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau.

<span id="an_69:18">69:18</span> Whakatata mai ki toku wairua, hokona:
whakaorangia ahau, e mahi nei oku hoariri.

<span id="an_69:19">69:19</span> E matau ana koe ki toku tawainga, ki
toku whakama, ki toku numinumi: kei tou aroaro oku hoariri katoa.

<span id="an_69:20">69:20</span> Maru noa toku ngakau i te tawai; a ki
tonu ahau i te pouri: i titiro ahau ki tetahi hei aroha mai, a kore ake;
ki etahi hei whakamarie, a kihai i kitea.

<span id="an_69:21">69:21</span> I homai he au hei kai maku: i toku
matewaitanga ano i whakainumia ahau ki te winika.

<span id="an_69:22">69:22</span> ¶ Kia meinga ta ratou tepu i to ratou
aroaro hei mahanga; hei rore hoki i to ratou wa rangimarie.

<span id="an_69:23">69:23</span> Kia whakapouritia o ratou kanohi, kei
kite ratou: kia wiri tonu hoki o ratou hope.

<span id="an_69:24">69:24</span> Ringihia atu tou riri ki runga ki a
ratou, kia mau hoki ratou i tou arita, i tou weriweri.

<span id="an_69:25">69:25</span> Kia ururuatia to ratou nohoanga: kaua
tetahi e noho ki o ratou teneti.

<span id="an_69:26">69:26</span> Mo ratou i tukino i te tangata i whiua
nei e koe; a korerotia ana e ratou te pouri o te hunga i werohia e koe.

<span id="an_69:27">69:27</span> Tapiritia he kino ki runga ki to ratou
kino; kaua hoki ratou e tukua kia tomo ki tou tika.

<span id="an_69:28">69:28</span> Kia murua atu ratou i te pukapuka o te
ora, kaua ano e tuhituhia ki roto ki te hunga tika.

<span id="an_69:29">69:29</span> Ko ahau ia, he rawakore, he pouri; kia
whakateiteitia ake ahau, e te Atua, e tau whakaoranga.

<span id="an_69:30">69:30</span> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti taku waiata ki te
ingoa o te Atua, ka whakanui ano taku whakawhetai i a ia.

<span id="an_69:31">69:31</span> Pai rawa tenei ki a Ihowa i te puru i
te kau, i te mea whai haona, whai maikuku.

<span id="an_69:32">69:32</span> Kua kite te hunga mahaki, kua hari: ka
ora ano o koutou ngakau, e te hunga e rapu nei i te Atua.

<span id="an_69:33">69:33</span> No te mea ka rongo a Ihowa ki nga
rawakore, e kore ano e whakahawea ki ana herehere.

<span id="an_69:34">69:34</span> Kia whakamoemiti te rangi me te whenua
ki a ia, nga moana, me nga mea katoa e tere ana i roto.

<span id="an_69:35">69:35</span> No te mea tera e whakaorangia e te Atua
a Hiona, ka hanga ano e ia nga pa o Hura; a ka noho ratou ki reira, ka
riro hoki a reira i a ratou.

<span id="an_69:36">69:36</span> A ka nohoia a reira e nga uri o ana
pononga: hei kainga tupu ano a reira mo te hunga e aroha ana ki tona
ingoa.

<span id="an_70:1">70:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Na Rawiri,
hei whakamahara. Kia hohoro, e te Atua, ki te whakaora i ahau: e Ihowa,
hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.

<span id="an_70:2">70:2</span> Kia whakama, kia pororaru ngatahi te
hunga e rapu ana i toku wairua: kia whakahokia ki muri, kia whakama te
hunga e hiahia ana kia he ahau.

<span id="an_70:3">70:3</span> Kia whakahokia ki muri mo to ratou
whakama, te hunga e mea ana ki ahau, Ha, ha.

<span id="an_70:4">70:4</span> Kia hari, kia koa, ki a koe te hunga
katoa e rapu ana i a koe; kia mea tonu te hunga e pai ana ki tau
whakaoranga, Kia whakanuia te Atua.

<span id="an_70:5">70:5</span> Ko ahau ia, he iti, he rawakore; hohoro
mai, e te Atua, ki ahau: ko koe toku awhina, toku kaiwhakaora; kaua ra e
whakaroa, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_71:1">71:1</span> ¶ Ko koe taku e whakawhirinaki ai, e
Ihowa: kei whakama ahau ake ake.

<span id="an_71:2">71:2</span> Whakaorangia ahau, i runga i tou tika,
kia mawhiti ano ahau: tahuri mai tou taringa ki ahau, whakaorangia hoki
ahau.

<span id="an_71:3">71:3</span> Kia ai koe hei teko e noho ai ahau, hei
hokihokinga tonutanga atu moku: kua kiia iho ahau e koe kia
whakaorangia: ko koe nei hoki toku kohatu, toku pourewa.

<span id="an_71:4">71:4</span> Whakaorangia ahau, e toku Atua, i te
ringa o te tangata kino, i te ringa o te whanoke, o te nanakia.

<span id="an_71:5">71:5</span> Ko koe nei hoki, e te Ariki, e Ihowa,
taku e tumanako atu nei, taku e whakawhirinaki nei no toku tamarikitanga
ake ano.

<span id="an_71:6">71:6</span> Nau ahau i tautoko ake no te kopu mai
ano; nau ahau i tango mai i roto i nga whekau o toku whaea; ko koe taku
e whakamoemiti tonu ai.

<span id="an_71:7">71:7</span> He miharotanga ahau na te tini; ko koe ia
toku piringa kaha.

<span id="an_71:8">71:8</span> Kia ki toku mangai i te whakamoemiti ki a
koe, i tou honore i te roa o te ra.

<span id="an_71:9">71:9</span> Kaua ahau e panga a te wa o te
koroheketanga, kaua ahau e whakarerea ina hemo toku kaha.

<span id="an_71:10">71:10</span> E korerotia ana hoki ahau e oku
hoariri, a e runanga tahi ana te hunga e whanga ana ki toku wairua.

<span id="an_71:11">71:11</span> E mea ana, Kua whakarerea ia e te Atua:
whaia, hopukia; kahore hoki tetahi hei whakaora.

<span id="an_71:12">71:12</span> E te Atua, kei matara atu koe i ahau: e
toku Atua, hohoro ki te awhina i ahau.

<span id="an_71:13">71:13</span> Kia whakama, kia pau nga hoariri o toku
wairua: kia hipokina ki te tawai, ki te whakama, te hunga e rapu ana i
te he moku.

<span id="an_71:14">71:14</span> ¶ Ko ahau ia, ka tumanako tonu: ka hono
tonu ano te whakamoemiti ki a koe.

<span id="an_71:15">71:15</span> Ma toku mangai e whakakite tou tika,
tau whakaoranga i te roa o te ra; kahore hoki ahau e mohio e hia ranei.

<span id="an_71:16">71:16</span> Ka haere ahau i runga i te kaha o te
Ariki, o Ihowa, ka whakahuatia e ahau tou tika, tou anake.

<span id="an_71:17">71:17</span> E te Atua, he mea whakaako ahau nau, no
toku tamarikitanga ake; a he whakapuaki taku i au mahi whakamiharo a
mohoa noa nei.

<span id="an_71:18">71:18</span> Na kaua ahau e whakarerea, e te Atua, a
koroheke noa, hina noa ahau, kia whakakitea ra ano e ahau tou kaha ki
tenei whakatupuranga, tou nui ki nga tangata katoa e puta mai a mua.

<span id="an_71:19">71:19</span> Kei runga rawa ano tou tika, e te Atua,
he nui nei hoki au mahi: e te Atua, ko wai te rite ki a koe?

<span id="an_71:20">71:20</span> He nui, he kino nga pouritanga ngakau i
whakakitea mai e koe ki a matou; tera ano koe ka whakahauora i a matou,
ka whakahoki ake ano i a matou i nga wahi hohonu o te whenua.

<span id="an_71:21">71:21</span> Whakaraneatia e koe toku nui, a tahuri
mai ano ka whakamarie i ahau.

<span id="an_71:22">71:22</span> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe i runga i
te hatere, ara ki tou pono, e toku Atua: ka himene ahau ki a koe i runga
i te hapa, e te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.

<span id="an_71:23">71:23</span> Ka tino hari oku ngutu ua himene ahau
ki a koe: me toku wairua ano i hokona nei e koe.

<span id="an_71:24">71:24</span> Ka korerotia hoki e toku arero tou tika
i te roa o te ra: kua whakama nei hoki, kua numinumi kau te hunga i rapu
i te he moku.

<span id="an_72:1">72:1</span> ¶ Na Horomona. Homai, e te Atua, au
whakaritenga ki te kingi, me tou tika ki te tama a te kingi.

<span id="an_72:2">72:2</span> ¶ Mana e whakawa tou iwi i runga i te
tika, au rawakore i runga i te whakawa tika.

<span id="an_72:3">72:3</span> Ka kawea mai e nga maunga te rongo mau ki
te iwi, e nga pukepuke i runga i te tika.

<span id="an_72:4">72:4</span> Ka whakawa ia mo nga ware o te iwi: ka
whakaorangia e ia nga tamariki a te rawakore; mongamonga noa i a ia te
kaitukino.

<span id="an_72:5">72:5</span> I te ra e mau ana, i te marama hoki, ka
pera te mau o to ratou wehi ki a koe i nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_72:6">72:6</span> E heke iho ia ano he ua ki runga ki te
kotinga tarutaru, me nga ua e whakamakuku nei i te whenua.

<span id="an_72:7">72:7</span> Ka tupu te tangata tika i ona ra: tona
roa ano o te ata noho, a kore noa te marama.

<span id="an_72:8">72:8</span> Ka kingi ia i tenei moana, a tae noa ki
tetahi moana, i te awa, a nga pito atu ano o te whenua.

<span id="an_72:9">72:9</span> Ka piko ki tona aroaro te hunga o te
koraha: a ka mitimiti ona hoariri i te puehu.

<span id="an_72:10">72:10</span> Ka maua mai he hakari e nga kingi o
Tarahihi, o nga motu: ka kawea mai he tahua e nga kingi o Hepa, o Tepa.

<span id="an_72:11">72:11</span> Ae, ka koropiko nga kingi katoa ki a
ia: ka mahi nga iwi katoa ki a ia.

<span id="an_72:12">72:12</span> Ka ora hoki i a ia te rawakore ua tangi
atu, te ware hoki me te tangata kahore nei ona kaiawhina.

<span id="an_72:13">72:13</span> E tohu ia i te tangata iti, i te
rawakore; ka ora ano i a ia nga wairua o nga rawakore.

<span id="an_72:14">72:14</span> Ka hokona e ia to ratou wairua i roto i
te tukino, i te tutu, he mea utu nui hoki o ratou toto ki tana titiro.

<span id="an_72:15">72:15</span> A e ora ratou; ka hoatu ano ki a ia he
koura no Hepa: ka tukua tonutia hoki te inoi mona; ka whakapaingia ia i
tenei ra, i tenei ra.

<span id="an_72:16">72:16</span> He kutanga witi tera i runga i te
whenua, i te tihi o nga maunga; ngarue ana ona hua, ano ko Repanona, a
ka rite te tupu o nga tangata o te pa ki to te tarutaru o te whenua.

<span id="an_72:17">72:17</span> Ka mau tonu tona ingoa ake ake; ka rite
tona ingoa ki te ra te pumau: kei roto i a ia te manaaki mo te tangata;
ka korerotia tona koa e nga iwi katoa.

<span id="an_72:18">72:18</span> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua, te
Atua o Iharaira: ko ia nei anake hei mahi i nga mahi whakamiharo;

<span id="an_72:19">72:19</span> Kia whakapaingia ano tona ingoa kororia
mo ake tonu atu; kia ki katoa hoki te whenua i tona kororia. Amine, ae
Amine.

<span id="an_72:20">72:20</span> Ko te mutunga tenei o nga inoi a
Rawiri, a te tama a Hehe.

<span id="an_73:1">73:1</span> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. He pono, he pai te
Atua ki a Iharaira; ki te hunga ngakau ma.

<span id="an_73:2">73:2</span> Ko ahau ia, wahi iti kua tapepa oku
waewae: me i kotahi kua paheke oku takahanga.

<span id="an_73:3">73:3</span> I hae hoki ahau ki te hunga whakahi, i
toku kitenga i te tangata hara e kake ana.

<span id="an_73:4">73:4</span> Kahore hoki he whakawiringa a te mate i a
ratou: he maro ano o ratou uaua.

<span id="an_73:5">73:5</span> Kahore nga mea whakapouri tangata e pa ki
a ratou; kahore ano ratou e whiua tahitia me te mano tangata.

<span id="an_73:6">73:6</span> Na reira, ano he hei te whakakake e awhi
nei i a ratou, ano he kakahu te tutu e hipokina nei ratou.

<span id="an_73:7">73:7</span> Pupuhi ana o ratou kanohi i te ngako: nui
ake nga mea i a ratou i a o ratou ngakau i hiahia ai.

<span id="an_73:8">73:8</span> E whakahi ana ratou, e korero kino ana mo
te whakatoi: kei runga noa ake a ratou korero.

<span id="an_73:9">73:9</span> Tutuki tonu to ratou mangai ki nga rangi:
e kopikopiko ana hoki to ratou arero i runga i te whenua.

<span id="an_73:10">73:10</span> Koia tona iwi i hoki mai ai ki konei: a
e whakawiria ana he wai mo ratou, ki tonu te kapu.

<span id="an_73:11">73:11</span> E mea ana ratou, Ma te aha e matau ai
te Atua? He matauranga koia to te Runga Rawa?

<span id="an_73:12">73:12</span> Nana, ko te hunga kino tenei, kei runga
tonu i te whenua rangatira, e hua ana o ratou taonga.

<span id="an_73:13">73:13</span> He pono he maumau taku mea i toku
ngakau kia ma, taku horoi hoki i oku ringa ki te harakore.

<span id="an_73:14">73:14</span> E whiua ana hoki ahau i te roa o te ra,
e pakia ana i nga ata katoa.

<span id="an_73:15">73:15</span> ¶ Me i ki ahau, Ka penei taku korero;
na e tinihanga ana ahau ki te whakatupuranga o au tamariki.

<span id="an_73:16">73:16</span> I taku meatanga kia matauria tenei, ka
kite ahau he mahi whakauaua rawa;

<span id="an_73:17">73:17</span> Tae noa ahau ki te wahi tapu o te Atua,
katahi ahau ka mohio ki to ratou mutunga.

<span id="an_73:18">73:18</span> He pono i whakaturia ratou e koe ki nga
wahi pahekeheke; a whakataka ana e koe ki te ngaromanga.

<span id="an_73:19">73:19</span> Ano te panga whakareretanga o to ratou
hunanga! kua pau rawa i nga wehi.

<span id="an_73:20">73:20</span> Ka rite ki te rekanga kanohi, ina ara
ake te tangata, tau whakahawea ki to ratou ahua, e te Ariki, ina ara ake
koe.

<span id="an_73:21">73:21</span> ¶ Na mamae noa iho toku ngakau, a
hukihuki ana oku whatumanawa.

<span id="an_73:22">73:22</span> He whakaarokore hoki ahau, he kuware:
me te mea he kirehe ahau i tou aroaro.

<span id="an_73:23">73:23</span> Ahakoa ra kei a koe tonu ahau; e
puritia ana e koe toku ringa matau.

<span id="an_73:24">73:24</span> Ma tou whakaaro ahau e arahi; muri iho
ka riro ahau i a koe ki te kororia.

<span id="an_73:25">73:25</span> Ko wai hoki toku i te rangi ko koe
anake? Kahore atu hoki oku i te whenua e hiahia ai, ko koe anake.

<span id="an_73:26">73:26</span> Hemo iho oku kikokiko me toku ngakau:
ko te Atua ia te kaha o toku ngakau, toku wahi ake ake.

<span id="an_73:27">73:27</span> Na, ko te hunga e mamao atu ana i a koe
ka mate: ka ngaro i a koe te hunga puremu katoa e whakarere nei i a koe.

<span id="an_73:28">73:28</span> Ko ahau ia, he pai ki ahau te whakatata
ki te Atua: kua waiho e ahau te Ariki, a Ihowa, hei whakawhirinakitanga
moku, kia whakapuakina ai e ahau au mahi katoa.

<span id="an_74:1">74:1</span> ¶ He Makiri na Ahapa. E te Atua, he aha i
panga ai matou e koe ake ake? He aha i pongere ai tou riri ki nga hipi o
tau mara?

<span id="an_74:2">74:2</span> Mahara ki tau whakaminenga i hokona e koe
i mua, i utua e koe hei iwi mo tou kainga tupu; a ki tenei Maunga Hiona
i nohoia nei e koe.

<span id="an_74:3">74:3</span> Hiki ake ou waewae ki nga whakangaromanga
e mau tonu nei, ki nga mahi kino katoa a te hoariri ki te wahi tapu.

<span id="an_74:4">74:4</span> Kua hamama nei ou hoariri i waenganui i
au whakaminenga, kua whakaturia e ratou a ratou kara hei tohu.

<span id="an_74:5">74:5</span> E rite ana ratou ki nga tangata e hapai
ana i te titaha ki te puia rakau.

<span id="an_74:6">74:6</span> Inaianei ia e tukitukia ana e ratou ona
mea whakairo, pakaruhia iho ana ki te titaha, ki te hama.

<span id="an_74:7">74:7</span> Kua toua tou wahi tapu ki te kapura, kua
noa i a ratou te nohoanga o tou ingoa, kei te whenua e takoto ana.

<span id="an_74:8">74:8</span> I mea to ratou ngakau, Me whakangaro
ratou a poto ake: kua tahuna e ratou nga whare huihui katoa o te Atua i
te whenua.

<span id="an_74:9">74:9</span> Kahore matou e kite i o matou tohu,
kahore atu he poropiti, kahore hoki tetahi o matou e matau ana kia pehea
ake te roa.

<span id="an_74:10">74:10</span> E te Atua, kia pehea ake te roa o te
tawai a te hoariri? Ka kohukohu tonu ranei te hoariri ki tou ingoa ake
ake?

<span id="an_74:11">74:11</span> He aha i pepeke ai tou ringa, tou
matau? Unuhia i roto i tou uma, whakamotitia ratou.

<span id="an_74:12">74:12</span> ¶ Ko te Atua ia toku Kingi o tua iho, e
mahi whakaora ana i waenganui i te whenua.

<span id="an_74:13">74:13</span> Nau, na tou kaha i wawae te moana:
pakaru ana i a koe nga matenga o nga tarakona i nga wai.

<span id="an_74:14">74:14</span> Mongamonga noa i a koe nga matenga o
rewiatana: a hoatu ana ia e koe hei kai ma te iwi o te koraha.

<span id="an_74:15">74:15</span> I wahia e koe te puna me te roma;
mimiti ake i a koe nga awa nunui.

<span id="an_74:16">74:16</span> Nau te ao, nau hoki te po; nau i
whakarite te marama me te ra.

<span id="an_74:17">74:17</span> Nau i whakatu nga rohe katoa o te
whenua: te raumati me te hotoke, he mea whakarite ena nau.

<span id="an_74:18">74:18</span> ¶ Kia mahara ki tenei, kua tawai te
hoariri, e Ihowa: kua kohukohu te hunga poauau ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_74:19">74:19</span> Kaua e tukua te wairua o tau kukupa ki
te kirehe: kei wareware ake ake ki te whakaminenga o au rawakore.

<span id="an_74:20">74:20</span> Whakaaroa te kawenata; kua kiki hoki
nga wahi pouri o te whenua i nga nohoanga nanakia.

<span id="an_74:21">74:21</span> Kei hoki whakama mai te tangata e
tukinotia ana: kia whakamoemititia tou ingoa e te ware, e te rawakore.

<span id="an_74:22">74:22</span> E ara, e te Atua, tohea tau tohe:
mahara ki ta te tangata poauau tawai ki a koe a pau noa te ra.

<span id="an_74:23">74:23</span> Kei wareware ki te reo o ou hoariri: e
kake tonu ana te ngangau a te hunga e whakatika ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_75:1">75:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Aratakiti. He
himene, he waiata na Ahapa. Ka whakawhetai tonu matou ki a koe, e te
Atua; ka whakawhetai tonu matou, kei te tata mai hoki tou ingoa: e
korerotia ana e te tangata au mahi whakamiharo.
