<span id="an_75:2">75:2</span> Ka kitea e ahau te wa e rite ana, ka tika
taku whakawa.

<span id="an_75:3">75:3</span> Kuteretere noa iho te whenua me ona
tangata katoa; naku i whakatu ona pou. (Hera.

<span id="an_75:4">75:4</span> I mea ahau ki te hunga whakakake, Kati ra
te whakakake; ki te hunga hara ano, Kaua e whakaarahia te haona.

<span id="an_75:5">75:5</span> Kaua to koutou haona e whakaarahia ki
runga: kati te whakamaro i te kaki ina korero.

<span id="an_75:6">75:6</span> ¶ No te mea kahore he aranga i te
rawhiti, kahore i te hauauru, kahore hoki i te tonga.

<span id="an_75:7">75:7</span> Ko te Atua ia te kaiwhakawa; ko tenei e
whakaititia iho ana e ia, ko tera e whakaarahia ake ana.

<span id="an_75:8">75:8</span> Kei te ringa hoki o Ihowa he kapu, pahuka
tonu te waina; ki tonu, whakananu rawa, hei ringihanga mana: ko nga
nganga ia, ma te hunga kino katoa o te whenua e tatau, e inu.

<span id="an_75:9">75:9</span> Ko ahau ia, ka kauwhau tonu: ka himene ki
te Atua o Hakopa.

<span id="an_75:10">75:10</span> A ka kotia e ahau nga haona katoa o te
hunga kino: ka whakaarahia ake ia nga haona o te tangata tika.

<span id="an_76:1">76:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Nekinoto. He
himene, he waiata na Ahapa. E matauria ana te Atua i roto i a Hura, he
nui tona ingoa i roto i a Iharaira.

<span id="an_76:2">76:2</span> Kei Harema hoki tona tapenakara; kei
Hiona tona nohoanga.

<span id="an_76:3">76:3</span> I whati i a ia i reira nga pere o te
kopere, te whakangungu rakau, te hoari, me nga mea mo te whawhai. (Hera.

<span id="an_76:4">76:4</span> Tera atu tou kororia, tou nui, i to nga
maunga kirehe.

<span id="an_76:5">76:5</span> Kua pahuatia te hunga ngakau toa, moe ana
ratou i ta ratou moe; kihai ano i whai ringa tetahi o nga marohirohi.

<span id="an_76:6">76:6</span> Na tau whakatupehupehu, e te Atua o
Hakopa, i parangia ai te hariata me te hoiho e te moe.

<span id="an_76:7">76:7</span> ¶ Ko koe, ina, ko koe e wehingia; ko wai
hoki e tu ki tou aroaro ina riri koe?

<span id="an_76:8">76:8</span> Nau i rangona iho ai te whakawa i te
rangi: wehi ana te whenua, whakaririka kau ana,

<span id="an_76:9">76:9</span> I te aranga ake o te Atua ki te whakawa,
ki te whakaora i te hunga mahaki katoa o te whenua. (Hera.

<span id="an_76:10">76:10</span> He pono ka whai kororia koe i te riri o
te tangata: mau ano e whitiki te toenga o te riri.

<span id="an_76:11">76:11</span> Whakapuakina te kupu taurangi ki a
Ihowa, ki to koutou Atua, whakamana hoki; e te hunga katoa i tetahi taha
ona, i tetahi taha, mauria he hakari ki a ia, ka tika hoki te wehi ki a
ia.

<span id="an_76:12">76:12</span> Mana e poro atu te wairua o nga
rangatira: e matakuria ana ia e nga kingi o te whenua.

<span id="an_77:1">77:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi, ki a
Ierutunu. He himene na Ahapa. Ki te Atua toku reo, e karanga nei ahau,
ki te Atua toku reo, a tera e tahuri mai tona taringa ki ahau.

<span id="an_77:2">77:2</span> I rapu ahau ki te Ariki i te ra o toku
pouri: maro tonu toku ringa i te po, kihai ano i pepeke; kihai toku
wairua i pai kia whakamarietia.

<span id="an_77:3">77:3</span> E mahara ana ahau ki te Atua, a e pouri
ana: kei te whakaaroaro, a ngaro iho toku wairua. (Hera.

<span id="an_77:4">77:4</span> E puritia ana e koe oku kanohi kia
mataara tonu; he pouri ahau, te ahei te korero.

<span id="an_77:5">77:5</span> Ka hoki oku whakaaro ki nga ra onamata,
ki nga tau o tua iho.

<span id="an_77:6">77:6</span> E whakamahara ana ahau ki taku waiata i
te po, e korerorero ana ki toku ngakau e rapurapu ana toku wairua.

<span id="an_77:7">77:7</span> Tera ranei te Ariki e panga tonu ake ake?
A heoi ano ranei ana manakohanga mai?

<span id="an_77:8">77:8</span> Kua kahore ranei tana mahi tohu mo ake
tonu atu? Kua whati ranei tana kupu a ake ake?

<span id="an_77:9">77:9</span> Kua wareware ranei te Atua ki te atawhai?
Kua riri ranei ia, a tutakina atu ana e ia tona aroha? (Hera.

<span id="an_77:10">77:10</span> Na ka mea ahau, Ko toku ngoikore tenei:
otira ka mahara ahau ki nga tau o te ringa matau o te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_77:11">77:11</span> ¶ Ka mahara ahau ki nga mahi a Ihowa;
ae ra, ka mahara ahau ki au mea whakamiharo o tua iho.

<span id="an_77:12">77:12</span> Ka whakaaro hoki ahau ki au meatanga
katoa, ka purakau ki au mahi.

<span id="an_77:13">77:13</span> E te Atua, kei te wahi tapu tou ara: ko
wai te atua nui hei rite ki te Atua?

<span id="an_77:14">77:14</span> Ko koe te Atua e mahi nei i nga mea
whakamiharo: kua whakapuakina e koe tou kaha i waenganui o nga iwi.

<span id="an_77:15">77:15</span> Hokona ana e tou ringa tau iwi, nga
tama a Hakopa raua ko Hohepa. (Hera.

<span id="an_77:16">77:16</span> I kite nga wai i a koe, e te Atua i
kite nga wai i a koe, mataku ana: i oho ano nga rire.

<span id="an_77:17">77:17</span> Ringihia ana he wai e nga kapua, puaki
ana te haruru o nga rangi: rererere ana au pere.

<span id="an_77:18">77:18</span> I roto i te awhiowhio te haruru o tau
whatitiri: marama noa te ao i nga uira; wiri ana te whenua, oioi ana.

<span id="an_77:19">77:19</span> I te moana tou ara, i nga wai nui tou
huarahi, e kore ano e kitea ou takahanga.

<span id="an_77:20">77:20</span> He mea arahi e koe tau iwi ano he
kahui, ara e te ringa o Mohi raua ko Arona.

<span id="an_78:1">78:1</span> ¶ He Makiri na Ahapa. Kia anga mai te
taringa, e toku iwi, ki taku ture: tahuri mai o koutou taringa ki nga
kupu a toku mangai.

<span id="an_78:2">78:2</span> Ka puaki te kupu whakarite i toku mangai,
ka korerotia e ahau nga mea ngaro onamata:

<span id="an_78:3">78:3</span> I rongo nei, i matau nei tatou, i korero
ai hoki o tatou matua ki a tatou.

<span id="an_78:4">78:4</span> E kore e huna e matou i a ratou tamariki:
me whakaatu ki to muri whakatupuranga nga whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa, me
tona kaha, me ana mahi whakamiharo i mea ai ia.

<span id="an_78:5">78:5</span> Kua pumau hoki i a ia he whakaaturanga i
roto i a Hakopa, kua takoto he ture i roto i a Iharaira: a whakahaua mai
ana e ia o tatou tupuna, kia whakaakona ki a ratou tamariki.

<span id="an_78:6">78:6</span> Kia matauria ai e to muri whakatupuranga,
e nga tamariki e whanau, e ara ake a mua: mo ta ratou whakaatu ki a
ratou tamariki.

<span id="an_78:7">78:7</span> Kia u ai ta ratou tumanako ki te Atua,
kei wareware hoki ki nga mahi a te Atua: engari kia mau ki ana whakahau.

<span id="an_78:8">78:8</span> Kei rite hoki ki o ratou tupuna, ki te
whakatupuranga whakakeke, tutu, ki te whakatupuranga kihai nei i
whakatikatika i to ratou ngakau, kihai hoki i u to ratou wairua ki te
Atua.

<span id="an_78:9">78:9</span> ¶ He hunga mau patu nga tama a Eparaima,
he hunga hapai kopere, heoi tahuri ana ratou i te ra o te tatauranga.

<span id="an_78:10">78:10</span> Kihai i puritia e ratou te kawenata a
te Atua; kihai ano i pai ki te haere i tana ture;

<span id="an_78:11">78:11</span> Heoi, kua wareware ki ana mahi, me ana
mea whakamiharo i whakakitea e ia ki a ratou.

<span id="an_78:12">78:12</span> He mea whakamiharo ana mahi i te aroaro
o o ratou tupuna, i te whenua o Ihipa, i te parae o Toana.

<span id="an_78:13">78:13</span> Tapahia ana e ia te moana, a meinga ana
ratou kia whiti: tu ake i a ia nga wai ano he puranga.

<span id="an_78:14">78:14</span> He mea arahi ratou e ia i te awatea ki
te kapua: i te roa hoki o te po ki te marama o te ahi.

<span id="an_78:15">78:15</span> I wahia e ia nga kohatu i te koraha; a
me te mea no nga rire nui tana wai hei inu ma ratou.

<span id="an_78:16">78:16</span> Puta mai ana i a ia he awa i roto i te
kamaka: meinga ana nga wai kia heke, ano he waipuke.

<span id="an_78:17">78:17</span> Heoi ka hara ano ratou ki a ia:
whakatoi ana ki te Runga Rawa i te koraha.

<span id="an_78:18">78:18</span> Na kei te whakamatautau to ratou ngakau
i te Atua, kei te inoi kai ma to ratou hiahia.

<span id="an_78:19">78:19</span> I korero kino ano ratou ki te Atua, i
mea; E ahei ranei i te Atua te taka he tepu ki te koraha?

<span id="an_78:20">78:20</span> Nana, ko tana patunga i te kohatu, ka
pakaru mai te wai, a puke ana nga awa: e taea ano ranei e ia te homai
taro, e pae ranei i a ia he kikokiko ma tana iwi?

<span id="an_78:21">78:21</span> Na ko te rongonga o Ihowa, na ka riri:
a toro ana te kapura ki a Hakopa, puta ake ana te riri ki a Iharaira;

<span id="an_78:22">78:22</span> Mo ratou kihai i whakapono ki te Atua,
kihai ano i whakawhirinaki ki tana whakaoranga.

<span id="an_78:23">78:23</span> Nana nei hoki i whakahau nga kapua i
runga, i whakatuwhera nga tatau o te rangi.

<span id="an_78:24">78:24</span> A whakauaina iho te mana ki runga ki a
ratou hei kai; homai ana hoki e ia te witi o te rangi ma ratou.

<span id="an_78:25">78:25</span> Kai ana te tangata i ta te anahera kai:
i tukua e ia he kai ma ratou, a makona noa.

<span id="an_78:26">78:26</span> I whakaohokia e ia te marangai i te
rangi: i takina ano te tonga e tona kaha.

<span id="an_78:27">78:27</span> A whakauaina iho e ia te kikokiko ki a
ratou ano he puehu; he manu whai pakau ano he one no te moana.

<span id="an_78:28">78:28</span> A whakangahorotia iho e ia ki waenganui
i to ratou puni: ki o ratou nohoanga a tawhio noa.

<span id="an_78:29">78:29</span> Na kai ana ratou, tino makona; i tukua
hoki e ia ki a ratou ta ratou i hiahia ai:

<span id="an_78:30">78:30</span> Kihai ratou i ngaruru ki ta ratou i
hiahia ai; a i roto tonu ta ratou kai i o ratou mangai,

<span id="an_78:31">78:31</span> Na ka pa te riri o te Atua ki a ratou,
a patua iho e ia te hunga tetere o ratou; piko ana i a ia nga
taitamariki o Iharaira.

<span id="an_78:32">78:32</span> Ahakoa pa katoa tenei, i hara ano
ratou, kihai ano i whakapono ki ana mahi whakamiharo.

<span id="an_78:33">78:33</span> I whakapaua ai e ia o ratou ra ki te
horihori, o ratou tau ki te potatutatu.

<span id="an_78:34">78:34</span> Ka patua ratou e ia, na, ka rapu ratou
i a ia, a ka hoki, ka ui wawe ki te Atua.

<span id="an_78:35">78:35</span> Ka mahara hoki ko te Atua to ratou
kohatu, ko te Atua, ko te Runga Rawa, to ratou kaihoko.

<span id="an_78:36">78:36</span> Otiia kei te patipati o ratou mangai ki
a ia, a teka ana o ratou arero ki a ia.

<span id="an_78:37">78:37</span> Kihai hoki to ratou ngakau i tika ki a
ia; kihai ano ratou i u ki tana kawenata.

<span id="an_78:38">78:38</span> Ko tana ia, he aroha; hipokina ana e ia
te he, kihai ano i whakangaro: ae ra, he maha ana whakahokinga iho i
tona riri, a kihai i oho katoa tona riri.

<span id="an_78:39">78:39</span> I mahara hoki ia he kikokiko nei ratou:
he hau e pahure atu ana, a e kore e hoki mai.

<span id="an_78:40">78:40</span> ¶ Ano te tini o a ratou whakatoinga i a
ia i te koraha, o a ratou whakapouritanga i a ia i te tahora!

<span id="an_78:41">78:41</span> Hoki whakamuri ana ratou, whakamatautau
ana i te Atua: whakatoia ana e ratou te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.

<span id="an_78:42">78:42</span> Kihai ratou i mahara ki tona ringa, ki
te ra i whakaorangia ai ratou e ia i te hoariri;

<span id="an_78:43">78:43</span> Ki tana meatanga i ana tohu ki Ihipa, i
ana merekara ki te parae o Toana;

<span id="an_78:44">78:44</span> I puta ke ai i a ia o ratou awa hei
toto, me o ratou manga wai, te inu ai ratou.

<span id="an_78:45">78:45</span> I tonoa ai e ia he huihuinga namu ki a
ratou, a pau iho ratou; he poroka, i huna ai ratou.

<span id="an_78:46">78:46</span> A hoatu ana e ia o ratou hua ki te
moka; me to ratou mauiui ki te mawhitiwhiti.

<span id="an_78:47">78:47</span> Whakamatea ana e ia a ratou waina ki te
whatu, a ratou rakau hikamora ki te haupapa.

<span id="an_78:48">78:48</span> Tukua ana e ia a ratou kararehe ma te
whatu, a ratou kahui ma nga uira.

<span id="an_78:49">78:49</span> I tukua whakareretia e ia ki a ratou
tona riri, aritarita, weriweri, me te raruraru; he whakaeke na nga
anahera kino.

<span id="an_78:50">78:50</span> A whakatikaia ana e ia he ara mo tona
riri; kihai i tohungia to ratou wairua kei mate: otiia tukua ana e ia to
ratou ora ki te mate uruta.

<span id="an_78:51">78:51</span> Na patua iho e ia nga matamua i Ihipa,
te muanga o to ratou kaha i nga teneti o Hama.

<span id="an_78:52">78:52</span> Otira arahina ana e ia ana ake tangata
ano he hipi; whakahaerea ana ratou e ia i te koraha ano he kahui.

<span id="an_78:53">78:53</span> Na ka arahina marietia ratou e ia, te
wehi ratou: ko o ratou hoariri ia taupokina iho e te moana.

<span id="an_78:54">78:54</span> Na ka kawea ratou e ia ki te rohe o
tona wahi tapu, ki tenei maunga, i hokona nei e tona matau.

<span id="an_78:55">78:55</span> Peia ana e ia nga tauiwi i to ratou
aroaro: a wehea ana e ia he kainga mo ratou ki te aho, whakanohoia iho
nga hapu o Iharaira ki o ratou teneti.

<span id="an_78:56">78:56</span> Heoi ka whakamatauria, ka whakatoia e
ratou te Atua, te Runga Rawa; kihai hoki i mau ki ana whakaaturanga;

<span id="an_78:57">78:57</span> A hoki whakamuri ana, mahi hianga ana,
pera ana me o ratou matua: parori ke ana ratou, he pera me te kopere
tinihanga.

<span id="an_78:58">78:58</span> Na ko o ratou wahi tiketike hei
whakapataritari i a ia; ko o ratou whakapakoko hei mea i a ia kia hae.

<span id="an_78:59">78:59</span> I te rongonga o te Atua, ka riri, ka
tino whakarihariha hoki ki a Iharaira.

<span id="an_78:60">78:60</span> A mahue ake i a ia te tapenakara a
Hiro, te teneti i whakaturia e ia ki waenganui i nga tangata;

<span id="an_78:61">78:61</span> A tukua ana e ia tona kaha hei
whakarau, tona kororia ki te ringa o te hoariri.

<span id="an_78:62">78:62</span> I tukua atu ano e ia tana iwi ma te
hoari; a i riri ki tona kainga tupu.

<span id="an_78:63">78:63</span> Pau ake a ratou taitama i te ahi; kihai
ano a ratou kotiro i marenatia.

<span id="an_78:64">78:64</span> I hinga o ratou tohunga i te hoari;
kihai hoki i tangi a ratou pouaru.

<span id="an_78:65">78:65</span> Na ka maranga te Ariki ano ko tetahi i
te moe, me te tangata kaha e hamama ana i te waina.

<span id="an_78:66">78:66</span> A patua iho e ia a muri o ona hoariri,
meinga ana ratou e ia hei taunutanga mo ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_78:67">78:67</span> I whakakahore ano ia ki te teneti a
Hohepa: a kihai i whiriwhiri i te hapu o Eparaima;

<span id="an_78:68">78:68</span> Heoi ko te hapu o Hura tana i
whiriwhiri ai, ko Maunga Hiona tana i aroha ai.

<span id="an_78:69">78:69</span> A whakaturia ana e ia tona wahi tapu
kia pera me nga wahi teitei; me te whenua i whakapumautia e ia mo ake
tonu atu.

<span id="an_78:70">78:70</span> I whiriwhiria ano e ia a Rawiri, tana
pononga: he mea tango nana i nga kainga hipi:

<span id="an_78:71">78:71</span> Mauria ana mai e ia i te whai i nga
hipi whaereere, hei whangai i a Hakopa, i tana iwi, i a Iharaira hoki, i
tona kainga tupu.

<span id="an_78:72">78:72</span> A rite tonu ki te tapatahi o tona
ngakau tana whangai i a ratou: he arahi mohio hoki ta tona ringa i a
ratou.

<span id="an_79:1">79:1</span> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. E te Atua, kua tae
mai nga tauiwi ki tou kainga tupu, kua noa i a ratou tou temepara tapu,
kua waiho a Hiruharama kia puranga kau ana.

<span id="an_79:2">79:2</span> Ko nga tinana mate o au pononga kua hoatu
e ratou hei kai ma nga manu o te rangi, ko te kikokiko o tau hunga tapu
ma nga kirehe o te whenua.

<span id="an_79:3">79:3</span> Ko o ratou toto, ringihia ake e ratou ano
he wai, ki nga taha o Hiruharama; kahore hoki he tangata hei tanu i a
ratou.

<span id="an_79:4">79:4</span> Kua waiho matou hei tawainga ma o matou
hoa, hei katanga ma te hunga i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha o matou.

<span id="an_79:5">79:5</span> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa? E riri tonu
ranei koe ake ake? E ngiha tonu ranei tou hae me he kapura?

<span id="an_79:6">79:6</span> ¶ Ringihia tou riri ki nga tauiwi kahore
nei e matau ki a koe, ki nga rangatiratanga kahore nei e karanga ki tou
ingoa.

<span id="an_79:7">79:7</span> Kua pau hoki a Hakopa i a ratou, kua
ururua i a ratou tona nohoanga.

<span id="an_79:8">79:8</span> Kaua ra e maharatia nga kino o o matou
tupuna; kia hohoro tou aroha ki mua i a matou; kua whakaititia rawatia
hoki matou.

<span id="an_79:9">79:9</span> Awhinatia matou, e te Atua o to matou
whakaoranga, kia whakakororiatia ai tou ingoa: whakaorangia matou,
hipokina hoki o matou hara, he mahara ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_79:10">79:10</span> Kia mea koia nga tauiwi, Kei hea to
ratou Atua? Kia kite atu matou e matau ana nga tauiwi ki te whakatakinga
i te toto o au pononga i whakahekea nei.

<span id="an_79:11">79:11</span> Kia tae atu ki tou aroaro te aue a te
herehere: kia rite ki te nui o tou kaha tau whakaora i te hunga e meatia
ana kia mate.

<span id="an_79:12">79:12</span> Takiwhitutia atu te utu e hoatu e koe
ki nga uma o o matou hoa mo ta ratou tawai, e tawai nei ratou ki a koe,
e te Ariki.

<span id="an_79:13">79:13</span> Penei ka whakawhetai matou, tau iwi,
nga hipi hoki e hepara nei koe, ki a koe ake ake: ka whakaitea e matou
te whakamoemiti ki a koe, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_80:1">80:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Hohanimi
Erutu. He himene na Ahapa. Tahuri mai tou taringa, e te Hepara o
Iharaira, e arahi nei i a Hohepa ano he kahui hipi; whiti mai koe e noho
mai na i waenganui i nga kerupima;

<span id="an_80:2">80:2</span> Whakaohoohokia tou kaha i te aroaro o
Eparaima, o Pineamine, o Manahi: a haere mai ki te whakaora i a matou.

<span id="an_80:3">80:3</span> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua: kia
marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.

<span id="an_80:4">80:4</span> E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, kia pehea
ake te roa o tou riri ki te inoi a tau iwi?

<span id="an_80:5">80:5</span> Kua whangaia mai e koe he roimata hei
taro ma ratou, he nui hoki te mehua roimata kua homai nei e koe kia
inumia e ratou.

<span id="an_80:6">80:6</span> Kua meinga matou e koe hei totohetanga ma
o matou hoa, a e kataina ana matou e o matou hoariri.

<span id="an_80:7">80:7</span> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua o nga
mano; kia marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.

<span id="an_80:8">80:8</span> ¶ I maua mai e koe he waina i Ihipa: ka
oti i a koe nga tauiwi te panga, na whakatokia iho e koe.

<span id="an_80:9">80:9</span> I whakapaia e koe he tunga mona, na, ka
hou ona pakiaka, a ka kapi te whenua.

<span id="an_80:10">80:10</span> Taumarumaru ana tona ata ki runga ki
nga pukepuke; ko ona manga rite tonu ki nga hita a te Atua.

<span id="an_80:11">80:11</span> I tautotoro atu ona manga ki te moana,
ona rara ki te awa.

<span id="an_80:12">80:12</span> He aha i pakaruhia ai e koe ona taiepa
ki raro, kia kowhakiwhakia ai ia e nga tangata katoa e tika ana i te
ara?

<span id="an_80:13">80:13</span> Mongamonga noa i te poaka toa o te
ngahere, e kainga ana e te kirehe mohoao o te parae.

<span id="an_80:14">80:14</span> Tahuri mai ano, e te Atua o nga mano, e
inoi atu nei matou: titiro iho i te rangi, kia kite mai koe, ka toro mai
i tenei waina.

<span id="an_80:15">80:15</span> I te rakau i whakatokia e tou matau, i
te manga hoki i meinga e koe kia pakari mau.

<span id="an_80:16">80:16</span> Kua pau i te ahi, kua tuaina ki raro:
ngaro iho ratou i te riri o tou mata.

<span id="an_80:17">80:17</span> Waiho tou ringa i runga i te tangata o
tou matau, i te tama a te tangata i whakakahangia e koe mau.

<span id="an_80:18">80:18</span> Penei e kore matou e hoki atu i a koe:
whakahauorangia matou, a ka karanga matou ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_80:19">80:19</span> Whakahokia ake matou, e Ihowa, e te
Atua o nga mano; kia marama mai tou mata, a ka ora matou.

<span id="an_81:1">81:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. Na
Ahapa. Kia kaha te waiata ki te Atua, ki to tatou kaha: kia hari te
hamama ki te Atua o Hakopa.

<span id="an_81:2">81:2</span> Whakahuatia te himene, maua mai ki konei
te timipera, te hapa reka me te hatere.

<span id="an_81:3">81:3</span> Whakatangihia te tetere i te kowhititanga
marama, i te kinga o te marama, i to tatou ra hakari.

<span id="an_81:4">81:4</span> Ko te tikanga hoki tenei ma Iharaira, he
mea whakarite na te Atua o Hakopa.

<span id="an_81:5">81:5</span> I whakatakotoria tenei e ia ma Hohepa hei
whakaaturanga, i tona haerenga puta noa i te whenua o Ihipa: i rongo ai
ahau ki reira i tetahi reo, kahore ahau i matau.

<span id="an_81:6">81:6</span> I tangohia mai e ahau tona pokohiwi i te
pikaunga: whakarerea ake e ona ringa te kete.

<span id="an_81:7">81:7</span> I karanga koe ki ahau i te pouritanga, a
kua ora koe i ahau; i whakahoki kupu ahau ki a koe i te wahi ngaro o te
whatitiri; i whakamatau i a koe ki nga wai o Meripa. (Hera.

<span id="an_81:8">81:8</span> ¶ Whakarongo, e taku iwi, a ka whakaatu
ahau ki a koe: e Iharaira, ki te whakarongo koe ki ahau;

<span id="an_81:9">81:9</span> Aua tetahi atua ke i roto i a koe; kaua
ano e koropiko ki te atua ke.

<span id="an_81:10">81:10</span> Ko Ihowa ahau, ko tou Atua, i arahina
mai ai koe i te whenua o Ihipa: kia nui te kowhera o tou mangai, a maku
e whakaki.

<span id="an_81:11">81:11</span> Otiia kihai taku iwi i pai ki te
whakarongo ki toku reo: kihai ano a Iharaira i aro ki ahau.

<span id="an_81:12">81:12</span> Na tukua atu ana ratou e ahau ki te
maro o o ratou ngakau: a haere ana ratou i runga i o ratou whakaaro.

<span id="an_81:13">81:13</span> Aue, te whakarongo taku iwi ki ahau! Te
haere a Iharaira i aku ara!

<span id="an_81:14">81:14</span> Penei e kore e aha kua whati i ahau te
tara o o ratou hoariri: kua tahuri ano toku ringa ki o ratou hoariri.

<span id="an_81:15">81:15</span> Ko te hunga e kino ana ki a Ihowa kua
ngohengohe ki a ia: ko to ratou taima ia kua mau tonu.

<span id="an_81:16">81:16</span> Kua whangainga hoki ratou e ia ki te
witi pai rawa, kua whakamakonatia ano koe e ahau ki te honi i roto i te
kohatu.

<span id="an_82:1">82:1</span> ¶ He himene na Ahapa. E tu ana te Atua i
roto i te whakaminenga o te Atua, e whakawa ana i waenganui i nga atua.

<span id="an_82:2">82:2</span> Kia pehea ake te roa o ta koutou whakawa
he, o ta koutou whakapai ki nga kanohi o te hunga kino. (Hera.

<span id="an_82:3">82:3</span> Whakatikaia ta te ware, ta te pani: kia
tika te whakawa mo te ngakau mamae, mo te rawakore.

<span id="an_82:4">82:4</span> Whakaorangia te ware me te rawakore;
tangohia mai ratou i te ringa o te tangata kino.

<span id="an_82:5">82:5</span> Kahore o ratou matauranga, kakore hoki e
mahara; e kopikopiko noa ana ratou i te pouri; e oioi ana nga turanga
katoa o te whenua.

<span id="an_82:6">82:6</span> ¶ I mea ahau, He atua koutou, he tama
katoa na te Runga Rawa.

<span id="an_82:7">82:7</span> Heoi ka pera koutou me te tangata, ka
mate; ka hinga, ka pera me tetahi o nga piriniha.

<span id="an_82:8">82:8</span> E ara, e te Atua, whakawakia te whenua:
mou hoki nga tauiwi katoa.

<span id="an_83:1">83:1</span> ¶ He waiata, he himene, na Ahapa. E te
Atua, kei wahangu koe, kei whakarongo puku, kei ata noho, e te Atua.

<span id="an_83:2">83:2</span> He mea hoki, tenei ou hoariri te ngangau
nei, a kua ara nga matenga o te hunga e kino ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_83:3">83:3</span> Kua ata ngarahu ratou ki tau iwi, e
whakatakoto korero ana hoki ratou mo au mea huna.

<span id="an_83:4">83:4</span> Kua mea nei ratou, Tena, tatou ka huna i
a ratou, kia kore ai tena iwi; kia kaua ai hoki e maharatia te ingoa o
Iharaira a muri ake nei.

<span id="an_83:5">83:5</span> Kua kotahi to ratou ngakau i a ratou e
runanga ana: kua whakatakoto ratou he tikanga kino ki a koe;

<span id="an_83:6">83:6</span> Ko nga teneti o Eroma, o nga Ihimaeri, o
Moapa, o nga Hakarini;

<span id="an_83:7">83:7</span> A Kepara, a Amona, a Amareke, nga
Pirihitini, me nga tangata o Taira:

<span id="an_83:8">83:8</span> Kua uru hoki a Ahiria ki roto ki a ratou;
kua awhinatia e ratou nga tamariki a Rota. (Hera.

<span id="an_83:9">83:9</span> ¶ Peratia ratou me Miriana: me Hihera, me
Iapini, i te awa i Kihona:

<span id="an_83:10">83:10</span> I mate nei ki Eneroro, i waiho nei hei
whakawairakau mo te whenua.

<span id="an_83:11">83:11</span> Kia rite o ratou rangatira ki a Orepe
raua ko Teepe, ae, o ratou ariki katoa hoki ki a Tepa raua ko Taramuna;

<span id="an_83:12">83:12</span> Mo ratou i mea, Tatou ka tango i nga
kainga o te Atua mo tatou.

<span id="an_83:13">83:13</span> E toku Atua, meinga ratou kia rite ki
te awhiowhio puehu, ki te papapa e puhia ana e te hau.

<span id="an_83:14">83:14</span> Kia rite ki te ahi e kai ana i te
ngahere, ki te mura hoki e toro ai nga maunga;

<span id="an_83:15">83:15</span> Kia pera te whai o tau awha i a ratou,
tau whakaohorere hoki i a ratou ki tau paroro.

<span id="an_83:16">83:16</span> Whakakiia o ratou kanohi ki te whakama:
kia rapu ai ratou ki tou ingoa, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_83:17">83:17</span> Kia whakama, kia ohorere ratou ake ake;
ae, kia numinumi ratou, kia ngaro hoki.

<span id="an_83:18">83:18</span> Kia matau ai ratou, ko koe anake, ko
Ihowa nei tou ingoa, te Runga Rawa i te whenua katoa.

<span id="an_84:1">84:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Kititi. He
himene ma nga tama a Koraha. Ano te ataahua o ou tapenakara, e Ihowa o
nga mano!

<span id="an_84:2">84:2</span> E hiahia ana toku wairua, ae, e hemo ana
ki nga marae o Ihowa: e tangi ana toku ngakau me oku kikokiko ki te Atua
ora.

<span id="an_84:3">84:3</span> Me te pihoihoi hoki kua kite i tetahi
whare, me te warou ano hoki i tetahi ohanga mona, hei takotoranga mo ana
pi, ara i au aata, e Ihowa o nga mano, e toku Kingi, e toku Atua.

<span id="an_84:4">84:4</span> Ka hari te hunga e noho ana i tou whare:
he whakamoemiti tonu ta ratou ki a koe. (Hera.

<span id="an_84:5">84:5</span> Ka hari te tangata ko tona kaha nei kei a
koe: kei roto i o ratou ngakau nga huarahi ki reira.

<span id="an_84:6">84:6</span> Ka haere ratou ra te raorao o Paka, ka
meinga e ratou hei puna: ngaro iho ano hoki nga poka i te ua.

<span id="an_84:7">84:7</span> Ka haere atu ratou i te kaha ki te kaha;
ka kitea ratou ki te aroaro o te Atua i Hiona.

<span id="an_84:8">84:8</span> ¶ E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano,
whakarongo ki taku inoi: tahuri mai tou taringa, e te Atua o Hakopa.
(Hera.

<span id="an_84:9">84:9</span> Titiro mai, e te Atua, e to matou
whakangungu rakau: tirohia iho hoki te mata o tau tangata i whakawahi
ai.

<span id="an_84:10">84:10</span> No te mea, he ra kotahi i ou whare, pai
atu i nga ra kotahi mano: te tiaki tatau i te whare o toku Atua, pai atu
ki ahau i te noho ki nga teneti o te kino.

<span id="an_84:11">84:11</span> He ra hoki a Ihowa te Atua, he
whakangungu rakau: ka homai e Ihowa te atawhai me te kororia; e kore e
kaiponuhia e ia tetahi mea pai ki te hunga e tapatahi ana te haere.

<span id="an_84:12">84:12</span> E Ihowa o nga mano, ka hari te tangata
e whakawhirinaki ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_85:1">85:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene ma
nga tama a Koraha. E Ihowa, kua aro mai koe ki tou whenua, kua
whakahokia mai e koe a Hakopa i te whakarau.

<span id="an_85:2">85:2</span> Kua murua e koe te kino o tau iwi, kua
hipokina e koe o ratou hara katoa (Hera.

<span id="an_85:3">85:3</span> Kua mutu katoa tou weriweri; kua tahuri
ke koe i te aritarita o tou riri.

<span id="an_85:4">85:4</span> Whakahokia ake matou, e te Atua o to
matou whakaoranga: meinga hoki kia mutu tou riri ki a matou.

<span id="an_85:5">85:5</span> E riri ranei koe ki a matou ake ake? E
mauahara tonu ranei, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa?

<span id="an_85:6">85:6</span> E kore ianei koe e whakahoki ake i a
matou ki te ora: kia hari ai tau iwi ki a koe?

<span id="an_85:7">85:7</span> E Ihowa, whakakitea mai tau mahi tohu ki
a matou: tukua mai ki a matou tau whakaoranga.

<span id="an_85:8">85:8</span> ¶ Ka whakarongo ahau ki ta te Atua, ki ta
Ihowa, e korero ai: no te mea mo te rongo mau ana korero ki tana iwi, ki
tana hunga tapu hoki; kaua ia ratou e hoki ki te wairangi.

<span id="an_85:9">85:9</span> Ina, he tata tonu tana whakaoranga ki te
hunga e wehi ana ki a ia, kia noho ai te kororia ki to tatou whenua.

<span id="an_85:10">85:10</span> Kua tutaki te mahi tohu raua ko te
pono: kua kihi ki a raua te tika me te rongo mau.

<span id="an_85:11">85:11</span> Ka tupu ake te pono i te whenua, a ka
titiro iho te tika i te rangi.

<span id="an_85:12">85:12</span> Ae, ka homai e Ihowa te pai: a ka tukua
mai ona hua e to tatou whenua.

<span id="an_85:13">85:13</span> Ka haere te tika i mua i a ia, hei
whakatu i a tatou ki te ara o ona hikoinga.

<span id="an_86:1">86:1</span> ¶ He inoi na Rawiri. Whakatitahatia iho
tou taringa, e Ihowa whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau; he ware hoki ahau,
he rawakore.

<span id="an_86:2">86:2</span> Tiakina toku wairua: he tapu hoki ahau;
mau, e toku Atua, e whakaora tau pononga e whakawhirinaki atu nei ki a
koe.

<span id="an_86:3">86:3</span> Tohungia ahau, e te Ariki: e karanga nei
hoki ahau ki a koe i te ra roa nei.

<span id="an_86:4">86:4</span> Whakaharitia te wairua o tau pononga; ka
ara atu nei hoki toku wairua, e te Ariki, ki a koe.

<span id="an_86:5">86:5</span> He pai hoki koe, e te Ariki, he ngawari:
e ranea ana hoki tau mahi tohu ki te hunga katoa e karanga ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_86:6">86:6</span> Tahuri mai tou taringa, e Ihowa, ki taku
inoi: whakarongo kitoku reo unene.

<span id="an_86:7">86:7</span> Ka karanga ahau ki a koe i te ra o toku
pouri: e whakahoki kupu mai hoki koe ki ahau.

<span id="an_86:8">86:8</span> ¶ Kahore he rite mou, e te Ariki, i roto
i nga atua: kahore hoki he rite mo au mahi.

<span id="an_86:9">86:9</span> Ka haere mai nga iwi katoa i hanga e koe,
a ka koropiko ki tou aroaro, e te Ariki; ka whakakororia hoki i tou
ingoa.

<span id="an_86:10">86:10</span> He nui hoki koe, e mahi ana i nga mea
whakamiharo: ko koe anake te Atua.

<span id="an_86:11">86:11</span> Whakaakona ahau ki tau ara, e Ihowa; ka
haere ahau i runga i tou pono: whakatapatahitia toku ngakau ki te wehi i
tou ingoa.

<span id="an_86:12">86:12</span> Ka whakamoemiti katoa toku ngakau ki a
koe, e te Ariki, e toku Atua: ka whakakororia ano i tou ingoa ake ake.

<span id="an_86:13">86:13</span> He nui hoki tau mahi tohu ki ahau: a
kua whakaorangia e koe toku wairua i te reinga i raro riro.

<span id="an_86:14">86:14</span> E te Atua, kua whakatika ki ahau te
hunga whakakake: kua whaia ano toku wairua e te huihuinga o te hunga
tutu; kahore hoki koe e waiho i to ratou aroaro.

<span id="an_86:15">86:15</span> Ko koe ia, e te Ariki, he Atua atawhai,
he tohu tangata: he puhoi ki te riri, e hua ana te mahi tohu me te pono.

<span id="an_86:16">86:16</span> Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki ahau:
homai tou kaha ki tau pononga, whakaorangia te tama a tau pononga
wahine.

<span id="an_86:17">86:17</span> Whakakitea mai ki ahau he tohu mo te
pai: kia kite ai te hunga e kino ana ki ahau, kia whakama ai: nou e
Ihowa i awhina i ahau, i whakamarie i ahau.

<span id="an_87:1">87:1</span> ¶ He himene, he waiata ma nga tama a
Koraha. Kei nga maunga tapu tona turanga:

<span id="an_87:2">87:2</span> E arohaina rawatia ana e Ihowa nga kuwaha
o Hiona i nga nohoanga katoa o Hakopa.

<span id="an_87:3">87:3</span> He mea kororia nga mea e korerotia ana
mou, e te pa o te Atua. (Hera.

<span id="an_87:4">87:4</span> ¶ Ka korerotia e ahau a Rahapa raua ko
Papurona ki roto i te hunga e matau ana ki ahau: tirohia atu a
Pirihitia, a Taira, a Etiopia; i whanau tenei ki reira.

<span id="an_87:5">87:5</span> Ae ra ko te kupu tenei mo Hiona, I whanau
tenei me tera ki reira: ma te Runga Rawa pu ano ia e whakapumau.

<span id="an_87:6">87:6</span> Ka korerotia e Ihowa, ina tuhituhia nga
iwi, I whanau tenei ki reira. (Hera.

<span id="an_87:7">87:7</span> Na ka mea te hunga waiata, me te hunga
kanikani, Kei a koe oku puna katoa.

<span id="an_88:1">88:1</span> ¶ He waiata, he himene ma nga tama a
Koraha. Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. Maharata Reanoto. He Makiri na Hemana
Eterahi. E Ihowa, e te Atua o toku whakaoranga, he tangi taku ki tou
aroaro i te ao, i te po.

<span id="an_88:2">88:2</span> Kia tae atu taku inoi ki tou aroaro:
whakatitahatia mai tou taringa ki taku tangi.

<span id="an_88:3">88:3</span> Kua ki hoki toku wairua i te pouri, a e
whakatata ana toku ora ki te reinga.

<span id="an_88:4">88:4</span> Kua taua tahitia ahau me te hunga e heke
ana ki te rua; e rite ana ahau ki te tangata kahore ona awhina!

<span id="an_88:5">88:5</span> I maka ki waenga i nga tupapaku, me he
tangata i patua e takoto ana i te urupa, kahore nei e maharatia e koe i
muri; he mea momotu ke ratou na tou ringa.

<span id="an_88:6">88:6</span> Kua whakatakotoria ahau e koe ki te rua i
raro riro, ki te pouri, ki nga rire.

<span id="an_88:7">88:7</span> E pehia ana ahau e tou riri, e pakia ana
hoki e koe ki au ngaru katoa. (Hera.

<span id="an_88:8">88:8</span> Kua whakamataratia atu e koe oku hoa kia
tawhiti i ahau: kua meinga ahau e koe hei mea whakarihariha ki a ratou:
kua uakina mai ahau, a kahore e puta ki waho.

<span id="an_88:9">88:9</span> Kua he toku kanohi i te tangihanga: e
karanga ana ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i nga ra katoa, kua totoro hoki oku
ringa ki a koe.

<span id="an_88:10">88:10</span> ¶ Tera ranei koe e mahi merekara ki nga
tupapaku? E ara koia te hunga kua mate ki te whakamoemiti ki a koe?
(Hera.

<span id="an_88:11">88:11</span> Ka kauwhautia ranei tou aroha i roto i
te urupa? tou pono i roto i te ngaromanga?

<span id="an_88:12">88:12</span> E matauria koia au mea whakamiharo i
roto i te pouri? tou tika i te whenua o te warewaretanga?

<span id="an_88:13">88:13</span> Ko ahau ia kua karanga ki a koe, e
Ihowa: a i te ata ka tae atu taku inoi ki tou aroaro.

<span id="an_88:14">88:14</span> He aha, e Ihowa, i panga ai toku wairua
e koe? He aha i huna ai tou mata ki ahau?

<span id="an_88:15">88:15</span> No toku tamarikitanga ake ano i pakia
ai ahau, i whakahemohemo ai: i ahau e pehia ana e au whakawehi, ka
pororaru noa iho.

<span id="an_88:16">88:16</span> I tika tou riri nui ma runga i ahau;
kua haukotia ahau e au mea whakawehi.

<span id="an_88:17">88:17</span> Ano he wai ratou ki te karapoti i ahau
i te ra roa nei; hui tahi ratou ki te taiawhio i ahau.

<span id="an_88:18">88:18</span> Kua wehea e koe kia tawhiti atu i ahau
te hoa hei aroha mai, me oku hoa ki roto ki te pouri.

<span id="an_89:1">89:1</span> ¶ He Makiri na Etana Eterahi. Ka
waiatatia e ahau nga mahi tohu a Ihowa ake ake: ka whakapuakina e toku
mangai tou pono ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_89:2">89:2</span> I mea hoki ahau, Ka hanga ake te mahi
tohu mo ake tonu atu: ka whakapumautia e koe tou pono ki nga tino rangi
ra ano.

<span id="an_89:3">89:3</span> Kua whakarite kawenata ahau ki taku i
whiriwhiri ai: kua oati ki taku pononga ki a Rawiri;

<span id="an_89:4">89:4</span> Ka pumau i ahau ou uri ake ake: ka hanga
tou torona ki nga whakatupuranga katoa. (Hera.

<span id="an_89:5">89:5</span> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti ano nga rangi, e Ihowa,
ki au mahi whakamiharo; ki tou pono hoki i roto i te whakaminenga o te
hunga tapu.

<span id="an_89:6">89:6</span> Ko wai oti i nga rangi hei rite mo Ihowa?
Ko wai i roto i nga tama a te hunga nunui e rite ana ki a Ihowa?

<span id="an_89:7">89:7</span> He Atua whakamataku rawa i roto i te
whakaminenga o te hunga tapu, e wehingia ana i runga ake i a ratou katoa
i tetahi taha, i tetahi taha ona?

<span id="an_89:8">89:8</span> E Ihowa, e te Atua o nga mano, ko wai te
mea kaha hei rite mou, e IHA? Hei rite ranei mo tou pono i tetahi taha
ou, i tetahi taha?

<span id="an_89:9">89:9</span> Ko koe te kingi o te huamo o te moana: ka
oho ona ngaru, ko koe hei whakamarino.

<span id="an_89:10">89:10</span> Mongamonga noa i a koe a Rahapa ano he
tangata i patua: marara ana i a koe, i tou ringa kaha ou hoariri.

<span id="an_89:11">89:11</span> Nau nga rangi, nau te whenua: te ao me
ona mea e hua ana i runga, nau ena i pumau ai.

<span id="an_89:12">89:12</span> Ko te raki me te tonga nau ena i hanga:
ka hari a Taporo raua ko Heremona ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_89:13">89:13</span> He takakau marohirohi tou: he pakari
tou ringa, rewa tonu tou matau ki runga.

<span id="an_89:14">89:14</span> Ko te tika me te whakawa te turanga o
tou torona: e haere ana te mahi tohu me te pono i mua i tou aroaro.

<span id="an_89:15">89:15</span> ¶ Ka hari te iwi e mohio ana ki te
tangi whakahari: e haere ana ratou, e Ihowa, i te marama o tou mata.

<span id="an_89:16">89:16</span> E hari ana ratou ki tou ingoa i te roa
o te ra: a ma tou tika ka kake ai ratou.

<span id="an_89:17">89:17</span> Ko koe hoki te kororia o to ratou kaha:
ma tau manako ano ka ara ai to matou haona.

<span id="an_89:18">89:18</span> Na Ihowa hoki to matou whakangungu
rakau: a na te Mea Tapu o Iharaira to tatou kingi.

<span id="an_89:19">89:19</span> ¶ I korero moemoea koe i reira ki tau
Mea Tapu, i mea, Kua hoatu e ahau he kaha ki runga ki tetahi marohirohi;
kua whakanuia e ahau tetahi i whiriwhiria i roto i te iwi.

<span id="an_89:20">89:20</span> Kua kitea e ahau taku pononga, a
Rawiri: kua whakawahia ia e ahau ki taku hinu tapu:

<span id="an_89:21">89:21</span> Ka u atu toku ringa hei awhina mona: ma
toku takakau ano ia e whakakaha.

<span id="an_89:22">89:22</span> E kore te hoariri e whai wahi ki a ia:
e kore ano hoki te tama a te kino e tukino i a ia.

<span id="an_89:23">89:23</span> Maku e tukituki ona hoariri ki tona
aroaro: ka whiua e ahau te hunga e kino ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_89:24">89:24</span> Otira ka mau ki a ia toku pono me taku
mahi tohu: a ma toku ingoa ka ara ai tona haona.

<span id="an_89:25">89:25</span> Maku ano tona ringa ka pa ai ki te
moana: tona matau ki nga awa.

<span id="an_89:26">89:26</span> Ka karanga ia ki ahau, Ko koe toku
Papa, toku Atua, te kohatu o toku whakaoranga.

<span id="an_89:27">89:27</span> Ka waiho ano ia hei matamua maku ki
runga ake i nga kingi o te whenua.

<span id="an_89:28">89:28</span> Ka rongoatia e ahau taku mahi tohu mona
ake tonu atu: ka mau tonu taku kawenata ki a ia.

<span id="an_89:29">89:29</span> Ka meinga hoki e ahau ona uri kia mau
tonu ake ake, tona torona ano ko nga ra o te rangi.

<span id="an_89:30">89:30</span> Ki te whakarerea e ana tamariki taku
ture, a kahore e haere i aku whakaritenga;

<span id="an_89:31">89:31</span> Ki te takahi ratou i aku tikanga; a
kahore e pupuri i aku whakahau;

<span id="an_89:32">89:32</span> Katahi ka whaia ta ratou mahi tutu e
taku rakau, o ratou kino e te whiu.

<span id="an_89:33">89:33</span> Otira e kore e tangohia rawatia e ahau
taku mahi tohu i a ia, e tuku ranei i toku pono kia he.

<span id="an_89:34">89:34</span> E kore taku kawenata e takahia e ahau,
e kore ano e whakarereketia te mea i puta i oku ngutu.

<span id="an_89:35">89:35</span> Kotahi aku oatitanga i toku tapu; e
kore ahau e teka ki a Rawiri.

<span id="an_89:36">89:36</span> Ka mau tonu tona uri ake ake; a ka rite
tona torona ki te ra i toku aroaro.

<span id="an_89:37">89:37</span> Ka rite tona pumau ki to te marama ake
ake: hei kaiwhakaatu pono ano i runga i te rangi. (Hera.

<span id="an_89:38">89:38</span> ¶ Na kua panga nei koe, kua
whakarihariha, kua riri ki tau i whakawahi ai.

<span id="an_89:39">89:39</span> Kua weriweri koe ki te kawenata ki tau
pononga: kua whakanoaia e koe tona karauna, taka noa ki te whenua.

<span id="an_89:40">89:40</span> Kua pakaruhia e koe ona taiepa katoa;
whakamotitia iho e koe ona pa kaha.

<span id="an_89:41">89:41</span> E pahua ana i a ia nga tangata katoa e
tika ana i te ara: he tawainga ia na ona hoa tata.

<span id="an_89:42">89:42</span> Kua whakarewaina e koe te ringa matau o
ona hoa whawhai: kua meinga e koe kia hari ona hoa whawhai katoa.

<span id="an_89:43">89:43</span> Ae, e ngore ana i a koe te mata o tana
hoari: kihai ano koe i tautoko i a ia ki te tatauranga.

<span id="an_89:44">89:44</span> Kua whakamutua e koe tona kororia, kua
maka tona torona ki raro ki te whenua.

<span id="an_89:45">89:45</span> Kua poroa e koe nga ra o tona
taitamarikitanga: kua hipokina ia e koe ki te whakama. (Hera.

<span id="an_89:46">89:46</span> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa, e whakangaro
ai koe i a koe, ake tonu atu? Kia pehea te roa e toro ana tou riri ano
he ahi?

<span id="an_89:47">89:47</span> Kia mahara ki te poto rawa o toku
taima: he aha i hanga ai e koe nga tangata katoa hei kore noa iho?

<span id="an_89:48">89:48</span> Ko wai tena tangata e ora nei, a e kore
e kite i te mate? E mawhiti koia i a ia tona wairua i te kaha o te
reinga? (Hera.

<span id="an_89:49">89:49</span> E te Ariki, kei hea au arohatanga o mua
i oatitia ai e koe ki a Rawiri i runga i tou pono?

<span id="an_89:50">89:50</span> Maharatia, e te Ariki, te tawai ki au
pononga; e mau nei ki toku uma te tawai a nga iwi nunui katoa:

<span id="an_89:51">89:51</span> Te tawai a ou hoariri, e Ihowa, ta
ratou tawai nei ki nga hikoinga o tau i whakawahi ai.

<span id="an_89:52">89:52</span> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa ake ake.
Amine, ae Amine.

<span id="an_90:1">90:1</span> ¶ He inoi na Mohi, na te tangata a te
Atua. E te Ariki, ko koe to matou nohoanga i nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_90:2">90:2</span> Kahore ano i whanau noa nga maunga,
kahore i hanga e koe te whenua me te ao, ko koe te Atua no tua whakarere
a ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_90:3">90:3</span> E whakahokia ana e koe te tangata kia
mongamonga noa, a e mea ana, E hoki, e nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_90:4">90:4</span> Ki tau titiro hoki, he rite nga tau
kotahi mano ki te ra onanahi, kua pahure atu nei, ki te mataaratanga
hoki i te po.

<span id="an_90:5">90:5</span> Me te mea na te waipuke tau kahakinga i a
ratou; he moe ratou: i te ata ano he tarutaru e tupu ana.

<span id="an_90:6">90:6</span> I te ata e tupu ana, e pihi ana: i te
ahiahi kua kotia, kua maroke.

<span id="an_90:7">90:7</span> ¶ Kua hemo nei hoki matou i tou riri: ka
ohorere hoki i tou aritatanga.

<span id="an_90:8">90:8</span> Kua maka e koe o matou kino ki tou
aroaro, o matou mea huna ki te marama o tou mata.

<span id="an_90:9">90:9</span> Ka pau o matou ra katoa, me te riri ano
koe: hemo ake o matou tau ano he korero e korerotia ana.

<span id="an_90:10">90:10</span> Ko nga ra o o matou tau e whitu tekau
tau; a ki te whai kaha, ka waru tekau tau; heoi he mahi mauiui, he pouri
to ratou kaha; ka hohoro hoki te hatepea atu, a ka rere atu matou.

<span id="an_90:11">90:11</span> Ko wai te matau ana ki te kaha o tou
riri? Rite pu ki te wehi ki a koe tou riri.

<span id="an_90:12">90:12</span> ¶ Akona matou ki te tatau i o matou ra,
kia anga ai te ngakau ki te whakaaro.

<span id="an_90:13">90:13</span> Hoki mai, e Ihowa, kia pehea ake te
roa? A kia puta ke he whakaaro mou ki au pononga.

<span id="an_90:14">90:14</span> Kia na matou i te ata i tau mahi tohu:
kia hari ai matou, kia koa ai, i o matou ra katoa.

<span id="an_90:15">90:15</span> Whakaharitia matou, kia rite ki nga ra
i whakawhiua ai matou e koe, ki nga tau i kite ai matou i te kino.

<span id="an_90:16">90:16</span> Kia puta mai tau mahi ki au pononga, me
tou kororia ki a ratou tamariki.

<span id="an_90:17">90:17</span> A hei runga i a matou te ataahua o
Ihowa, o to matou Atua: whakapumautia ano ki a matou te mahi a o matou
ringa, ae ra, te mahi a o matou ringa, whakapumautia e koe.

<span id="an_91:1">91:1</span> ¶ Ko te tangata kei te wahi ngaro o te
Runga Rawa tona kainga, ka noho ia i raro i te taumarumarutanga o te
Kaha Rawa.

<span id="an_91:2">91:2</span> Ka kiia e ahau a Ihowa, Ko ia toku
piringa, toku pa, toku Atua, ka whakawhirinaki ahau ki a ia.

<span id="an_91:3">91:3</span> Mana hoki koe e whakaora i te mahanga a
te kaihopu manu, i te mate nanakia.

<span id="an_91:4">91:4</span> Ka hipokina koe e ia ki ona hou, a ka
piri koe ki raro i ona pakau: ko tona pono hei whakangungu rakau, hei
puapua mou.

<span id="an_91:5">91:5</span> E kore koe e wehi i te mea whakamataku i
te po: i te pere e rere ana i te awatea.

<span id="an_91:6">91:6</span> I te mate uruta e rere ana i te pouri: i
te whakangaromanga e whakangaro ana i te poutumarotanga.

<span id="an_91:7">91:7</span> He mano te hinga ki tou taha, tekau hoki
nga mano ki tou matau; otiia e kore e tata ki a koe.

<span id="an_91:8">91:8</span> Ka titiro kau ou kanohi, ka matakitaki ki
te utu mo te hunga kino.

<span id="an_91:9">91:9</span> ¶ Ko koe hoki, e Ihowa, toku piranga! kua
waiho e koe te Runga Rawa hei nohoanga mou:

<span id="an_91:10">91:10</span> Kahore he kino e pa ki a koe, kahore
ano he whiu e tata ki tou teneti.

<span id="an_91:11">91:11</span> Ka korerotia iho hoki koe e ia ki ana
anahera kia tiakina koe i ou ara katoa.

<span id="an_91:12">91:12</span> Ma ratou koe e hiki ake ki o ratou
ringa, kei tutuki tou waewae ki te kohatu.

<span id="an_91:13">91:13</span> Ka haere koe i runga i te raiona, i te
neke: ka takahia e koe ki raro te kuao raiona me te nakahi.

<span id="an_91:14">91:14</span> Ka whakaora ahau i a ia, mona i aroha
ki ahau; maku ia e whakateitei ake, mona i matau ki toku ingoa.

<span id="an_91:15">91:15</span> Ka karanga ia ki ahau, a ka whakahoki
kupu ahau ki a ia: ka tata ahau ki a ia i te wa o te he; maku ia e
whakaora, maku ano ia e whakahonore.

<span id="an_91:16">91:16</span> Ka whakaroaina e ahau ona ra, a na noa
ia: ka whakakitea hoki taku whakaoranga ki a ia.

<span id="an_92:1">92:1</span> ¶ He himene, he waiata mo te ra Hapati.
He mea pai te whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, te himene atu ki tou ingoa, e te
Runga Rawa:

<span id="an_92:2">92:2</span> Te whakakite i tou atawhai i te ata, i
tou pono i nga po katoa;

<span id="an_92:3">92:3</span> I runga i te aho tekau, i te hatere; i te
tangi huatau a te hapa.

<span id="an_92:4">92:4</span> Nau hoki ahau, e Ihowa, i whakahari ki
tau mahi: ka whakamanamana ahau ki nga meatanga a ou ringa.

<span id="an_92:5">92:5</span> Ano te nui o au mahi, e Ihowa! hohonu
rawa ou whakaaro.

<span id="an_92:6">92:6</span> Ko te tangata poauau, kahore ia e matau;
kahore hoki tenei e mohiotia e te kuware.

<span id="an_92:7">92:7</span> ¶ Kia pihi ake nga whakaarokore ano he
tarutaru, a kia tupu nga kaimahi katoa i te kino; he ngaromanga tena no
ratou ake ake;

<span id="an_92:8">92:8</span> Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, kei runga rawa ake
ake.

<span id="an_92:9">92:9</span> Na, ko ou hoa whawhai, e Ihowa, na, ko ou
hoa whawhai, ka ngaro; ka marara katoa nga kaimahi i te kino.

<span id="an_92:10">92:10</span> Otira ka ara i a koe toku haona, ka
pera i to te kau maka: ka whakawahia ahau ki te hinu hou.

<span id="an_92:11">92:11</span> Ka kite hoki toku kanohi i taku i
hiahia ai ki runga ki oku hoariri, ka rongo oku taringa i taku i hiahia
ai o te hunga kino e whakatika ana mai ki ahau.

<span id="an_92:12">92:12</span> Ka rite te tupu o te tangata tika ki to
te nikau; ka rite tona nui ki to te hita i Repanona.

<span id="an_92:13">92:13</span> Ko te hunga i whakatokia ki te whare o
Ihowa ka tupu ki nga marae o to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_92:14">92:14</span> Ka whai hua tonu ratou ua hina: ki tonu
i te wai, matomato tonu;

<span id="an_92:15">92:15</span> Hei whakakite i te tika o Ihowa: ko ia
toku kohatu, kahore hoki ona he.

<span id="an_93:1">93:1</span> ¶ E kingi ana a Ihowa; he kororia tona
kakahu; he kakahu to Ihowa, he mea whitiki ia ki te kaha: kua u hoki te
ao, te taea te nekeneke.

<span id="an_93:2">93:2</span> No mua iho tou torona i whakapumautia ai:
nonamata riro koe.

<span id="an_93:3">93:3</span> Ko nga roma, e Ihowa, kua ara, nga roma
nei, kua ara to ratou reo; ka ara nga ngaru o nga roma.

<span id="an_93:4">93:4</span> I runga ake i nga reo o nga wai maha, i
nga tuatea nunui o te moana, ko Ihowa i runga, te mea kaha.

<span id="an_93:5">93:5</span> Pono atu au whakaaturanga: he huatau te
tapu mo tou whare, e Ihowa, mo ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_94:1">94:1</span> ¶ E Ihowa, e te Atua, e te Kairapu utu; e
te Atua, e te Kairapu utu, tiaho mai.

<span id="an_94:2">94:2</span> E ara, e te Kaiwhakawa o te whenua: hoatu
te utu e rite ana ki te hunga whakakake.

<span id="an_94:3">94:3</span> Kia pehea te roa, e Ihowa, o te hunga
kino nei, kia pehea te roa o te hunga kino e whakamanamana ana?

<span id="an_94:4">94:4</span> Kei te korero whakatu ratou, kei te
korero whakahi: kei te korero whakapehapeha ki a ratou nga kaimahi katoa
i te kino.

<span id="an_94:5">94:5</span> Mongamonga noa tau iwi i a ratou, e
Ihowa: e tukinotia ana e ratou tou kainga tupu.

<span id="an_94:6">94:6</span> E patua ana e ratou te pouaru, te manene:
e kohuru ana i te pani.

<span id="an_94:7">94:7</span> A e mea ana, E kore a Ihowa e kite; e
kore e maharatia e te Atua o Hakopa.

<span id="an_94:8">94:8</span> Kia matau, e nga poauau o te iwi: a hea
ano koutou whai mahara ai, e nga kuware?

<span id="an_94:9">94:9</span> Ko te kaiwhakato o te taringa, e kore
ranei ia e rongo? Ko te kaihanga o te kanohi, e kore ianei ia e kite?

<span id="an_94:10">94:10</span> Ko te kaipapaki o nga iwi e kore ranei
ia e papaki, ara ko te kaiwhakaako nei i te tangata kia mohio?

<span id="an_94:11">94:11</span> E matau ana a Ihowa ki nga whakaaro o
te tangata, he mea teka noa.

<span id="an_94:12">94:12</span> ¶ Ka hari te tangata e pakia ana e koe,
e Ihowa: e whakaakona ana i roto i tau ture;

<span id="an_94:13">94:13</span> Kia marie ai tona ngakau i a koe i nga
ra o te he, a keria noatia iho te poka mo te tangata kino.

<span id="an_94:14">94:14</span> E kore hoki a Ihowa e panga i tana iwi,
e kore ano e whakarere i tona kainga tupu.

<span id="an_94:15">94:15</span> Engari e hoki te whakawa ki te tika: a
e arumia e nga tangata ngakau tika katoa.

<span id="an_94:16">94:16</span> Ko wai toku hei whakatika ake ki te
hunga kino? Ko wai toku hei tu ake ki nga kaimahi i te hara?

<span id="an_94:17">94:17</span> Mehemea kaua a Ihowa hei awhina moku,
penei kua noho kupukore noa atu toku wairua.

<span id="an_94:18">94:18</span> I taku meatanga, Ka paheke toku waewae;
na tau mahi tohu, e Ihowa, ahau i tautoko ake.

<span id="an_94:19">94:19</span> I oku whakaaronga maha i roto i toku
ngakau ko au whakamarie toku oranga ngakau.

<span id="an_94:20">94:20</span> Tera ranei e whakahoa ki a koe te
torona o te kino, e whakatakoto nei i te mahi nanakia hei ture?

<span id="an_94:21">94:21</span> Kei te whakahuihui ratou ki te poke i
te wairua o te tangata tika, e mea ana kia heke te toto harakore.

<span id="an_94:22">94:22</span> Ko Ihowa ia toku pa teko: ko toku Atua
hei kohatu piringa moku.

<span id="an_94:23">94:23</span> A nana i whakahoki to ratou kino ki
runga ki a ratou, a tera ia e whakangaro i a ratou i roto i o ratou
kino: ma Ihowa, ma to tatou Atua ratou e whakangaro.

<span id="an_95:1">95:1</span> ¶ Tena, kia waiata tatou ki a Ihowa: kia
hari te hamama ki te kamaka o to tatou whakaoranga.

<span id="an_95:2">95:2</span> Kia haere tatou me te whakawhetai atu ki
tona aroaro: kia ngahau hoki a tatou himene ki a ia.

<span id="an_95:3">95:3</span> No te mea he Atua nui hoki a Ihowa, he
Kingi nui i nga atua katoa.

<span id="an_95:4">95:4</span> Kei tona ringa nga wahi hohonu o te
whenua: a nana nga maunga teitei.

<span id="an_95:5">95:5</span> Nana te moana, nana ano i hanga, a na ona
ringa i whai ahua ai te whenua maroke.

<span id="an_95:6">95:6</span> Haere mai tatou, kia koropiko, kia tuohu:
kia tukua nga turi ki te aroaro o Ihowa, o to tatou Kaihanga.

<span id="an_95:7">95:7</span> ¶ Ko ia hoki to tatou Atua; ko tatou tana
iwi e hepara ai, nga hipi a tona ringa. Ki te rongo koutou ki tona reo
aianei.

<span id="an_95:8">95:8</span> Kaua e whakapakeketia o koutou ngakau:
kei pera me o te whakatoinga, me o te ra o te whakamatautauranga i te
koraha;

<span id="an_95:9">95:9</span> I ahau i whakamatautauria e o koutou
matua, i ata mohiotia, i to ratou kitenga ano hoki i aku mahi.

<span id="an_95:10">95:10</span> E wha tekau nga tau i hoha ai ahau ki
tenei whakatupuranga, na ka mea ahau; He iwi ngakau kotiti ke ratou,
kahore hoki ratou e mohio ki aku ara.

<span id="an_95:11">95:11</span> Na reira i riri ai ahau, i oati ai
hoki; e kore ratou e tae ki toku okiokinga.

<span id="an_96:1">96:1</span> ¶ Waiatatia he waiata hou ki a Ihowa:
waiata, e te whenua katoa, ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_96:2">96:2</span> Waiata ki a Ihowa, whakapaingia tona
ingoa: whakakitea tana whakaoranga i tenei ra, i tenei ra.

<span id="an_96:3">96:3</span> Whakapuakina tona kororia i waenganui i
nga tauiwi, ana mahi whakamiharo i waenganui i nga iwi katoa.

<span id="an_96:4">96:4</span> He nui hoki a Ihowa, he tika ano kia nui
te whakamoemiti ki a ia: kia wehingia nuitia ai i nga atua katoa.

<span id="an_96:5">96:5</span> He whakapakoko hoki nga atua katoa o nga
iwi: na Ihowa ia i hanga nga rangi.

<span id="an_96:6">96:6</span> He honore, he kororia kei tona aroaro:
kei tona wahi tapu te kaha me te ataahua.

<span id="an_96:7">96:7</span> Waiho atu i a Ihowa, e nga hapu katoa o
nga iwi: waiho atu i a Ihowa te kororia me te kaha.

<span id="an_96:8">96:8</span> Waiho atu i a Ihowa te kororia e tika ana
mo tona ingoa: maua mai he whakahere, haere mai hoki ki ona marae.

<span id="an_96:9">96:9</span> Koropiko ki a Ihowa i roto i te ataahua o
te tapu: kia wehi ra ki tona aroaro, e te whenua katoa.

<span id="an_96:10">96:10</span> ¶ Mea atu i waenganui o nga tauiwi, E
kingi ana a Ihowa: ka u te whenua, te taea te whakangaueue; ka tika ana
whakawa mo nga iwi.

<span id="an_96:11">96:11</span> Kia hari nga rangi, kia koa te whenua,
kia haruru te moana, me nga mea e hua ana i roto.

<span id="an_96:12">96:12</span> Kia hari te mara, me nga mea katoa i
runga: ko reira ano koa ai nga rakau katoa o te ngahere;

<span id="an_96:13">96:13</span> Ki te aroaro o Ihowa, e haere mai ana
hoki ia; e haere mai ana ia ki te whakawa mo te whenua: ka whakawa ia mo
te ao i runga i te tika, mo nga iwi hoki i runga i tona pono.

<span id="an_97:1">97:1</span> ¶ Ko Ihowa te Kingi, kia hari te whenua,
kia koa nga tini moutere.

<span id="an_97:2">97:2</span> Ko te kapua me te pouri kei ona taha
katoa: ko te tika, ko te whakawa, te turanga o tona torona.

<span id="an_97:3">97:3</span> He kapura e haere ana i mua i a ia, a pau
ake ona hoariri a taka noa.

<span id="an_97:4">97:4</span> Marama tonu te ao i ana uira: i kite te
whenua, a wiri ana.

<span id="an_97:5">97:5</span> Rewa noa nga maunga, ano he ware pi, i te
aroaro o Ihowa, i te aroaro o te Ariki o te whenua katoa.

<span id="an_97:6">97:6</span> E whakapuakina ana e nga rangi tona tika:
a e kitea ana e nga iwi katoa tona kororia.

<span id="an_97:7">97:7</span> Kia whakama katoa te hunga e mahi ana ki
nga whakapakoko, e whakamanamana ana ki nga atua horihori: koropiko ki a
ia, e nga atua katoa.

<span id="an_97:8">97:8</span> ¶ I rongo a Hiona, a koa ana:
whakamanamana ana nga tamahine o Hura, e Ihowa, ki au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_97:9">97:9</span> Ko koe hoki, e Ihowa, kei runga noa ake i
te whenua katoa: kua whakanuia koe ki runga noa ake i nga atua katoa.

<span id="an_97:10">97:10</span> E te hunga e aroha ana ki a Ihowa, e
kino ki te he: e tiakina ana e ia nga wairua o tana hunga tapu; e
whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i nga ringa o te hunga kino.

<span id="an_97:11">97:11</span> Kua oti te marama te whakato mo te
hunga tika: me te koa mo te hunga ngakau tapatahi.

<span id="an_97:12">97:12</span> Kia hari ki a Ihowa, e te hunga tika:
whakamoemiti ki tona ingoa tapu.

<span id="an_98:1">98:1</span> ¶ He himene. Waiatatia ki a Ihowa he
waiata hou; he mahi whakamiharo hoki ana: na tona ringa matau, na tona
ringa tapu, i taea ai e ia te whakaora.

<span id="an_98:2">98:2</span> Kua whakakitea e Ihowa tana whakaoranga,
kua whakapuakina e ia tona tika ki te aroaro o nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_98:3">98:3</span> Kua mahara ia ki tana mahi tohu, ki tona
pono ki te whare o Iharaira; a kua kite nga pito katoa o te whenua i te
whakaoranga a to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_98:4">98:4</span> ¶ Kia hari te hamama, e te whenua katoa,
ki a Ihowa: hamama, kia hari, ae ra, himene atu.

<span id="an_98:5">98:5</span> Himene ki a Ihowa i runga i te hapa; i
runga i te hapa, me te himene ano te reo.

<span id="an_98:6">98:6</span> I runga i te tetere, i te tangi ano o te
koronete: kia hari te hamama ki te aroaro o Ihowa, o te Kingi.

<span id="an_98:7">98:7</span> Kia haruru te moana me nga mea e hua ana
i roto, te ao me ona tangata e noho ana i runga.

<span id="an_98:8">98:8</span> Kia papaki nga ringa o nga roma, kia hari
tahi nga pukepuke.

<span id="an_98:9">98:9</span> Ki te aroaro o Ihowa: e haere mai ana
hoki ia ki te whakawa mo te whenua: ka whakawa ia mo te ao i runga i te
tika, mo nga iwi hoki i runga i te pono.

<span id="an_99:1">99:1</span> ¶ Ko Ihowa te Kingi; kia wiri nga iwi: e
noho ana ia i waenganui i nga kerupima; kia ngaueue te whenua.

<span id="an_99:2">99:2</span> He nui a Ihowa i Hiona: kei runga ake ia
i nga iwi katoa.

<span id="an_99:3">99:3</span> Kia whakamoemiti ratou ki tou ingoa nui,
whakamataku; he tapu ia.

<span id="an_99:4">99:4</span> E matenui ana hoki te kaha o te kingi ki
te whakawa tika; ko koe hei whakapumau i te pono: he whakawa tika, he
hekore tau mahi i roto i a Hakopa.

<span id="an_99:5">99:5</span> Whakanuia a Ihowa, to tatou Atua:
koropiko ki tona turanga waewae; he tapu ia.

<span id="an_99:6">99:6</span> ¶ Ko Mohi raua ko Arona i roto i ana
tohunga, me Hamuera i roto i te hunga e karanga ana ki tona ingoa: i
karanga ratou ki a Ihowa, a whakahoki kupu ana mai ia ki a ratou.

<span id="an_99:7">99:7</span> I korero ia ki a ratou i roto i te pou
kapua: i pupuri ratou i ana whakaaturanga, i te tikanga i whakatakotoria
e ia ki a ratou.

<span id="an_99:8">99:8</span> E Ihowa, e to matou Atua, i whakahoki
kupu koe ki a ratou: he Atua tohu koe i a ratou, otiia i rapu utu ano
koe mo a ratou mahi.

<span id="an_99:9">99:9</span> Whakanuia a Ihowa, to tatou Atua,
koropiko atu i tona maunga tapu: he tapu hoki a Ihowa, to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_100:1">100:1</span> ¶ He himene whakamoemiti. Kia hari te
hamama ki a Ihowa, e nga whenua katoa:

<span id="an_100:2">100:2</span> Mahi atu ki a Ihowa i runga i te koa,
waiata haere ki tona aroaro.

<span id="an_100:3">100:3</span> Kia matau ki a Ihowa, ko ia te Atua:
nana tatou i hanga, ehara hoki i a tatou: ko tana iwi tatou, ko ana hipi
e hepara ai.

<span id="an_100:4">100:4</span> Tomokia ona tatau i runga i te
whakawhetai, ona marae i runga i te whakamoemiti: whakawhetai atu ki a
ia, whakapaingia tona ingoa.

<span id="an_100:5">100:5</span> He pai hoki a Ihowa, pumau tonu tana
mahi tohu: a kei tena whakatupuranga, kei tena whakatupuranga, tona
pono.

<span id="an_101:1">101:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. Ka waiatatia e
ahau te mahi tohu me te whakawa tika: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe, e
Ihowa.

<span id="an_101:2">101:2</span> Ka ata whakahaere ahau i ahau i runga i
te ara tika. A hea koe haere mai ai ki ahau? Ka haereere ahau i roto i
toku whare i runga i te ngakau tapatahi.

<span id="an_101:3">101:3</span> E kore te mea tutua e waiho e ahau i
mua i oku kanohi; e kino ana ahau ki te mahi a te hunga peka ke: e kore
e piri ki ahau.

<span id="an_101:4">101:4</span> Ka mawehe atu i ahau te ngakau parori
ke: e kore ahau e mohio ki te mea kino.

<span id="an_101:5">101:5</span> Ko te tangata e ngautuara puku ana ki
tona hoa ka whakangaromia e ahau: e kore ahau e aro ki te tangata kanohi
whakakake, ki te tangata ngakau whakapakari.

<span id="an_101:6">101:6</span> Kei runga i nga mea pono o te whenua
oku kanohi, kia noho ai ratou ki ahau: ko te tangata e haere ana i te
ara tika, ka mahi tena ki ahau.

<span id="an_101:7">101:7</span> E kore e noho ki toku whare te kaimahi
i te hianga: e kore e tu ki toku aroaro te tangata korero teka.

<span id="an_101:8">101:8</span> I tenei ata, i tenei ata, ka
whakangaromia e ahau nga tangata kikino katoa o te whenua: kia hatepea
atu ai i te pa o te Atua te hunga katoa e mahi ana i te kino.

<span id="an_102:1">102:1</span> ¶ He inoi na te ngakau mamae, i a ia e
pehia ana, a maringi a wai ana tana tangi ki te aroaro o Ihowa.
Whakarongo ki taku inoi, e Ihowa, kia puta atu taku tangi ki a koe.

<span id="an_102:2">102:2</span> Kaua e huna tou mata ki ahau i te ra e
pouri ai ahau; whakatitahatia mai tou taringa ki ahau: hohoro te
whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau i te ra e karanga ai ahau.

<span id="an_102:3">102:3</span> Ka memeha hoki oku ra ano he paoa: ka
kaia oku wheua ano he motumotu.

<span id="an_102:4">102:4</span> Kua pakia toku ngakau, kua memenge, ano
he tarutaru; i wareware ai ahau ki te kai i taku taro.

<span id="an_102:5">102:5</span> Piri tonu oku iwi ki toku kiri i toku
reo aue.

<span id="an_102:6">102:6</span> He rite ahau ki te matuku i te koraha,
ki te koukou i te wahi mokemoke.

<span id="an_102:7">102:7</span> Mataara tonu ahau; toku rite kei te
pihoihoi mokemoke i runga i te tuanui.

<span id="an_102:8">102:8</span> E tawai ana oku hoariri ki ahau i te ra
roa; ko te hunga e porangirangi ana mai ki ahau, ko ahau ta ratou oati.

<span id="an_102:9">102:9</span> Kainga ana e ahau te pungarehu ano he
taro: whakananua iho toku wai inu ki te roimata.

<span id="an_102:10">102:10</span> I tou riri hoki, i tou weriweri; nau
hoki ahau i hapai ake, a taia atu ano ahau e koe.

<span id="an_102:11">102:11</span> He rite oku ra ki te atarangi e
whakawairua kau ana: a kua memenge ahau ano he tarutaru.

<span id="an_102:12">102:12</span> ¶ Ko koe ia, e Ihowa, ka mau tonu ake
ake, ka maharatia ano koe e nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_102:13">102:13</span> Tera koe e whakatika, e aroha ki a
Hiona; kua taka mai hoki te wa, ae ra, te tino wa, hei atawhainga i a
ia.

<span id="an_102:14">102:14</span> E manakohia ana hoki e au pononga ona
kohatu, e awangawanga ana ki tona puehu.

<span id="an_102:15">102:15</span> Penei ka wehingia te ingoa o Ihowa e
nga tauiwi, tou kororia hoki e nga kingi katoa o te whenua.

<span id="an_102:16">102:16</span> Na Ihowa hoki i hanga a Hiona, kua
kitea ia i tona kororia.

<span id="an_102:17">102:17</span> Kua tahuri ia ki te inoi a te
rawakore: kihai i whakahawea ki ta ratou inoi.

<span id="an_102:18">102:18</span> Ka tuhituhia tenei mo to muri
whakatupuranga: a ka whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa te iwi meake hanga.

<span id="an_102:19">102:19</span> Mona i titiro iho i te tiketike o
tona wahi tapu: i titiro iho a Ihowa i te rangi ki te whenua;

<span id="an_102:20">102:20</span> Ki te whakarongo ki te aue a te
herehere, ki te wewete i te hunga kua motuhia mo te mate;

<span id="an_102:21">102:21</span> Kia whakapuakina ai te ingo o Ihowa i
Hiona, me te whakamoemiti ki a ia i Hiruharama;

<span id="an_102:22">102:22</span> I te huihuinga o nga iwi, o nga
kingitanga, ki te mahi ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_102:23">102:23</span> ¶ Whakangoikoretia iho e ia toku kaha
i te ara: kua torutoru i a ia oku ra.

<span id="an_102:24">102:24</span> I mea ahau, E toku Atua, kaua ahau e
tangohia i waenganui o oku ra: kei nga whakatupuranga katoa ou tau.

<span id="an_102:25">102:25</span> Nonamata te whenua i whakaturia ai e
koe, a he mahi nga rangi na ou ringa.

<span id="an_102:26">102:26</span> Ko era e hemo atu, ko koe ia e mau
tonu: ae ra, ka tawhitotia katoatia me he weweru; ka whakaputaia ketia
ratou e koe ano he kakahu, a ka whakaputaia ketia.

<span id="an_102:27">102:27</span> Ko koe ia, ko koe tonu, kahore hoki
he mutunga o ou tau.

<span id="an_102:28">102:28</span> Ka whai nohoanga nga tama a au
pononga, ka pumau o ratou uri ki tou aroaro.

<span id="an_103:1">103:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e
toku wairua; e nga mea katoa i roto i ahau, whakapaingia tona ingoa
tapu.

<span id="an_103:2">103:2</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua,
kei wareware hoki ki ana painga katoa.

<span id="an_103:3">103:3</span> Ko ia te muru nei i ou kino katoa; te
rongo a nei i ou mate katoa.

<span id="an_103:4">103:4</span> Ko ia te hoko nei i tou ora kei ngaro;
te karauna nei i a koe ki te atawhai, ki te aroha.

<span id="an_103:5">103:5</span> Nana nei i makona ai tou mangai i nga
mea papai; i hou ai tou taitamarikitanga, i rite ai ki to te ekara.

<span id="an_103:6">103:6</span> ¶ Ka puta i a Ihowa nga mahi tika, me
te whakawa tika ki te hunga katoa e tukinotia ana.

<span id="an_103:7">103:7</span> I whakaakona e ia ana ara ki a Mohi,
ana mahi ki nga tama a Iharaira.

<span id="an_103:8">103:8</span> Ki tonu a Ihowa i te aroha me te
atawhai, he puhoi ki te riri, he nui hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_103:9">103:9</span> E kore ia e whakatupuehupehu tonu, e
kore ano e mauahara ake ake.

<span id="an_103:10">103:10</span> Kihai i rite ki o tatou hara ana
meatanga ki a tatou: kihai ano i rite ki o tatou kino ana utu mai ki a
tatou.

<span id="an_103:11">103:11</span> He rite hoki ki te rangi e tiketike
ake ana i te whenua, pera tonu te nui o tana mahi tohu ki te hunga e
wehi ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_103:12">103:12</span> Pera i te matara o te rawhiti i te
uru, pera tonu tana whakamataratanga atu i a tatou mahi tutu i a tatou.

<span id="an_103:13">103:13</span> E aroha ana te matua ki ana tamariki,
pera tonu to Ihowa aroha ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_103:14">103:14</span> E matau ana hoki ia ki to tatou ahua,
e mahara ana he puehu tatou.

<span id="an_103:15">103:15</span> Ko te tangata ia, rite tonu ona ra ki
o te tarutaru: kei te puawai o te mara, ko tona ngawhatanga.

<span id="an_103:16">103:16</span> E rarungatia ana hoki e te hau, a kua
kahore; kahore hoki e mohiotia a muri e tona wahi.

<span id="an_103:17">103:17</span> Tena ko te mahi tohu a Ihowa no tua
whakarere, a ake tonu ake, ki te hunga e wehi ana ki a ia: tona tika
hoki ki nga uri o nga tamariki;

<span id="an_103:18">103:18</span> Ki te hunga e pupuri ana i tana
kawenata, ki te hunga hoki e mahara ana ki ana ako kia mahia.

<span id="an_103:19">103:19</span> ¶ Kua oti i a Ihowa tona torona te
whakatu ki nga rangi; a e kawanatia ana nga mea katoa e tona kingitanga.

<span id="an_103:20">103:20</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana anahera,
e hira nei te kaha, e whakarite nei i tana kupu, e whakarongo nei ki
tona reo ina korero.

<span id="an_103:21">103:21</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana mano
katoa, e ana minita e mahi nei i tana e pai ai.

<span id="an_103:22">103:22</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e ana mahi
katoa i nga wahi katoa o tona kingitanga: whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku
wairua.

<span id="an_104:1">104:1</span> ¶ Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e toku wairua.
E Ihowa, e toku Atua, he nui rawa koe; he honore, he kororia ou kakahu.

<span id="an_104:2">104:2</span> E roropi nei i te marama ki a koe ano
he kakahu, e hora nei i nga rangi ano he kakahu tauarai.

<span id="an_104:3">104:3</span> E whakanoho nei i nga kurupae o ona
ruma ki nga wai: e mea nei i nga kapua hei hariata mona: e haere nei i
runga i nga pakau o te hau.

<span id="an_104:4">104:4</span> E mea nei i nga hau hei karere mana, i
te mura ahi hei kaimahi mana.

<span id="an_104:5">104:5</span> Nana nei i whakatu te whenua ki runga
ki ona turanga, kei nekenekehia ake ake.

<span id="an_104:6">104:6</span> Nau ano i hipoki ki te rire hei kakahu:
tu ana nga wai i runga i nga maunga.

<span id="an_104:7">104:7</span> Rere ana ratou i tau riri: tahuti tonu
atu i te reo o tau whatitiri;

<span id="an_104:8">104:8</span> Puke ake ana ra nga maunga, heke iho
ana ma nga whawharua ki te wahi i whakaritea e koe mo ratou.

<span id="an_104:9">104:9</span> Kua whakatakotoria e koe he rohe kei
koni mai ratou, kei hoki mai hei taupoki mo te whenua.

<span id="an_104:10">104:10</span> ¶ Nana i tono nga puna ki roto ki nga
awaawa, e rere nei i waenga o nga puke.

<span id="an_104:11">104:11</span> Hei wai mo nga kirehe katoa o te
parae: na noa te matewai o nga kaihe mohoao.

<span id="an_104:12">104:12</span> Kei reira nga nohoanga o nga manu o
te rangi, e korihi nei i roto i nga manga.

<span id="an_104:13">104:13</span> He mea whakamakuku nana nga puke i
ona ruma: ka makona te whenua i nga hua o au mahi.

<span id="an_104:14">104:14</span> Ko ia hei whakatupu i te tarutaru ma
te kararehe, i te otaota hei mea ma te tangata; kia whakaputaina ake ai
he taro i te whenua;

<span id="an_104:15">104:15</span> He waina hei whakahari i te ngakau o
te tangata, he hinu e piata ai tona mata, me te taro hei whakakaha i te
ngakau o te tangata.

<span id="an_104:16">104:16</span> Ki tonu i te wai nga rakau a Ihowa,
nga hita o Repanona i whakatokia e ia.

<span id="an_104:17">104:17</span> Hanga ake e nga manu he ohanga ki
reira: te taaka, ko nga kauri tona whare.

<span id="an_104:18">104:18</span> Hei piringa nga puke tiketike mo nga
koati mohoao: nga kohatu mo nga rapeti.

<span id="an_104:19">104:19</span> ¶ I hanga e ia te marama hei tohu
taima: e matau ana te ra ki tona torengitanga.

<span id="an_104:20">104:20</span> Ko koe hei whakapouri, a kua po: na
ngoki mai ana nga kirehe katoa o te ngahere.

<span id="an_104:21">104:21</span> Ko nga kuao raiona ngengere ana
ratou, he mea kai, he rapu kai ma ratou i te Atua.

<span id="an_104:22">104:22</span> Ko te putanga mai o te ra ka poto atu
ratou, takoto ana i o ratou kuhunga.

<span id="an_104:23">104:23</span> Ko te tangata ka haere ki ana hanga,
ki tana mahi, a ahiahi noa.

<span id="an_104:24">104:24</span> Ano te tini o au mahi, e Ihowa! he
mohio rawa tau mahi i aua mea katoa; ki tonu te whenua i au taonga.

<span id="an_104:25">104:25</span> Kei ko ra ko te moana, tona nui
tuauriuri: kei reira nga mea ngokingoki e kore e taea te tatau, nga
kirehe hoki, ana nonohi, ana nunui.

<span id="an_104:26">104:26</span> Kei reira nga kaipuke e teretere ana:
kei reira taua rewiatana i hanga e koe hei takaro ki reira.

<span id="an_104:27">104:27</span> E tatari katoa ana enei ki a koe, kia
hoatu e koe te kai ma ratou i te wa e tika ai.

<span id="an_104:28">104:28</span> Ko tau e hoatu ai ma ratou, kohikohia
ana e ratou: te wherahanga o tou ringa, makona tonu ratou i te pai.

<span id="an_104:29">104:29</span> Ko te hunanga o tou mata, pororaru
ana ratou: ka kapohia e koe to ratou manawa, ka marere ratou, a ka hoki
ano ki to ratou puehu.

<span id="an_104:30">104:30</span> Ko tau tononga mai i tou wairua, kua
hanga ratou; a whakahoutia ana e koe te mata o te whenua.

<span id="an_104:31">104:31</span> ¶ Kia whai kororia a Ihowa ake ake,
kia hari a Ihowa ki ana mahi:

<span id="an_104:32">104:32</span> Tana tirohanga iho ki te whenua, ru
ana: kua pa ki nga puke, na pongere ana.

<span id="an_104:33">104:33</span> Ka waiata ahau ki a Ihowa i ahau e
ora ana: ka himene ki toku Atua i ahau ano i te ao nei.

<span id="an_104:34">104:34</span> Kia reka toku whakaaronga ki a ia, ka
hari ahau ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_104:35">104:35</span> Kia moti nga tangata hara i runga i
te whenua, ko te hunga kino kia poto katoa atu. Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e
toku wairua. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_105:1">105:1</span> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, karanga atu
ki tona ingoa: whakapuakina ana mahi ki waenganui o nga iwi.

<span id="an_105:2">105:2</span> Waiata ki a ia, himene ki a ia:
korerotia ana mahi whakamiharo katoa.

<span id="an_105:3">105:3</span> Whakamanamana ki tona ingoa tapu: kia
hari te ngakau o te hunga e rapu ana i a Ihowa.

<span id="an_105:4">105:4</span> Rapua a Ihowa me tona kaha: rapua
tonutia tona mata, ake ake.

<span id="an_105:5">105:5</span> Maharatia ana mahi whakamiharo i mahia
e ia; ana merekara me nga whakaritenga a tona mangai,

<span id="an_105:6">105:6</span> E nga uri o Aperahama, o tana pononga,
e nga tama a Hakopa, e ana i whiriwhiri ai.

<span id="an_105:7">105:7</span> Ko Ihowa ia, ko to tatou Atua; kei te
whenua katoa ana whakaritenga.

<span id="an_105:8">105:8</span> ¶ Mahara tonu ia ki tana kawenata ake
ake, ki te kupu i kiia iho e ia ki te mano o nga whakatupuranga.

<span id="an_105:9">105:9</span> Ki tana i whakarite ai ki a Aperahama,
ki tana oati hoki ki a Ihaka;

<span id="an_105:10">105:10</span> A whakapumautia iho e ia hei tikanga
ki a Hakopa, hei kawenata mau tonu ki a Iharaira.

<span id="an_105:11">105:11</span> I a ia ra i mea, Ka hoatu e ahau ki a
koe te whenua o Kanaana hei wahi pumau mo koutou.

<span id="an_105:12">105:12</span> I te mea he hunga torutoru ratou: ae
ra, he iti rawa, he manene ano ki reira.

<span id="an_105:13">105:13</span> I a ratou e haereere ana i tenei iwi
ki tera atu iwi, i tetahi rangatiratanga ki tetahi iwi ke;

<span id="an_105:14">105:14</span> Kihai ratou i tukua e ia kia
tukinotia e te tangata: he whakaaro ano ki a ratou i riria ai e ia nga
kingi.

<span id="an_105:15">105:15</span> I mea ia, Kei pa ki aku i whakawahi
ai: kei kino ki aku poropiti.

<span id="an_105:16">105:16</span> I karangatia e ia te matekai ki te
whenua: whati katoa i a ia te tokotoko, ara te taro.

<span id="an_105:17">105:17</span> I tonoa e ia he tangata i mua i a
ratou; i hokona a Hohepa hei pononga:

<span id="an_105:18">105:18</span> I whakamamaetia ona waewae ki te
mekameka: takoto ana ia i te rino;

<span id="an_105:19">105:19</span> A puta noa tana kupu:
whakamatautauria ana ia e te kupu a Ihowa.

<span id="an_105:20">105:20</span> I tono te kingi, a wetekina ana ia;
ara te kingi o nga iwi, a tukua ana ia.

<span id="an_105:21">105:21</span> A meinga ana ia e ia hei ariki mo
tona whare, hei rangatira mo ona taonga katoa;

<span id="an_105:22">105:22</span> Hei herehere i ana rangatira ua pai
ia, hei ako i ana kaumatua ki te whakaaro.

<span id="an_105:23">105:23</span> I haere mai ano a Iharaira ki Ihipa:
a noho ana a Hakopa ki te whenua o Hama.

<span id="an_105:24">105:24</span> Na ka tino whakanuia e ia tana iwi: a
ka meinga ratou kia kaha ake i o ratou hoariri.

<span id="an_105:25">105:25</span> ¶ I whakakoarotia e ia to ratou
ngakau kia kino ki tana iwi, kia mahi lhianga ki ana pononga.

<span id="an_105:26">105:26</span> I tonoa e ia a Mohi, tana pononga,
raua ko Arona, ko tana i whiriwhiri ai.

<span id="an_105:27">105:27</span> Whakaputaina ana e raua ana tohu i
waenganui i a ratou, he merekara i te whenua o Hama.

<span id="an_105:28">105:28</span> I tukua e ia te pouri, a kua pouri:
kihai ano ratou i whakakeke ki ana kupu.

<span id="an_105:29">105:29</span> I whakaputaia ketia e ia o ratou wai
hei toto; a mate ake i a ia a ratou ngohi.

<span id="an_105:30">105:30</span> I whakangahue ake to ratou whenua i
te poroka, i roto i nga whare moenga o o ratou kingi.

<span id="an_105:31">105:31</span> I whai kupu ia, a puta ana mai nga
pokai namu: me te kutu i o ratou kainga.

<span id="an_105:32">105:32</span> I tukua iho e ia ki a ratou te whatu
hei ua, me te ahi mura ki to ratou whenua.

<span id="an_105:33">105:33</span> I pakia ano e ia a ratou waina me a
ratou piki; a whatiwhatiia ana e ia nga rakau o o ratou kainga.

<span id="an_105:34">105:34</span> I korero ia, a puta ana mai te
mawhitiwhiti me te moka, te taea te tatau.

<span id="an_105:35">105:35</span> A kainga katoatia ana nga otaota o to
ratou whenua; pau ake nga hua o to ratou oneone.

<span id="an_105:36">105:36</span> I whakamatea katoatia ano hoki e ia
nga matamua o to ratou whenua, te muanga o to ratou kaha.

<span id="an_105:37">105:37</span> A whakaputaina mai ana ratou e ia, me
te hiriwa, me te koura, kahore hoki he mea tuoi i roto i ana iwi.

<span id="an_105:38">105:38</span> Na hari ana a Ihipa i to ratou
haerenga; i mau hoki to ratou wehi ki a ratou.

<span id="an_105:39">105:39</span> I horahia e ia te kapua hei hipoki,
me te ahi hei whakamarama i te po.

<span id="an_105:40">105:40</span> I inoi ratou, a homai ana e ia te
koitareke; a ka makona ratou i te taro o te rangi.

<span id="an_105:41">105:41</span> I wahia e ia te kohatu, a ka pakaru
mai nga wai: rere ana i nga wahi maroke, koia ano kei te awa.

<span id="an_105:42">105:42</span> I mahara hoki ia ki tana kuputapu, ki
a Aperahama ano, ki tana pononga.

<span id="an_105:43">105:43</span> A whakaputaina mai ana e ia tana iwi
i runga i te hari, ana i whiriwhiri ai i runga i te koa.

<span id="an_105:44">105:44</span> A homai ana e ia ki a ratou nga
whenua o nga tauiwi: a riro ana i a ratou nga mauiuitanga o te iwi;

<span id="an_105:45">105:45</span> Kia puritia ai e ratou ana tikanga,
kia mau ai ki ana ture. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_106:1">106:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakawhetai
ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki ia: he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_106:2">106:2</span> Me wai e korero nga mahi nunui a Ihowa:
e whakakite katoa nga whakamoemiti ki a ia?

<span id="an_106:3">106:3</span> Ka hari te hunga e mau ana ki te
whakarite tika; me te kaimahi i te tika i nga wa katoa.

<span id="an_106:4">106:4</span> Maharatia mai ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite
ki tau manako ki tau iwi: tirotirohia mai ahau i runga i tau
whakaoranga.

<span id="an_106:5">106:5</span> Kia kite ai ahau i te pai o au i
whiriwhiri ai: kia koa ai, koa tahi me tau iwi; kia whakamanamana tahi
ai me tou kainga tupu.

<span id="an_106:6">106:6</span> ¶ Kua hara tahi matou me o matou matua,
kua mahi matou i te kino, i te mea he.

<span id="an_106:7">106:7</span> Kihai o matou matua i mohio ki au mea
whakamiharo i Ihipa, kihai hoki i mahara ki te tini o au arohatanga;
engari ia i whakatoi ratou ki a koe i te moana, ae, i te Moana Whero.

<span id="an_106:8">106:8</span> Otira whakaorangia ana ratou e ia, he
whakaaro ki tona ingoa, kia matauria ai tona kaha.

<span id="an_106:9">106:9</span> I riria ano e ia te Moana Whero, a kua
maroke: na arahina ana ratou e ia i nga rire, ano ko waenga koraha.

<span id="an_106:10">106:10</span> Na whakaorangia ake ratou e ia i te
ringa o te tangata i kino ki a ratou; a hokona ana ratou i roto i te
ringa o te hoariri.

<span id="an_106:11">106:11</span> A taupokina ana e nga wai o ratou
hoariri, hore rawa tetahi morehu.

<span id="an_106:12">106:12</span> Na whakapono ana ratou ki ana kupu: a
waiata ana i te whakamoemiti ki a ia.

<span id="an_106:13">106:13</span> ¶ Hohoro tonu to ratou wareware ki
ana mahi: kihai i taria e ratou tona whakaaro:

<span id="an_106:14">106:14</span> Engari i whakaputa nui i o ratou
hiahia i te tahora; whakamatautau ana ratou i te Atua i te koraha.

<span id="an_106:15">106:15</span> Na ka hoatu e ia ta ratou i inoi ai;
otira i tukua atu e ia te hiroki ki to ratou wairua.

<span id="an_106:16">106:16</span> I hae hoki ratou ki a Mohi i te puni,
ki a Arona ano, ki te tangata tapu a Ihowa.

<span id="an_106:17">106:17</span> Ko te hamamatanga o te whenua, na
horomia ana a Ratana; a taupokina iho te ropu o Apirama.

<span id="an_106:18">106:18</span> A mura ana te ahi i to ratou ropu;
wera ana i te mura te hunga kino.

<span id="an_106:19">106:19</span> I hanga e ratou he kuao kau ki
Horepa, a koropiko ana ki te whakapakoko i whakarewaina.

<span id="an_106:20">106:20</span> Koia i whitia ai e ratou to ratou
kororia mo te mea i rite ki te puru kai tarutaru.

<span id="an_106:21">106:21</span> Wareware ake i a ratou te Atua, to
ratou kaiwhakaora, i mahi nei i nga mea nunui ki Ihipa.

<span id="an_106:22">106:22</span> I nga mahi whakamiharo ki te whenua o
Hama, i nga mea whakamataku ki te Moana Whero.

<span id="an_106:23">106:23</span> Na ka mea ia, kia whakangaromia
ratou, me i kaua a Mohi, tana i whiriwhiri ai, te tu ki tona aroaro i te
takiwa, hei papare ake i tona riri, kei huna ratou e ia.

<span id="an_106:24">106:24</span> Ae ra, i whakahawea ratou ki te
whenua ahuareka; kihai ratou i whakapono ki tana kupu;

<span id="an_106:25">106:25</span> Heoi amuamu ana i roto i o ratou
teneti, kihai i whakarongo ki te reo o Ihowa.

<span id="an_106:26">106:26</span> Na reira ka ara tona ringa ki a
ratou, ki te turaki i a ratou i te koraha;

<span id="an_106:27">106:27</span> Ki te turaki i o ratou uri i roto i
nga iwi: ki te whakamarara i a ratou ki nga whenua.

<span id="an_106:28">106:28</span> I whakauru atu hoki ratou ki a
Paarapeoro: a kai ana i nga patunga tapu ma nga mea mate.

<span id="an_106:29">106:29</span> Koia i whakapataritari ai ratou i a
ia ki a ratou hanga kia riri; a pakaru ana mai te mate uruta ki a ratou.

<span id="an_106:30">106:30</span> Na ko te whakatikanga ake o Pinehaha,
ki te whakaputa whakawa: a mutu iho te mate.

<span id="an_106:31">106:31</span> I kiia ai ia he tika i nga
whakatupuranga katoa ake ake.

<span id="an_106:32">106:32</span> I whakapataritari ano ratou i a ia ki
nga wai o Meripa; na hemanawa ana a Mohi mo ratou:

<span id="an_106:33">106:33</span> Na ratou hoki i whakatoi tona wairua,
