i he ai te kupu a ona ngutu.

<span id="an_106:34">106:34</span> ¶ Kihai ratou i whakangaro i nga iwi
i kiia nei e Ihowa ki a ratou;

<span id="an_106:35">106:35</span> Heoi uru ana ki roto ki nga tauiwi, a
ako ana i a ratou mahi.

<span id="an_106:36">106:36</span> I mahi hoki ratou ki a ratou
whakapakoko, i mahangatia ai ratou.

<span id="an_106:37">106:37</span> Ae, i patua e ratou a ratou tama me a
ratou tamahine ma nga atua maori;

<span id="an_106:38">106:38</span> I whakahekea hoki te toto harakore,
nga toto o a ratou tama, o a ratou tamahine, i patua nei e ratou ma nga
whakapakoko o Kanaana; a poke iho te whenua i te toto.

<span id="an_106:39">106:39</span> Na poke iho ratou i a ratou mahi: a
puremu ana ki a ratou mahi.

<span id="an_106:40">106:40</span> Koia i mura ai te riri o Ihowa ki
tana iwi; a whakarihariha ana ia ki tona kainga tupu.

<span id="an_106:41">106:41</span> A tukua ana ratou e ia ki te ringa o
nga tauiwi; waiho ana te hunga i kino ki a ratou hei rangatira mo ratou.

<span id="an_106:42">106:42</span> Na ka tukinotia ratou e o ratou
hoariri: ka pehia ki raro i o ratou ringa.

<span id="an_106:43">106:43</span> He maha ana whakaoranga i a ratou: ko
ratou ia i whakatoi ki a ia i o ratou whakaaro, a whakaititia ana i ta
ratou kino.

<span id="an_106:44">106:44</span> Ahakoa ra, i titiro ia ki to ratou
matenga, i tona rongonga i ta ratou tangi:

<span id="an_106:45">106:45</span> I mahara hoki ia ki tana kawenata ki
a ratou, a rite tonu ki te tini o ana mahi aroha te putanga ketanga o
ona whakaaro:

<span id="an_106:46">106:46</span> I meinga hoki ratou e ia kia arohaina
e te hunga katoa i whakaraua atu ai ratou.

<span id="an_106:47">106:47</span> Whakaorangia matou, e Ihowa, e to
matou Atua, kohikohia matou i roto i nga tauiwi: kia whakawhetai ai ki
tou ingoa tapu, kia whakamanamana ai ki tou whakamoemiti.

<span id="an_106:48">106:48</span> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, te Atua o
Iharaira, i tua whakarere ano, a ake ake. A kia mea katoa te iwi, Amine.
Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_107:1">107:1</span> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, he pai hoki
ia: he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_107:2">107:2</span> Kia pena ano te korero a te hunga i
hokona e Ihowa, i hokona nei e ia i roto i te ringa o te hoariri;

<span id="an_107:3">107:3</span> I kohikohia nei i nga whenua, i te
rawhiti, i te uru, i te raki, i te tonga.

<span id="an_107:4">107:4</span> I haereere ratou i te koraha i te wahi
mokemoke, te kitea tetahi pa hei nohoanga.

<span id="an_107:5">107:5</span> I matekai ratou, i matewai: hemo noa to
ratou wairua i roto i a ratou.

<span id="an_107:6">107:6</span> Na ka tangi ratou ki a Ihowa i to ratou
pouri: a whakaorangia ana ratou e ia i o ratou mate.

<span id="an_107:7">107:7</span> A arahina ana e ia ra te ara tika; kia
haere ai ki te pa hei nohoanga.

<span id="an_107:8">107:8</span> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a
Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!

<span id="an_107:9">107:9</span> E whakamakonatia ana hoki e ia te
wairua hiahia: ko te wairua hiakai, whakakiia ana e ia ki te pai.

<span id="an_107:10">107:10</span> ¶ Ko te hunga i noho i te pouri, i te
atarangi o te mate: he mea here ki te mamae, ki te rino;

<span id="an_107:11">107:11</span> Mo ratou i tutu ki nga kupu a te
Atua, i whakahawea ki te whakaaro o te Runga Rawa;

<span id="an_107:12">107:12</span> Koia i pehia iho ai e ia o ratou
ngakau ki te mahi: hinga iho ratou, kahore hoki he kaiawhina.

<span id="an_107:13">107:13</span> Na ka tangi ratou ki a Ihowa i to
ratou pouri; a ka whakaorangia ratou e ia i o ratou mate.

<span id="an_107:14">107:14</span> Whakaputaina mai ana ratou e ia i te
pouri, i te atarangi o te mate; motumotuhia ana o ratou here.

<span id="an_107:15">107:15</span> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a
Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!

<span id="an_107:16">107:16</span> Kua tukitukia hoki e ia nga tatau
parahi: kua tapahia e ia nga tutaki rino, motu rawa.

<span id="an_107:17">107:17</span> ¶ Ko nga kuware, na a ratou mahi
tutu, na o ratou kino, i pakia ai ratou.

<span id="an_107:18">107:18</span> Ka wetiweti to ratou wairua ki nga
kai katoa; a ka whakatata ratou ki nga kuwaha o te mate.

<span id="an_107:19">107:19</span> Na ka tangi ki a Ihowa i to ratou
pouri, a ka whakaorangia ratou e ia i o ratou mate.

<span id="an_107:20">107:20</span> Tukua mai ana e ia tana kupu, a
rongoatia ana ratou: a whakaputaina ana ratou i o ratou ngaromanga.

<span id="an_107:21">107:21</span> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a
Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!

<span id="an_107:22">107:22</span> Kia tukua ano e ratou te whakahere,
ara te whakamoemiti; kia whakapuaki i ana mahi i runga i te hari.

<span id="an_107:23">107:23</span> ¶ Ko te hunga e haere ana ki raro, ki
te moana, i runga kaipuke, a e whai mahi ana i nga wai nunui,

<span id="an_107:24">107:24</span> Ko ratou e kite i nga mahi a Ihowa, i
ana mahi whakamiharo i te rire.

<span id="an_107:25">107:25</span> Puta kau tana kupu, kua maranga te
tupuhi, mana e whakatutu ona ngaru.

<span id="an_107:26">107:26</span> Ka kake ratou ki runga ki te rangi,
ka heke ano ki raro ki te rire: ngohe noa o ratou wairua i te pawera.

<span id="an_107:27">107:27</span> Ka tiu ratou, ka hurorirori ano he
tangata e haurangi ana; a kahore he mahara i toe.

<span id="an_107:28">107:28</span> Heoi ka tangi ki a Ihowa i to ratou
hemanawa: a whakaorangia ana ratou i o ratou mate.

<span id="an_107:29">107:29</span> Meinga ana e ia te tupuhi kia marino,
ona ngaru kia mariri.

<span id="an_107:30">107:30</span> Na ka koa ratou, no te mea ka marie:
a ka kawea ratou e ia ki te tauranga i hiahia ai ratou.

<span id="an_107:31">107:31</span> Aue! me i whakapaingia e te tangata a
Ihowa mo tona atawhai, mo ana mahi whakamiharo ki nga tama a te tangata!

<span id="an_107:32">107:32</span> Kia whakanui hoki ratou i a ia i roto
i te whakaminenga o te iwi; kia whakamoemiti ki a ia i roto i te
nohoanga kaumatua.

<span id="an_107:33">107:33</span> ¶ Ko ia hei mea i nga awa hei koraha,
i nga puputanga wai hei oneone maroke;

<span id="an_107:34">107:34</span> I te whenua whai hua, kia titohea, mo
te hara o te hunga e noho ana i reira.

<span id="an_107:35">107:35</span> Ko ia hei mea i te koraha hei
harotoroto wai, i te whenua maroke hei puputanga wai.

<span id="an_107:36">107:36</span> A whakanohoia iho e ia te hunga
matekai ki reira, hanga ai i tetahi pa hei nohoanga;

<span id="an_107:37">107:37</span> Hei rui mara, hei whakato mara waina,
e tupu ai, e maha ai nga hua.

<span id="an_107:38">107:38</span> Ko ia ano hei manaaki i a ratou, no
ka nui rawa; kahore hoki e tukua kia torutoru haere a ratou kararehe.

<span id="an_107:39">107:39</span> Na kua iti haere ano ratou, kua piko
i te tukino, i te he, i te pouri.

<span id="an_107:40">107:40</span> E ringihia ana e ia te whakahawea ki
runga ki nga rangatira: e meinga ana kia hehe i te ururua, i te wahi
kahore nei he ara;

<span id="an_107:41">107:41</span> Otira kei te whakateitei ia i te
rawakore ki runga i te mamae, kei te mea i ona hapu kia rite ki te kahui
hipi.

<span id="an_107:42">107:42</span> Ka kite nga tangata tika, a ka hari;
ko nga he katoa hoki, kipia ake te mangai.

<span id="an_107:43">107:43</span> Ko te tangata whakaaro nui ka mahara
ki enei mea, a ka mohio ratou ki te aroha o Ihowa.

<span id="an_108:1">108:1</span> ¶ He waiata, he himene na Rawiri. Pumau
tonu toku ngakau, e te Atua; ka waiata ahau, ae ra, ka himene ahau, me
toku kororia ano.

<span id="an_108:2">108:2</span> E ara, e te hatere, e te hapa: ka ara
wawe ano ahau.

<span id="an_108:3">108:3</span> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa,
i waenganui i nga iwi: ka himene ki a koe i waenganui i nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_108:4">108:4</span> He nui atu hoki tau mahi tohu i nga
rangi, a ko tou pono tutuki noa atu ki nga kapua.

<span id="an_108:5">108:5</span> Kia whakanuia koe, e te Atua, ki runga
atu i nga rangi: hei runga atu i te whenua katoa tou kororia.

<span id="an_108:6">108:6</span> ¶ Kia puta tau i aroha ai, ma tou ringa
matau matou e whakaora, a whakahokia mai he kupu ki a matou.

<span id="an_108:7">108:7</span> Kua korero te Atua i runga i tona tapu:
Ka hari ahau, ka kotikoti i Hekeme, ka roherohe i te raorao o Hukota.

<span id="an_108:8">108:8</span> Noku Kireara; noku a Manahi; ko
Eparaima ano hoki te kaha o toku matenga; ko Hura taku hepeta.

<span id="an_108:9">108:9</span> Ko Moapa taku oko horoi; ka maka e ahau
toku hu ki runga ki Eroma: ka whakamanamana ahau ki Pirihitia.

<span id="an_108:10">108:10</span> Ma wai ahau e kawe ki te pa
tuwatawata? Ko wai nana ahau i arahi ki Eroma?

<span id="an_108:11">108:11</span> He teka ianei kua panga matou e koe,
e te Atua? kahore hoki koe, e te Atua, e haere tahi me o matou taua.

<span id="an_108:12">108:12</span> Homai ki a matou he awhina ki te
hoariri: he teka kau noa hoki te awhina a te tangata.

<span id="an_108:13">108:13</span> Ma te Atua tatou ka toa ai: mana hoki
e takahi ki raro o tatou hoa whawhai.

<span id="an_109:1">109:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene
na Rawiri. E te Atua, e whakamoemiti nei ahau, kei wahangu koe:

<span id="an_109:2">109:2</span> Kua puaki hoki te mangai o te tangata
kino me te mangai o te tangata tinihanga, ki te he moku: he teka o ratou
arero, e korero nei moku.

<span id="an_109:3">109:3</span> I karapotia hoki ahau e ratou ki nga
kupu mauahara, a i whawhai takekore ki ahau.

<span id="an_109:4">109:4</span> Mo toku aroha he riri ta ratou
whakautu: ko ahau ia, he inoi taku.

<span id="an_109:5">109:5</span> E homai ana e ratou ki ahau he kino mo
te pai, he mauahara mo toku aroha.

<span id="an_109:6">109:6</span> ¶ Meinga he tangata kino hei rangatira
mona; kia tu he hoariri ki tona ringa matau.

<span id="an_109:7">109:7</span> Kia tau te he ki a ia, ina whakawakia:
kia waiho ano tana inoi hei hara.

<span id="an_109:8">109:8</span> Kia torutoru ona ra; kia riro tana mahi
tirotiro i tetahi atu.

<span id="an_109:9">109:9</span> Kia pania ana tamariki, kia pouarutia
hoki tana wahine.

<span id="an_109:10">109:10</span> Kia kopikopiko noa ana tamariki,
pinono ai: kia rapu kai hoki ma ratou i o ratou wahi mokemoke.

<span id="an_109:11">109:11</span> Kia haoa e te kaituku moni ana mea
katoa; kia pahuatia hoki e nga tangata iwi ke ana mauiuitanga.

<span id="an_109:12">109:12</span> Kaua tetahi hei hoatu noa i te aroha
ki a ia: kaua hoki tetahi hei atawhai i ana pani.

<span id="an_109:13">109:13</span> Kia hatepea putia ona uri: a i to
muri whakatupuranga kia horoia rawatia atu o ratou ingoa.

<span id="an_109:14">109:14</span> Kia maharatia e Ihowa te kino o ona
matua: kei murua hoki te hara o tona whaea.

<span id="an_109:15">109:15</span> Kia mau tonu ki te aroaro o Ihowa:
kia hatepea atu ai e ia te maharatanga ki a ratou i runga i te whenua.

<span id="an_109:16">109:16</span> Mona kihai i mahara ki te mahi tohu:
heoi tukino ana ia i te ware, i te rawakore, i te hunga ngakau maru, kia
patua ai ratou.

<span id="an_109:17">109:17</span> Ae ra, i pai ia ki te kanga, a kua
tae mai ki a ia: kihai ia i aro ki te manaaki, heoi kua mamao tera i a
ia.

<span id="an_109:18">109:18</span> I kakahu ia i te kanga ki a ia, ano
ko tona kakahu: na kua tae tera ki roto ki a ia ano he wai, me he hinu
hoki ki roto ki ona wheua.

<span id="an_109:19">109:19</span> Waiho ki a ia hei kakahu hipoki mona,
hei whitiki hoki e whitikiria tonutia ai ia.

<span id="an_109:20">109:20</span> Na hei utu tena ma Ihowa ki oku
hoariri, ki te hunga hoki e korero kino nei ki toku wairua.

<span id="an_109:21">109:21</span> ¶ Kia puta tau mahi moku, e te Atua,
e te Ariki, he whakaaro ki tou ingoa: na te mea he pai tau mahi tohu,
whakaorangia ahau,

<span id="an_109:22">109:22</span> He ware hoki ahau, he rawakore, kua
mamae hoki toku ngakau i roto i ahau.

<span id="an_109:23">109:23</span> Ka riro ahau me te atarangi e
whakawairua kau ana: e peipeia ana ahau me he mawhitiwhiti.

<span id="an_109:24">109:24</span> Hurorirori kau oku turi i te
nohopuku; a e kohia ana te ngako o oku kikokiko.

<span id="an_109:25">109:25</span> Kua waiho ahau hei tawainga ma ratou:
ka kite ratou i ahau, ka ruru o ratou matenga.

<span id="an_109:26">109:26</span> Awhinatia ahau, e Ihowa, e toku Atua:
kia rite ki tou aroha tau whakaora i ahau.

<span id="an_109:27">109:27</span> Kia matau ai ratou ko tou ringa
itene: a nau tenei, e Ihowa, i mea.

<span id="an_109:28">109:28</span> Ma ratou e kanga, mau ia e manaaki:
kia whakama ratou ina whakatika; ko tau pononga ia kia hari.

<span id="an_109:29">109:29</span> Kia whakakakahuria oku hoariri ki te
whakama, a ko to ratou numinumi hei koroka hipoki mo ratou.

<span id="an_109:30">109:30</span> Ka tino whakawhetai toku mangai ki a
Ihowa, ae ra, ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a ia i waenganui o te mano.

<span id="an_109:31">109:31</span> E tu hoki ia ki te ringa matau o te
rawakore, hei whakaora i a ia i te hunga e whakahe ana i tona wairua.

<span id="an_110:1">110:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. I mea a Ihowa ki
toku Ariki: Hei toku matau koe noho ai, kia meinga ra ano e ahau ou
hoariri hei turanga waewae mou.

<span id="an_110:2">110:2</span> Ma Ihowa e tono mai te tokotoko o tou
kaha i Hiona: hei rangatira koe i waenganui i ou hoariri.

<span id="an_110:3">110:3</span> Ka kakama tou iwi ki te tapae atu i a
ratou i te ra o tou kaha: i te ataahua o nga mea tapu, no te kopu mai o
te ata, kei a koe te tomairangi o tou whanaketanga.

<span id="an_110:4">110:4</span> Kua oati a Ihowa, e kore ano tana e
puta ke; Hei tohunga koe ake ake, no te tikanga o Merekihereke.

<span id="an_110:5">110:5</span> ¶ Kei tou matau te Ariki, ka maru i a
ia nga kingi i te ra e riri ai ia.

<span id="an_110:6">110:6</span> E whakawa ia i waenganui i nga tauiwi;
e whakakiia e ia nga whenua ki te tupapaku: ka maru i a ia nga upoko i
nga whenua maha.

<span id="an_110:7">110:7</span> Ka inu wai ia i te awa i te ara: a ka
ara tona matenga.

<span id="an_111:1">111:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Ka whakapaua
toku ngakau ki te whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, i te runanga o te hunga tika,
i te whakaminenga.

<span id="an_111:2">111:2</span> He nui nga mahi a Ihowa; e whakatakina
ana e te hunga katoa e manako ana ki aua mea.

<span id="an_111:3">111:3</span> He mea honore, he mea kororia tana
mahi: tu tonu tona tika ake ake.

<span id="an_111:4">111:4</span> Kua meinga e ia kia maharatia ana mahi
whakamiharo: he atawhai a Ihowa, he aroha.

<span id="an_111:5">111:5</span> E homai ana e ia he kai ma te hunga e
wehi ana ki a ia: ka mahara tonu ia ki tana kawenata.

<span id="an_111:6">111:6</span> ¶ Kua whakakitea e ia ki tana iwi te
kaha o ana mahi, i tana hoatutanga i to nga tauiwi hei kainga tupu mo
ratou.

<span id="an_111:7">111:7</span> Ko nga mahi a ona ringa he pono, he
whakawa tika: pono tonu ana akoranga katoa,

<span id="an_111:8">111:8</span> U tonu ake ake, e mahia ana i runga i
te pono, i te tika.

<span id="an_111:9">111:9</span> I tonoa mai e ia he whakaoranga mo tana
iwi: kua kiia iho e ia tana kawenata mo ake tonu atu; he tapu tona
ingoa, e wehingia ana.

<span id="an_111:10">111:10</span> Ko te timatanga o te whakaaro nui he
wehi ki a Ihowa: he ngarahu nui to te hunga katoa nana era mahi; mau te
whakamoemiti ki a ia, ake ake.

<span id="an_112:1">112:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Ka hari te
tangata e wehi ana i a Ihowa, e aro nui ana ki ana whakahau.

<span id="an_112:2">112:2</span> Ka nui ona uri ki runga ki te whenua;
ka manaakitia te whakatupuranga o te hunga tika.

<span id="an_112:3">112:3</span> Kei tona whare te rawa, te taonga: ka
pumau tonu tona tika, ake ake.

<span id="an_112:4">112:4</span> Ka maea ake te marama i roto i te pouri
ki te hunga tika: he atawhai ia, he aroha, he tika.

<span id="an_112:5">112:5</span> He pono ka whiwhi painga te tangata he
atawhai, he ohaoha tana mahi: ka u ana kupu i te whakawakanga.

<span id="an_112:6">112:6</span> ¶ E kore hoki ia e whakangaueuetia ake
ake: ka maharatia tonutia te tangata tika ake ake.

<span id="an_112:7">112:7</span> E kore ia e mataku i te rongo kino: e u
ana tona ngakau, e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_112:8">112:8</span> Ka u tona ngakau, e kore ia e wehi, kia
kite ra ano ia i tana i hiahia ai ki ona hoariri.

<span id="an_112:9">112:9</span> Kua tuwhaina e ia, kua hoatu ki te
hunga rawakore: pumau tonu tona tika ake ake; ka ara tona haona i runga
i te kororia.

<span id="an_112:10">112:10</span> Ka kite te tangata kino, a ka pouri;
ka pakiri ona niho, memeha iho: pirau iho te hiahia o te hunga kino.

<span id="an_113:1">113:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.
Whakamoemititia, e nga pononga a Ihowa, whakamoemititia te ingoa o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_113:2">113:2</span> Kia whakapaingia te ingo o Ihowa aianei
a ake ake.

<span id="an_113:3">113:3</span> Kia whakamoemititia te ingoa o Ihowa i
te putanga mai o te ra, a tae noa ki tona torengitanga.

<span id="an_113:4">113:4</span> Kei runga rawa a Ihowa i nga iwi katoa:
kei runga ake i nga rangi tona kororia.

<span id="an_113:5">113:5</span> Ko wai te rite ana ki a Ihowa, ki to
tatou Atua, kei runga nei tona nohoanga,

<span id="an_113:6">113:6</span> E whakaiti nei i a ia ki te titiro iho
ki nga mea kei te rangi, kei te whenua?

<span id="an_113:7">113:7</span> E whakaara ake ana ia i te iti i roto i
te puehu, e whakateitei ake ana i te rawakore i roto i te puranga paru;

<span id="an_113:8">113:8</span> Kia whakanohoia ai e ia ki roto ki nga
rangatira, ki nga rangatira o tana iwi.

<span id="an_113:9">113:9</span> Nana hoki te pakoko i whai whare ai,
hei whaereere e koa ana ki ana tamariki. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_114:1">114:1</span> ¶ I te putanga mai o Iharaira i Ihipa,
o te whare o Hakopa i te iwi reo ke,

<span id="an_114:2">114:2</span> Ko Hura tona wahi tapu, ko Iharaira
tona rangatiratanga.

<span id="an_114:3">114:3</span> I kite te moana, a whati ana: i
whakahokia ki muri a Horano.

<span id="an_114:4">114:4</span> Pekepeke ana nga maunga ano he hipi
toa, nga pukepuke ano he reme.

<span id="an_114:5">114:5</span> I ahatia koe, e te moana, i whati ai
koe e Horano, i whakahokia ai koe ki muri?

<span id="an_114:6">114:6</span> E nga maunga, i pekepeke ai koutou ano
he hipi toa; e nga pukepuke, ano he reme?

<span id="an_114:7">114:7</span> E wiri, e te whenua, i te aroaro o te
Ariki; i te aroaro o te Atua o Hakopa;

<span id="an_114:8">114:8</span> I meinga ai te toka hei hopua wai; te
kiripaka hei puna wai.

<span id="an_115:1">115:1</span> ¶ Aua ki a matou, e Ihowa, aua ki a
matou, engari me hoatu te kororia ki tou ingoa: whakaaroa tou aroha, tou
pono.

<span id="an_115:2">115:2</span> Kia mea koia nga tauiwi: Kei hea ianei
to ratou Atua?

<span id="an_115:3">115:3</span> Kei te rangi ia to matou Atua; kua
meatia e ia nga mea katoa i pai ai ia.

<span id="an_115:4">115:4</span> He hiriwa a ratou whakapakoko, he
koura, he mahi na te ringa tangata.

<span id="an_115:5">115:5</span> He mangai o ratou, a kahore e korero:
he kanohi o ratou, a kahore e kite:

<span id="an_115:6">115:6</span> He taringa o ratou, a kahore e rongo:
he ihu o ratou, a kahore e hongi:

<span id="an_115:7">115:7</span> He ringa o ratou, a kahore e whawha: he
waewae o ratou, a kahore e haere: kahore hoki o ratou korokoro e korero.

<span id="an_115:8">115:8</span> Ka rite ki a ratou o ratou kaihanga; ae
ra, te hunga katoa ano e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ratou.

<span id="an_115:9">115:9</span> ¶ E Iharaira, whakawhirinaki ki a
Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu rakau.

<span id="an_115:10">115:10</span> E te whare o Arona, whakawhirinaki ki
a Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu rakau.

<span id="an_115:11">115:11</span> E te hunga e wehi ana i a Ihowa,
whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa: ko ia to ratou awhina, to ratou whakangungu
rakau.

<span id="an_115:12">115:12</span> Kua mahara a Ihowa ki a tatou, mana
tatou e manaaki: mana e manaaki te whare o Iharaira, mana e manaaki te
whare o Arona.

<span id="an_115:13">115:13</span> Ka manaakitia e ia te hunga e wehi
ana ki a Ihowa, te iti, te rahi.

<span id="an_115:14">115:14</span> Ka tapiritia ano e Ihowa ki a koutou,
ki a koutou tahi ko a koutou tamariki.

<span id="an_115:15">115:15</span> He manaakitanga koutou na Ihowa, na
te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua.

<span id="an_115:16">115:16</span> Ko nga rangi, he rangi no Ihowa; ko
te whenua ia, he mea homai nana ki nga tama a te tangata.

<span id="an_115:17">115:17</span> E kore nga tupapaku e whakamoemiti ki
a Ihowa: me te hunga katoa ano e heke ana ki te wahangutanga.

<span id="an_115:18">115:18</span> Ko matou ia ka whakapai ki a Ihowa
aianei a ake ake. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_116:1">116:1</span> ¶ E aroha ana ahau ki a Ihowa: mona i
whakarongo ki toku reo, ki aku inoi.

<span id="an_116:2">116:2</span> I tahuri mai tona taringa ki ahau: mo
reira ka karanga ahau ki a ia i ahau e ora ana.

<span id="an_116:3">116:3</span> I karapotia ahau e nga whakawiringa a
te mate: mau pu ahau i nga mamae o te reinga, i kite ahau i te pawera, i
te pouri.

<span id="an_116:4">116:4</span> Na ko taku karangatanga ki te ingoa o
Ihowa; Tena ra, e Ihowa, whakaorangia toku wairua.

<span id="an_116:5">116:5</span> He atawhai a Ihowa, he tika: ae, he
aroha to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_116:6">116:6</span> E tiakina ana e Ihowa te hunga kuware:
i whakaititia ahau, a nana ahau i whakaora.

<span id="an_116:7">116:7</span> E hoki, e toku wairua, ki tou
okiokinga; kua atawhaitia hoki koe e Ihowa.

<span id="an_116:8">116:8</span> Nau hoki toku wairua i whakaora kei
mate, oku kanohi kei whai roimata, oku waewae kei paheke.

<span id="an_116:9">116:9</span> Tera ahau e haereere i te aroaro o
Ihowa i te whenua o te ora.

<span id="an_116:10">116:10</span> ¶ I whakapono ahau, koia ahau i
korero ai: he nui toku whakawhiunga.

<span id="an_116:11">116:11</span> I mea ahau i toku ohoreretanga, He
teka kau nga tangata katoa.

<span id="an_116:12">116:12</span> He aha taku e whakahoki ai ki a Ihowa
mo ana atawhainga katoa i ahau?

<span id="an_116:13">116:13</span> Ka mau ahau ki te kapu o te
whakaoranga, ka karanga ki te ingoa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_116:14">116:14</span> Ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi
ki a Ihowa i te aroaro o tana iwi katoa.

<span id="an_116:15">116:15</span> He mea utu nui ki ta Ihowa titiro te
matenga o tana hunga tapu.

<span id="an_116:16">116:16</span> E Ihowa, he pono ko ahau tau pononga;
ko ahau tau pononga, ko te tama a tau pononga wahine; nau i wewete oku
here.

<span id="an_116:17">116:17</span> Ka tukua e ahau te patunga tapu, ara
te whakawhetai: ka karanga ki te ingoa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_116:18">116:18</span> Ka whakamana e ahau aku kupu taurangi
ki a Ihowa, ae, ki te aroaro o tana iwi katoa.

<span id="an_116:19">116:19</span> Ki nga marae o te whare o Ihowa, ki
waenganui ou, e Hiruharama. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_117:1">117:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, e nga tauiwi
katoa: whakamoemititia ia, e nga iwi katoa.

<span id="an_117:2">117:2</span> He nui hoki tana mahi tohu ki a tatou:
e mau ana hoki te pono o Ihowa ake ake. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:1">118:1</span> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki
ia, he pumau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_118:2">118:2</span> Kia mea a Iharaira, He pumau tonu tana
mahi tohu.

<span id="an_118:3">118:3</span> Kia mea te whare o Arona, He pumau tonu
tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_118:4">118:4</span> Kia mea te hunga e wehi ana i a Ihowa,
He pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_118:5">118:5</span> I karanga ahau ki a Ihowa i roto i te
pouri: i whakahoki kupu mai a Ihowa ki ahau, i whakatu hoki i ahau ki te
wahi whanui.

<span id="an_118:6">118:6</span> Kei ahau a Ihowa; e kore ahau e wehi:
he aha ta te tangata e mea ai ki ahau?

<span id="an_118:7">118:7</span> Kei ahau a Ihowa kei roto i oku
kaiawhina: no reira tera ahau e kite i taku i hiahia ai ki te hunga e
kino ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_118:8">118:8</span> Ko te whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, pai
atu i te whakaaro ki te tangata.

<span id="an_118:9">118:9</span> Ko te whakawhirinaki ki a Ihowa, pai
atu i te okioki ki nga rangatira.

<span id="an_118:10">118:10</span> I karapotia ahau e nga iwi katoa: ka
ngaro ratou i ahau i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:11">118:11</span> I karapotia ahau e ratou: ae, i
karapotia ahau e ratou: ka ngaro ratou i ahau i runga i te ingoa o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:12">118:12</span> Me te mea he pi ratou e mui ana ki
ahau; kua pirau ratou ano he ahi tataramoa: i ngaro hoki ratou i ahau i
runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:13">118:13</span> Kaha pu tau turaki i ahau, kia hinga
ai ahau: na Ihowa ia ahau i awhina mai.

<span id="an_118:14">118:14</span> Ko Ihowa toku kaha, taku himene, ko
ia ano toku whakaoranga.

<span id="an_118:15">118:15</span> He reo hari, he reo whakaoranga, kei
nga tapenakara o te hunga tika: he maia nga mahi a te ringa matau o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:16">118:16</span> Kua whakanuia te matau o Ihowa: he
maia nga mahi a te ringa matau o Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:17">118:17</span> E kore ahau e mate, engari tera ahau
e ora, hei whakapuaki i nga mahi a Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:18">118:18</span> I pakia rawatia ahau e Ihowa: otiia
kihai ahau i tukua e ia kia mate.

<span id="an_118:19">118:19</span> ¶ Whakatuwheratia ki ahau nga kuwaha
o te tika: ka tomo ahau ki roto, ka whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:20">118:20</span> Ko te kuwaha tenei o Ihowa: ka tomo
te hunga tika ki reira.

<span id="an_118:21">118:21</span> Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe, mou i
whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau, kua meinga hoki ko koe hei whakaora moku.

<span id="an_118:22">118:22</span> Ko te kohatu i kapea e nga kaihanga,
kua meinga hei upoko mo te kokonga.

<span id="an_118:23">118:23</span> Na Ihowa tenei: he mea miharo ki o
tatou kanohi.

<span id="an_118:24">118:24</span> Ko te ra tenei i hanga e Ihowa kia
whakamanamana, kia koa tatou i reira.

<span id="an_118:25">118:25</span> Whakaorangia ra aianei, e Ihowa: tena
ra, e Ihowa, homai he ngahuru ki a matou.

<span id="an_118:26">118:26</span> Kia whakapaingia te tangata e haere
mai ana i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa: kua whakapaingia koutou e matou i
roto i te whare o Ihowa.

<span id="an_118:27">118:27</span> Ko Ihowa te Atua, a nana i homai te
marama ki a tatou: herea te patunga tapu ki nga aho, ki nga haona ra ano
o te aata.

<span id="an_118:28">118:28</span> Ko koe toku Atua, maku koe e
whakamoemiti: toku Atua, maku koe e whakanui.

<span id="an_118:29">118:29</span> Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa; he pai hoki
ia: he pumau tonu tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_119:1">119:1</span> ¶ AREPE Ka hari te hunga he tapatahi
nei i te ara, e haere nei i te ture a Ihowa.

<span id="an_119:2">119:2</span> Ka hari te hunga e mau ana ki ana
whakaaturanga; e whakapaua ana o ratou ngakau ki te rapu i a ia.

<span id="an_119:3">119:3</span> Ae, e kore ratou e mahi i te kino; e
haere ana ratou i ana ara.

<span id="an_119:4">119:4</span> ¶ Kua oti matou te whakahau ki au
akoranga, kia ata puritia e matou.

<span id="an_119:5">119:5</span> Aue, me i whakatikaia toku ara ki te
pupuri i au akoranga!

<span id="an_119:6">119:6</span> Ko reira ahau ka kore ai e whakama: i
ahau ka whai whakaaro nei ki au whakahau katoa.

<span id="an_119:7">119:7</span> ¶ Ka whakamoemiti ahau ki a koe i runga
i te ngakau tika, ina ako ahau i au whakaritenga tika.

<span id="an_119:8">119:8</span> Ka puritia e ahau au tikanga: kaua ahau
e whakarerea rawatia. PETA

<span id="an_119:9">119:9</span> ¶ He aha te mea e ma ai i te
taitamariki tona ara? kia rite ki tau kupu tana whakamaharatanga iho.

<span id="an_119:10">119:10</span> ¶ Kua whakapaua e ahau toku ngakau ki
te rapu i a koe: kaua ahau e tukua kia kotiti ke i au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:11">119:11</span> ¶ Kua whakatakotoria e ahau tau kupu
ki roto ki toku ngakau, kei hara ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_119:12">119:12</span> ¶ E Ihowa, ka whakapaingia koe:
whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:13">119:13</span> ¶ Kua whakapuakina e oku ngutu nga
whakaritenga katoa a tou mangai.

<span id="an_119:14">119:14</span> Ko toku koa i te ara o au
whakaaturanga, me te mea mo nga taonga katoa.

<span id="an_119:15">119:15</span> Ka whakaaroaro ahau ki au ako, a ka
whai mahara ki au huarahi.

<span id="an_119:16">119:16</span> He oranga ngakau ki ahau au tikanga:
e kore ahau e wareware ki tau kupu. KIMERE

<span id="an_119:17">119:17</span> ¶ Kia atawhai ki tau pononga, kia ora
ai ahau; kia puritia ai hoki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:18">119:18</span> ¶ Whakatirohia oku kanohi kia kite ai
ahau i nga mea whakamiharo i roto i tau ture.

<span id="an_119:19">119:19</span> ¶ He manene ahau i runga i te whenua:
kaua au whakahau e huna ki ahau.

<span id="an_119:20">119:20</span> ¶ Ka ngawha toku wairua i te matenui
atu ki au whakaritenga i nga wa katoa.

<span id="an_119:21">119:21</span> ¶ Kua riria e koe te hunga whakakake
kua oti nei te kanga, e kotiti ke nei i au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:22">119:22</span> ¶ Parea atu i ahau te tawai me te
whakahawea: kua mau hoki ahau ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:23">119:23</span> ¶ I noho ano hoki nga rangatira ki te
korero kino moku: otira e whakaaro ana tau pononga ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:24">119:24</span> ¶ Ko au whakaaturanga ano toku oranga
ngakau, oku hoa whakatakoto whakaaro. TARETE

<span id="an_119:25">119:25</span> ¶ Piri tonu toku wairua ki te puehu;
whakahauoratia ahau kia rite ki atu kupu.

<span id="an_119:26">119:26</span> ¶ I whakaaturia e ahau oku ara, a
whakahoki kupu ana koe ki ahau: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:27">119:27</span> Meinga ahau kia matau ki te ara o au
ako: kia whakaaroaro ai ahau ki au mahi whakamiharo.

<span id="an_119:28">119:28</span> ¶ E maturuturu iho ana toku wairua i
te pouri: kia rite ki tau kapu tau whakau ake i ahau.

<span id="an_119:29">119:29</span> Whakamataratia atu i ahau te ara o te
teka: kia atawhai mai hoki, a homai tau ture.

<span id="an_119:30">119:30</span> ¶ Kua whiriwhiria e ahau te ara o te
pono: ka waiho e ahau au whakaritenga ki toku aroaro.

<span id="an_119:31">119:31</span> Piri tonu ahau ki au whakaaturanga: e
Ihowa, kei whakama ahau.

<span id="an_119:32">119:32</span> Ka oma ahau i te ara o au whakahau,
ina whakanuia e koe toku ngakau. HE

<span id="an_119:33">119:33</span> ¶ E Ihowa, whakaakona ahau ki te ara
o au tikanga: a ka mau i ahau taea noatia te mutunga.

<span id="an_119:34">119:34</span> Homai he matauranga ki ahau, a ka mau
i ahau tau ture; ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te pupuri.

<span id="an_119:35">119:35</span> ¶ Meinga ahau kia haere i te ara o au
whakahau; ko taku hoki tena e whakaahuareka nei.

<span id="an_119:36">119:36</span> Whakaangahia toku ngakau ki au
whakaaturanga; kaua hoki ki te apo.

<span id="an_119:37">119:37</span> ¶ Whakatahuritia ketia oku kanohi kei
kite i te horihori: whakahauorangia ahau i tau ara.

<span id="an_119:38">119:38</span> ¶ Whakapumautia tau kupu ki tau
pononga, e wehi nei ki a koe.

<span id="an_119:39">119:39</span> ¶ Parea atu toku tawainga, e wehi nei
ahau: he pai hoki au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_119:40">119:40</span> ¶ Nana, kua matenui ahau ki au ako:
whakahauorangia ahau i runga i tou tika. WHAU

<span id="an_119:41">119:41</span> ¶ Kia puta ano au mahi tohu ki ahau,
e Ihowa: ara tau whakaoranga, kia rite ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:42">119:42</span> Penei ka whai kupu maku ki toku
kaitawai; noku ka whakawhirinaki ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:43">119:43</span> ¶ Kaua e tangohia rawatia i toku
mangai te kupu o te pono: e tumanako nei hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_119:44">119:44</span> Penei ka puritia e ahau tau ture ake
ake.

<span id="an_119:45">119:45</span> ¶ A ka haereere noa ahau; kua rapua
hoki e ahau au akoranga.

<span id="an_119:46">119:46</span> Ka korerotia ano e ahau au
whakaaturanga ki te aroaro o nga kingi, e kore ano e whakama.

<span id="an_119:47">119:47</span> A ka waiho e ahau hei oranga ngakau
moku au whakahau e aroha nei ahau.

<span id="an_119:48">119:48</span> Ka toro atu hoki oku ringa ki au
whakahau e aroha nei ahau, ka whakaaroaro ano ki au tikanga. TAINE

<span id="an_119:49">119:49</span> ¶ Maharatia te kupu ki tau pononga,
no te mea kua meinga ahau e koe kia tumanako atu.

<span id="an_119:50">119:50</span> ¶ Ko toku oranga ngakau tenei i ahau
e tangi nei: na tau kupu nei hoki ahau i whakahauora.

<span id="an_119:51">119:51</span> ¶ Nui rawa te whakahi ki ahau o te
hunga whakakake: heoi kihai ahau i peka ke i tau ture.

<span id="an_119:52">119:52</span> ¶ I mahara ahau ki au whakaritenga, e
Ihowa, o tua iho; a marie ana toku ngakau.

<span id="an_119:53">119:53</span> ¶ Mau pu ahau i te pawera, mo te
hunga kino kua whakarere nei i tau ture.

<span id="an_119:54">119:54</span> ¶ Ko au tikanga aku e himene ai i te
whare i noho manene ai ahau.

<span id="an_119:55">119:55</span> ¶ I mahara ahau ki tou ingoa i te po,
e Ihowa: a puritia ana e ahau tau ture.

<span id="an_119:56">119:56</span> I ahau tenei, he mau noku ki au ako.
KETE

<span id="an_119:57">119:57</span> ¶ Ko Ihowa toku wahi: kua mea nei
ahau, ka pupuri ahau i au kupu.

<span id="an_119:58">119:58</span> ¶ I whakapaua toku ngakau ki te inoi
ki a koe kia pai mai: kia rite ki tau kupu tau mahi tohu ki ahau.

<span id="an_119:59">119:59</span> ¶ I whakaaro ahau ki oku ara: a anga
ana oku waewae ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:60">119:60</span> I hohoro ahau, a kihai i whakaroa ki
te pupuri i au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:61">119:61</span> ¶ Karapotia putia ana ahau e nga here
a te hunga kino: kihai ia ahau i wareware ki tau ture.

<span id="an_119:62">119:62</span> ¶ I waenganui po ka ara ahau ki te
whakawhetai ki a koe mo au whakaritenga tika.

<span id="an_119:63">119:63</span> ¶ He hoa ahau no te hunga katoa e
wehi ana i a koe; no te hunga ano e pupuri ana i au ako.

<span id="an_119:64">119:64</span> ¶ Ki tonu, e Ihowa, te whenua i tau
mahi tohu: whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga. TETE

<span id="an_119:65">119:65</span> ¶ Pai rawa tau hanga ki tau pononga,
e Ihowa; rite tonu ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:66">119:66</span> Whakaakona ahau ki te ngarahu pai, ki
te matauranga: kua whakapono hoki ahau ki au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:67">119:67</span> ¶ I ahau kiano i whakawhiua, i he
ahau: tena ko tenei ka puritia e ahau tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:68">119:68</span> ¶ He pai koe, he pai hoki au mahi:
whakaakona ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:69">119:69</span> ¶ Kua titoa e te hunga whakakake he
teka moku: ka whakapaua toku ngakau ki te pupuri i au ako.

<span id="an_119:70">119:70</span> He ngako rawa to ratou ngakau, koia
ano kei te taupa: ko ahau ia, he oranga ngakau ki ahau tau ture.

<span id="an_119:71">119:71</span> ¶ Marie ano ahau kia pehia e te
pouri; i ako ai ahau i au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:72">119:72</span> ¶ Ko te ture a tou mangai pai ke atu
ki ahau i nga mano o te koura, o te hiriwa. IOTA

<span id="an_119:73">119:73</span> ¶ Na ou ringa ahau i hanga, i
whakawhaiahua: homai he matauranga ki ahau, kia ako ai ahau ki au
whakahau.

<span id="an_119:74">119:74</span> ¶ Ka hari te hunga e wehi ana i a koe
ina kite i ahau: noku i tumanako ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:75">119:75</span> ¶ E matau ana ahau, e Ihowa, he tika
au whakaritenga; a he pono nou i pehia ai toku ngakau e koe.

<span id="an_119:76">119:76</span> ¶ Tena ra, waiho tau mahi tohu hei
whakamarie moku; kia rite ki tau kupu ki tau pononga.

<span id="an_119:77">119:77</span> Kia puta ki ahau au mahi aroha, kia
ora ai ahau; ko tau ture hoki toku oranga ngakau.

<span id="an_119:78">119:78</span> ¶ Kia whakama te hunga whakakake; no
te mea kahore he take i he ai ta ratou hanga ki ahau; ko ahau ia ka
whakaaroaro ki au akoranga.

<span id="an_119:79">119:79</span> Ko te hunga e wehi ana ki a koe me
anga ki ahau, a ka mohio ratou ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:80">119:80</span> ¶ Kia tapatahi toku ngakau ki au
tikanga; kei whakama ahau. KAPA

<span id="an_119:81">119:81</span> ¶ E matenui ana toku wairua ki tau
whakaoranga: otiia ka tumanako ahau ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:82">119:82</span> Matawaia ana oku kanohi, he meatanga
ki tau kupu, i ahau e mea ana, Ahea koe whakamarie ai i ahau?

<span id="an_119:83">119:83</span> ¶ Kua rite nei hoki ahau ki te koki i
roto i te paoa: he ahakoa e kore ahau e wareware ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:84">119:84</span> ¶ E hia nga ra o tau pononga? a hea
koe whakarite whakawa ai mo te hunga e tukino nei i ahau?

<span id="an_119:85">119:85</span> ¶ Kua keri poka te hunga whakakake
moku; he mea kahore e rite ki tau ture.

<span id="an_119:86">119:86</span> Pono tonu au whakahau katoa: e tukino
takekore ana ratou i ahau; awhinatia mai ahau.

<span id="an_119:87">119:87</span> Wahi iti kua moti ahau i a ratou i
runga i te whenua: otira kihai i mahue i ahau au akoranga.

<span id="an_119:88">119:88</span> ¶ Kia rite ki tou aroha tau
whakahauora i ahau: a ka puritia e ahau nga whakaaturanga a tou mangai.
RAMERE

<span id="an_119:89">119:89</span> ¶ Pumau tonu tau kupu, e Ihowa, ake
ake i runga i te rangi.

<span id="an_119:90">119:90</span> Kei nga whakatupuranga katoa tou
pono: whakaungia ana e koe te whenua, a e tu nei ano.

<span id="an_119:91">119:91</span> E tu nei ano inaianei, pera tonu me
tau i whakarite ai, he pononga hoki nga mea katoa nau.

<span id="an_119:92">119:92</span> ¶ Me kaua tau ture hei oranga mo toku
ngakau, kua ngaro ahau i reira i toku auetanga.

<span id="an_119:93">119:93</span> ¶ E kore rawa ahau e wareware ki au
ako, he mea whakahauora hoki nau ena i ahau.

<span id="an_119:94">119:94</span> ¶ Nau ahau, mau ahau e whakaora: kua
rapua hoki e ahau au ako.

<span id="an_119:95">119:95</span> ¶ Kua tatari te hunga kino ki ahau
kia whakamatea: ka whakaaro ia ahau ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:96">119:96</span> ¶ Kua kitea e ahau te mutunga o nga
mea tino tika katoa: he whanui rawa ia tau whakahau. MEME

<span id="an_119:97">119:97</span> ¶ Ano toku aroha ki tau ture! Ko taku
tena e whakaaroaro ai i te roa o te ra.

<span id="an_119:98">119:98</span> ¶ Nau i hira ake ai oku whakaaro i o
oku hoariri, na au whakahau, e piri tonu nei ki ahau.

<span id="an_119:99">119:99</span> Nui atu oku mahara i o oku
kaiwhakaako katoa: noku i whakaaroaro tonu ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:100">119:100</span> Tera atu toku mohio i to nga
kaumatua, no te mea i pupuri ahau i au ako.

<span id="an_119:101">119:101</span> ¶ Kua kaiponuhia mai e ahau oku
waewae i nga ara kino katoa, kia pupuri ai ahau i tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:102">119:102</span> ¶ Kihai ahau i titaha i au
whakaritenga; nau hoki ahau i ako.

<span id="an_119:103">119:103</span> ¶ Ano te reka o au kupu ki toku
ngao; ae ra, reka atu i te honi ki toku mangai.

<span id="an_119:104">119:104</span> Na au ako ahau i whai mohio ai: na
reira ahau i kino ai ki nga ara teka katoa. NUNU

<span id="an_119:105">119:105</span> ¶ He rama tau kupu ki oku waewae,
he marama ki toku ara.

<span id="an_119:106">119:106</span> ¶ Kua oati ahau, a ka whakamana ano
e ahau: kia puritia e ahau au whakaritenga tika.

<span id="an_119:107">119:107</span> ¶ He nui te mamae o toku ngakau:
whakahauorangia ahau, e Ihowa, kia rite ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:108">119:108</span> ¶ Manakohia, e Ihowa, nga
ohaohatanga a toku mangai, whakaakona hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_119:109">119:109</span> ¶ Kei toku ringa tonu toku wairua,
heoi kahore ahau e wareware ki tau ture.

<span id="an_119:110">119:110</span> Kua whakatakotoria e te hunga kino
he mahanga moku: heoi kahore ahau i peka ke i au ako.

<span id="an_119:111">119:111</span> ¶ Ka waiho e ahau au whakaaturanga
hei kainga tupu moku ake ake: ko toku koanga ngakau hoki ena.

<span id="an_119:112">119:112</span> Kua whakaanga e ahau toku ngakau ki
te mahi tonu i au tikanga: a te mutunga ra ano. HAMEKE

<span id="an_119:113">119:113</span> ¶ E kino ana ahau ki te hunga
whakaaro ruarua; ko tau ture ia taku e aroha ai.

<span id="an_119:114">119:114</span> ¶ Ko toku piringa koe, ko toku
whakangungu rakau: e tumanako ana ahau ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:115">119:115</span> ¶ Mawehe atu i ahau, e te hunga
kino; ka whakaritea hoki e ahau nga whakahau a toku Atua.

<span id="an_119:116">119:116</span> ¶ Kia rite ki tau kupu tau tautoko
ake i ahau, kia ora ai ahau: kaua hoki ahau e tukua kia whakama ki taku
e tumanako atu nei.

<span id="an_119:117">119:117</span> Tautokona ake ahau, kia ora ai
ahau, a ka whai whakaaro tonu ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:118">119:118</span> ¶ Kua whakahaweatia e koe te hunga
katoa e kotiti ke ana i au tikanga; he horihori hoki to ratou tinihanga.

<span id="an_119:119">119:119</span> Ka whakakahoretia e koe te hunga
kino katoa o te whenua, ano he para mata: koia ahau i aroha ai ki au
whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:120">119:120</span> Wiri ana oku kikokiko i te wehi ki
a koe; e mataku ana hoki ahau ki au whakaritenga. AINE

<span id="an_119:121">119:121</span> ¶ He whakawa tika, he tika taku
mahi: kaua ahau e tukua ki oku kaitukino.

<span id="an_119:122">119:122</span> Ko koe hei tuara mo tau pononga mo
te pai: kei tukinotia ahau e te hunga whakakake.

<span id="an_119:123">119:123</span> ¶ Matawaia ana oku kanohi i te
meatanga ki tau whakaora, ki te kupu hoki o tau tika.

<span id="an_119:124">119:124</span> ¶ Kia rite ki tou aroha tau mahi ki
tau pononga: whakaakona hoki ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:125">119:125</span> He pononga ahau nau; homai he
mahara ki ahau, kia matau ai ki au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:126">119:126</span> ¶ Kua rite te wa hei mahinga ma
Ihowa; kua whakakahoretia hoki e ratou tau ture.

<span id="an_119:127">119:127</span> ¶ Na reira i arohaina rawatia ai e
ahau au whakahau i te koura, ae, i te tino koura.

<span id="an_119:128">119:128</span> Na reira tika tonu ki ahau au ako
katoa mo nga mea katoa: kino iho ano ahau ki nga ara teka katoa. PE

<span id="an_119:129">119:129</span> ¶ He mea whakamiharo au
whakaaturanga: i mau ai toku wairua ki reira.

<span id="an_119:130">119:130</span> ¶ Ko te whakapuakanga o au kupu he
homai marama; na reira i homai he mahara ki nga kuware.

<span id="an_119:131">119:131</span> ¶ I hamama toku mangai, i kihakiha:
he matenui noku ki au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:132">119:132</span> ¶ Tahuri mai ki ahau, tohungia hoki
ahau: kia rite ki tau hanga ki te hunga e aroha ana ki tou ingoa.

<span id="an_119:133">119:133</span> ¶ Whakatikaia oku hikoinga ki runga
i tau kupu: kaua hoki tetahi he e tukua hei rangatira moku.

<span id="an_119:134">119:134</span> ¶ Whakaorangia ahau i te tukino a
te tangata: a ka puritia e ahau au ako.

<span id="an_119:135">119:135</span> ¶ Kia marama mai tou mata ki tau
pononga: whakaakona hoki ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:136">119:136</span> ¶ Heke noa nga awa wai o oku
kanohi; mo ratou kahore i pupuri i tau ture. TARI

<span id="an_119:137">119:137</span> ¶ He tika koe, e Ihowa, he tika ano
au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_119:138">119:138</span> He tika, he pono rawa au
whakaaturanga i whakahaua mai e koe.

<span id="an_119:139">119:139</span> ¶ Ka ngaro ahau i toku ngakau
whakapuke, mo au kupu ka wareware nei i oku hoariri.

<span id="an_119:140">119:140</span> ¶ Hore rawa he para o tau kupu:
koia i arohaina ai e tau pononga.

<span id="an_119:141">119:141</span> ¶ He iti ahau, e whakahaweatia ana:
heoi kahore ahau e wareware ki au ako.

<span id="an_119:142">119:142</span> ¶ He tika pumau tonu tou tika; he
pono hoki tau ture.

<span id="an_119:143">119:143</span> ¶ Kua pa mai ki ahau te pouri me te
mamae: ko au whakahau ia toku oranga ngakau.

<span id="an_119:144">119:144</span> Pumau tonu te tika o au
whakaaturanga: homai he mahara ki ahau, a ka ora ahau. KOPO

<span id="an_119:145">119:145</span> ¶ I whakapaua toku ngakau ki te
karanga; whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau, e Ihowa; ka mau i ahau au
tikanga.

<span id="an_119:146">119:146</span> I karanga ahau ki a koe:
whakaorangia ahau, a ka puritia e ahau au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:147">119:147</span> ¶ Kiano te ata i puao noa, kua
karanga ahau: i tumanako ahau ki au kupu.

<span id="an_119:148">119:148</span> I hohoro oku kanohi i nga
mataaratanga ki te whakaaroaro ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:149">119:149</span> ¶ Whakarongo ki toku reo, kia rite
ki tou aroha: kia rite, e Ihowa, ki tau i whakarite ai tau whakahauora i
ahau.

<span id="an_119:150">119:150</span> ¶ E whakatata mai ana te hunga e
whai ana i te whanoke: kei tawhiti atu ratou i tau ture.

<span id="an_119:151">119:151</span> E tata ana mai koe, e Ihowa: he
pono katoa au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:152">119:152</span> ¶ Nonamata ahau i matau ai ki au
whakaaturanga, he mea whakapumau nau no tua whakarere. REHE

<span id="an_119:153">119:153</span> ¶ Whakaaro mai ki toku mate, a
whakaorangia ahau: kahore hoki ahau e wareware ki tau ture.

<span id="an_119:154">119:154</span> Tohea taku tohe, whakaorangia hoki
ahau: kia rite ki tau kupu tau whakahauoranga i ahau.

<span id="an_119:155">119:155</span> ¶ Kei tawhiti atu i te hunga kino
te whakaoranga: kahore hoki ratou e rapu ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:156">119:156</span> ¶ E Ihowa, he nui au mahi tohu: kia
rite ki au whakaritenga tau whakahauora i ahau.

<span id="an_119:157">119:157</span> ¶ He tokomaha oku kaitukino, oku
hoariri: heoi kahore ahau i peka ke i au whakaaturanga.

<span id="an_119:158">119:158</span> ¶ I kite ahau i nga kaimahi i te
kino, a pouri iho: no ratou kahore e pupuri i tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:159">119:159</span> ¶ Tirohia mai toku aroha ki au ako:
kia rite ki tou aroha, e Ihowa, tau whakahauora i ahau.

<span id="an_119:160">119:160</span> ¶ Ko te huinga katoatanga o tau
kupu he pono; pumau katoa anao au whakaritenga tika ake ake. HINE

<span id="an_119:161">119:161</span> ¶ Hore he rawa i tukinotia ai ahau
e nga rangatira: otiia e wehi ana toku ngakau i tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:162">119:162</span> ¶ E hari ana ahau ki tau kupu: ano
he tangata kua whiwhi ki te taonga nui.

<span id="an_119:163">119:163</span> ¶ E kino ana ahau, e whakarihariha
ana ki te korero teka: ko tau ture ia taku i aroha ai.

<span id="an_119:164">119:164</span> ¶ Takiwhitu aku whakamoemiti ki a
koe i te ra tahi mo au whakaritenga tika.

<span id="an_119:165">119:165</span> ¶ He rangimarie nui to te hunga e
aroha ana ki tau ture: e kore hoki o ratou waewae e tutuki.

<span id="an_119:166">119:166</span> ¶ A kua tumanako ahau ki tau
whakaora, e Ihowa, kua mahi ahau i au whakahau.

<span id="an_119:167">119:167</span> ¶ Kua puritia e toku wairua au
whakaaturanga, ae, e arohaina nuitia ana e ahau.

<span id="an_119:168">119:168</span> Kua puritia e ahau au ako me au
whakaaturanga: kei tou aroaro hoki oku ara katoa. TAU

<span id="an_119:169">119:169</span> ¶ Tukua atu taku tangi kia tata atu
ki tou aroaro, e Ihowa: homai he mahara ki ahau, kia rite ki tau kupu.

<span id="an_119:170">119:170</span> Kia tae atu taku inoi ki tou
aroaro: kia rite ki tau kupu whakaora i ahau.

<span id="an_119:171">119:171</span> ¶ Kia whakapuaki oku ngutu i te
whakamoemiti: e whakaako ana hoki koe i ahau ki au tikanga.

<span id="an_119:172">119:172</span> ¶ Ma toku arero e korero tau kupu:
he tika hoki au whakahau katoa.

<span id="an_119:173">119:173</span> ¶ Kia rite tou ringa ki te awhina i
ahau; kua whiriwhiria hoki e ahau ko au ako.

<span id="an_119:174">119:174</span> Kua matenui ahau ki tau whakaora, e
Ihowa: ko tau ture hoki toku oranga ngakau.

<span id="an_119:175">119:175</span> ¶ Kia ora toku wairua, a ka
whakamoemiti ia ki a koe: kia awhinatia hoki ahau e au whakaritenga.

<span id="an_119:176">119:176</span> ¶ Kua kotiti ke ahau me he hipi
ngaro: rapua tau pononga, kahore hoki ahau e wareware ki au whakahau.

<span id="an_120:1">120:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I tangi,
ahau ki a Ihowa i toku matenga; a i whakahoki kupu mai ia ki ahau.

<span id="an_120:2">120:2</span> E Ihowa, whakaorangia toku wairua i te
ngutu teka, i te arero hianga.

<span id="an_120:3">120:3</span> Ko te aha e hoatu ki a koe? ko te aha
hoki e tapiritia atu mau, e te arero hianga?

<span id="an_120:4">120:4</span> Ko nga pere koi a te hunga nunui, me
nga waro hunipa.

<span id="an_120:5">120:5</span> ¶ Aue, toku mate, to te manene i
Meheke, toku hoki e noho nei i nga teneti o Kerara!

<span id="an_120:6">120:6</span> Kua roa te nohoanga tahitanga o toku
wairua ki te tangata e kino ana ki te ata noho.

<span id="an_120:7">120:7</span> Mo te ata noho ahau, engari ka korero
ahau, ka anga ratou ka whawhai.

<span id="an_121:1">121:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka anga atu
oku kanohi ki nga maunga; no reira nei te awhina moku.

<span id="an_121:2">121:2</span> No Ihowa te awhina moku, no te kaihanga
o te rangi, o te whenua.

<span id="an_121:3">121:3</span> E kore ia e tuku i tou waewae kia
nekehia; e kore tou kaitiaki e moe.

<span id="an_121:4">121:4</span> Ina, e kore te kaitiaki o Iharaira e
parangia, e moe.

<span id="an_121:5">121:5</span> Ko Ihowa tou kaitiaki, ko Ihowa tou
whakamarumaru i tou matau.

<span id="an_121:6">121:6</span> E kore koe e pakia e te ra i te awatea,
e te marama ranei i te po.

<span id="an_121:7">121:7</span> Ma Ihowa koe e tiaki i roto i nga kino
katoa; mana e tiaki tou wairua.

<span id="an_121:8">121:8</span> Ma Ihowa e tiaki tou haerenga atu, me
tou haerenga mai aianei a ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_122:1">122:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. I
koa ahau i ta ratou meatanga mai ki ahau; Tatou ka haere ki te whare o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_122:2">122:2</span> E tu ana o matou waewae ki ou tatau, e
Hiruharama:

<span id="an_122:3">122:3</span> Ko te hanganga o Hiruharama, rite tonu
ki to te pa kua tuhonohonoa ki a ia ano..

<span id="an_122:4">122:4</span> Haereere ana ki reira nga iwi, nga iwi
o Ihowa, ki to Iharaira whakaaturanga, ki te whakawhetai ki te ingoa o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_122:5">122:5</span> Kua whakaturia hoki ki reira nga torona
whakawa, nga torona o te whare o Rawiri.

<span id="an_122:6">122:6</span> ¶ Inoia he ata noho mo Hiruharama: ka
whiwhi ki te pai te hunga e aroha ana ki a koe.

<span id="an_122:7">122:7</span> Kia mau te rongo ki ou taiepa, me te
pai ki ou whare kingi.

<span id="an_122:8">122:8</span> He mea mo oku teina, mo oku hoa, taku e
mea nei, Kia mau te rongo ki roto ki a koe.

<span id="an_122:9">122:9</span> He whakaaro ki te whare o Ihowa, o to
tatou Atua, ka rapu ahau i te pai mou.

<span id="an_123:1">123:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka anga atu
oku kanohi ki a koe, e koe e noho mai nei i nga rangi.

<span id="an_123:2">123:2</span> Ina, pera tonu nga kanohi o nga pononga
e titiro nei ki te ringa o to ratou rangatira, nga kanohi hoki o te
kotiro ki te ringa o tona rangatira wahine; me o matou kanohi e titiro
nei ki a Ihowa, ki to matou Atua, kia tohu ra ano ia i a matou.

<span id="an_123:3">123:3</span> Tohungia matou, e Ihowa, tohungia
matou: kua tino kapi hoki matou i te whakahawea.

<span id="an_123:4">123:4</span> Kapi tonu to matou wairua i te whakahi
a te hunga e noho noa ana, i te whakahawea a te hunga whakakake.

<span id="an_124:1">124:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri.
Me kaua a Ihowa i a tatou, he ki tenei ma Iharaira:

<span id="an_124:2">124:2</span> Me kaua a Ihowa i a tatou, i te
whakatikanga mai o te tangata ki a tatou;

<span id="an_124:3">124:3</span> Penei kua horomia oratia tatou e ratou,
i te muranga o to ratou riri ki a tatou.

<span id="an_124:4">124:4</span> Kua ngaro tatou i nga wai, kua
taupokina o tatou wairua e te ia.

<span id="an_124:5">124:5</span> Penei kua taupokina o tatou wairua e
nga wai whakakake.

<span id="an_124:6">124:6</span> ¶ Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa, kihai nei i
tuku i a tatou hei ngaunga ma o ratou niho.

<span id="an_124:7">124:7</span> Kua mawhiti o tatou wairua, me he manu
i roto i te mahanga a nga kaihopu; kua motu te mahanga, a mawhiti ana
tatou.

<span id="an_124:8">124:8</span> Kei te ingoa o Ihowa he awhina mo
tatou, kei te kaihanga i te rangi, i te whenua.

<span id="an_125:1">125:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ko te hunga
e whakawhirinaki ana ki a Ihowa ka rite ki Maunga Hiona, e kore nei e
taea te whakangaueue, pumau tonu ake ake.

<span id="an_125:2">125:2</span> Me nga maunga e taiawhio nei i
Hiruharama, te karapoti a Ihowa i tona iwi, aianei a ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_125:3">125:3</span> E kore hoki te tokotoko a te
whakaarokore e waiho tonu i runga i te wahi o te hunga tika: kei totoro
te ringa o te hunga tika ki te kino.

<span id="an_125:4">125:4</span> ¶ Kia pai tau mahi, e Ihowa, ki te
hunga pai, ki te hunga he tika nei o ratou ngakau.

<span id="an_125:5">125:5</span> Ko te hunga ia e peka ke ana ki o ratou
ara kopikopiko, ma Ihowa ratou e arahi tahi atu me nga kaimahi i te
kino. Kia mau te rongo ki a Iharaira.

<span id="an_126:1">126:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I ta Ihowa
whakahokinga mai i nga pononga o Hiona i rite matou ki te hunga e
moehewa ana.

<span id="an_126:2">126:2</span> Katahi to matou mangai ka ki i te kata,
to matou arero hoki i te waiata: katahi ka korerotia i roto i nga
tauiwi, He nui nga mahi a Ihowa ki a ratou.

<span id="an_126:3">126:3</span> He mea nunui a Ihowa i mea ai mo tatou,
a e koa ana tatou.

<span id="an_126:4">126:4</span> ¶ E Ihowa, whakahokia matou i te
whakarau: kia pera me nga awa o te tonga.

<span id="an_126:5">126:5</span> Ko te hunga e rui ana i runga i te
roimata, ka kokoti i runga i te hari.

<span id="an_126:6">126:6</span> Ahakoa haere tangi atu ia me te kawe i
ana purapura hei whakatokanga; tera ia e haere hari mai ano me te mau
mai i ana paihere.

<span id="an_127:1">127:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Horomona.
Ki te kore e hanga e Ihowa te whare, he maumau mahi ta nga kaihanga; ki
te kore e tiakina e Ihowa te pa, maumau mataara noa te kaitiaki.

<span id="an_127:2">127:2</span> He maumau to koutou ara wawe, to koutou
noho roa i te po, ta koutou kai i te taro o te mauiui: ko tana moe tena
ka homai nei ki tana e aroha ai.

<span id="an_127:3">127:3</span> Na he taonga pumau na Ihowa nga
tamariki, ko nga hua ano o te kopu tana utu.

<span id="an_127:4">127:4</span> E rite ana ki nga pere i te ringaringa
o te tangata kaha te whanau o te taitamarikitanga.

<span id="an_127:5">127:5</span> Ka hari te tangata kua ki nei tana papa
pere i a ratou: e kore ratou e whakama, ina korero ki o ratou hoariri i
te kuwaha.

<span id="an_128:1">128:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Ka hari nga
tangata katoa e wehi ana i a Ihowa: e haere ana i ana ara.

<span id="an_128:2">128:2</span> E kai hoki koe i te mahinga a ou ringa:
e hari koe, a ka tau te pai ki a koe.

<span id="an_128:3">128:3</span> E rite tau wahine ki te waina hua, i
roto rawa i tou whare: au tamariki ki nga mahuri oriwa, i nga taha o tau
tepu.

<span id="an_128:4">128:4</span> Na he pera te manaaki mo te tangata e
wehi ana i a Ihowa.

<span id="an_128:5">128:5</span> Ka Manaakitia koe e Ihowa i Hiona; a e
kite koe i te pai o Hiruharama i nga ra katoa e ora ai koe.

<span id="an_128:6">128:6</span> Ae, e kite koe i nga tamariki a au
tamariki. Kia mau te rongo ki a Iharaira.

<span id="an_129:1">129:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. He ki tenei
ma Iharaira, Ka maha a ratou tukinotanga i ahau o toku tamarikitanga
ake;

<span id="an_129:2">129:2</span> Ka maha a ratou tukinotanga i ahau o
toku tamarikitanga ake; heoi kihai ahau i taea e ratou.

<span id="an_129:3">129:3</span> I parautia toku tuara e nga kaiparau;
he roa a ratou parautanga.

<span id="an_129:4">129:4</span> He tika ta Ihowa: motu pu i a ia nga
aho a te hunga kino.

<span id="an_129:5">129:5</span> ¶ Kia whakama, kia whakahokia ki muri,
te hunga katoa e kino nei ki Hiona.

<span id="an_129:6">129:6</span> Kia rite ratou ki te tarutaru i nga
tuanui, e memenge nei i te mea kiano i tupu ake.

<span id="an_129:7">129:7</span> E kore nei e ki te ringa o te kaikoti,
te uma hoki o te kaipaihere.

<span id="an_129:8">129:8</span> E kore ano te hunga e haere ana i te
taha e mea, Kia tau ki a koutou te manaaki a Ihowa: ko ta matou manaaki
tenei ki a koutou i runga i te ingoa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_130:1">130:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. I karanga
ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa, i roto i nga hohonu.

<span id="an_130:2">130:2</span> E te Ariki, whakarongo mai ki toku reo:
kia anga mai ou taringa ki toku reo inoi.

<span id="an_130:3">130:3</span> Me i maharatia e koe nga kino, e Ihowa,
ko wai, e te Ariki, e tu?

<span id="an_130:4">130:4</span> Otira he muru hara tau, e wehingia ai
koe.

<span id="an_130:5">130:5</span> ¶ E tatari ana ahau ki a Ihowa; e
tatari ana toku wairua: e tumanako ana hoki ahau ki tana kupu.

<span id="an_130:6">130:6</span> Ko te taringa o toku wairua i te Ariki
nui atu i to te hunga e whanga ana ki te ata; ae, i to te hunga e whanga
ana ki te ata.

<span id="an_130:7">130:7</span> E Iharaira, kia tumanako ki a Ihowa,
kei a Ihowa hoki te mahi tohu, a kei a ia te hokonga nui.

<span id="an_130:8">130:8</span> A mana a Iharaira e hoko i roto i ona
he katoa.

<span id="an_131:1">131:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri. E
Ihowa, ehara toku i te ngakau whakapehapeha: ehara ano oku i te kanohi
whakakake: kahore hoki ahau e rahurahu ki nga mea nunui, e kore nei e
taea e ahau.

<span id="an_131:2">131:2</span> He pono kua meinga e ahau toku wairua
kia tau, a kia mahaki, pera i to te tamaiti kua wehea i te u o tona
whaea: he rite toku wairua ki te tamaiti katahi nei ka wehe i te u.

<span id="an_131:3">131:3</span> E Iharaira, kia tumanako ki a Ihowa:
aianei a ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_132:1">132:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. E Ihowa,
maharatia a Rawiri, me ona mamaetanga ngakau katoa;

<span id="an_132:2">132:2</span> Tana oati ki a Ihowa, tana kupu
taurangi ki te Mea Nui o Hakopa;

<span id="an_132:3">132:3</span> E kore rawa ahau e tae ki toku whare e
noho ai ahau, e eke ranei ki runga ki toku moenga;

<span id="an_132:4">132:4</span> E kore ahau e tuku i oku kanohi kia
moe, i oku kamo kia nenewha;

<span id="an_132:5">132:5</span> Kia kitea ra ano e ahau he wahi mo
Ihowa, he nohoanga mo te Mea Nui o Hakopa.

<span id="an_132:6">132:6</span> Na i rangona e matou ki Eparata, i
kitea ki nga mara o te ngahere.

<span id="an_132:7">132:7</span> Ka haere matou ki roto ki ona
tapenakara; ka koropiko ki tona turanga waewae.

<span id="an_132:8">132:8</span> E ara, e Ihowa, ki tou okiokinga, a
koe, me te aaka o tou kaha.

<span id="an_132:9">132:9</span> Kia whakakakahuria au tohunga ki te
tika; kia hamama tau hunga tapu i te hari.

<span id="an_132:10">132:10</span> Whakaaro ki a Rawiri, ki tau pononga:
kaua e whakapeaua atu te mata o tau i whakawahi ai.

<span id="an_132:11">132:11</span> ¶ Kua oati pono a Ihowa ki a Rawiri,
e kore ia e tahuri ke i tena; Ka whakanohoia e ahau tetahi hua o tou
kopu ki tou torona.

<span id="an_132:12">132:12</span> Ki te puritia e au tama taku
kawenata, me taku whakaaturanga e ako ai ahau ki a ratou, ka noho ano a
ratou tama ki tou torona ake ake.

<span id="an_132:13">132:13</span> Kua whiriwhiria hoki e Ihowa a Hiona;
kua hiahiatia e ia hei nohoanga mona.

<span id="an_132:14">132:14</span> Ko toku okiokinga tenei ake ake; ko
konei ahau noho ai, kua hiahiatia hoki e ahau.

<span id="an_132:15">132:15</span> Ka manaakitia rawatia e ahau tana
kai; ka whakamakonatia e ahau ona rawakore ki te taro.

<span id="an_132:16">132:16</span> Ka whakakakahuria hoki e ahau ona
tohunga ki te whakaoranga; a ka hamama tona hunga tapu i te hari.

<span id="an_132:17">132:17</span> Ka meinga e ahau kia pihi ki reira te
haona o Rawiri: kua whakapaia e ahau he rama mo taku i whakawahi ai.

<span id="an_132:18">132:18</span> Ka whakakakahuria e ahau ona hoariri
ki te whakama; a ka matomato tona karauna i runga i a ia.

<span id="an_133:1">133:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na Rawiri.
Na, ano te pai, ano te ahuareka o te nohoanga o nga teina, o nga tuakana
i runga i te whakaaro kotahi!

<span id="an_133:2">133:2</span> Tona rite kei te hinu utu nui i runga i
te upoko, i heke iho nei ki te pahau, ae ki te pahau o Arona; i heke iho
nei ki te remu o ona kakahu:

<span id="an_133:3">133:3</span> Kei te tomairangi ano o Heremona, kei
tera i heke iho ki nga maunga o Hiona: i whakahaua iho hoki e Ihowa te
manaaki mo reira, te ora mo ake tonu atu.

<span id="an_134:1">134:1</span> ¶ He waiata; he pikitanga. Na,
whakapaingia a Ihowa, e nga pononga katoa a Ihowa, e tu nei i te whare o
Ihowa i te po.

<span id="an_134:2">134:2</span> Totoro ake o koutou ringa ki te wahi
tapu, whakapaingia hoki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_134:3">134:3</span> Ma Ihowa koe e manaaki i roto i Hiona,
mana, ma te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua.

<span id="an_135:1">135:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.
Whakamoemititia te ingoa o Ihowa; whakamoemititia ia, e nga pononga a
Ihowa.

<span id="an_135:2">135:2</span> E koutou e tu nei i roto i te whare o
Ihowa, i nga marae o te whare o to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_135:3">135:3</span> Whakamoemititia a Ihowa; he pai hoki a
Ihowa; himene atu ki tona ingoa; he mea ahuareka hoki tena.

<span id="an_135:4">135:4</span> Kua whiriwhiria hoki e Ihowa a Hakopa
mana, a Iharaira hei tino taonga mona.

<span id="an_135:5">135:5</span> ¶ E matau ana hoki ahau he nui a Ihowa:
kei runga atu hoki to tatou Ariki i nga atua katoa.

<span id="an_135:6">135:6</span> Ko nga mea katoa i pai ai a Ihowa, kua
oti i a ia, i te rangi, i te whenua, i nga moana, i nga wahi hohonu
katoa.

<span id="an_135:7">135:7</span> Nana i pupu ake ai nga kohu i nga pito
o te whenua: i hanga e ia nga uira mo te ua; e whakaputaina mai ana e ia
te hau i roto i ona whare taonga.

<span id="an_135:8">135:8</span> Nana nei i patu nga matamua o Ihipa, a
te tangata, a te kararehe;

<span id="an_135:9">135:9</span> I tonoa e ia he tohu, he merekara ki
waenganui ou, e Ihipa: ki runga ki a Parao ratou ko ana pononga katoa.

<span id="an_135:10">135:10</span> Nana i patu nga iwi maha, i whakamate
nga kingi rarahi;

<span id="an_135:11">135:11</span> A Hihona kingi o nga Amori, a Oka
kingi o Pahana, me nga rangatiratanga katoa o Kanaana;

<span id="an_135:12">135:12</span> A homai ana e ia to ratou whenua hei
kainga pumau, hei kainga pumau mo Iharaira, mo tana iwi.

<span id="an_135:13">135:13</span> E Ihowa, pumau tonu tou ingoa, me tou
maharatanga, e Ihowa, ki nga whakatupuranga katoa.

<span id="an_135:14">135:14</span> Ka whakawa hoki a Ihowa mo tana iwi;
a ka puta ke tona whakaaro ki ana pononga.

<span id="an_135:15">135:15</span> ¶ He hiriwa, he koura nga whakapakoko
a nga tauiwi, he mahi na te ringa tangata.

<span id="an_135:16">135:16</span> He mangai o ratou, a kahore e korero:
he kanohi o ratou, a kahore e kite:

<span id="an_135:17">135:17</span> He taringa o ratou, a kahore e rongo:
kahore ano he manawa i o ratou mangai.

<span id="an_135:18">135:18</span> Ka rite ki a ratou te hunga nana
ratou i hanga; ae, me nga tangata katoa e whakawhirinaki ana ki a ratou.

<span id="an_135:19">135:19</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o
Iharaira; whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o Arona;

<span id="an_135:20">135:20</span> Whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te whare o
Riwai; whakapaingia a Ihowa, e te hunga katoa e wehi ana i a Ihowa;

<span id="an_135:21">135:21</span> Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa i roto i
Hiona, e noho nei i Hiruharama. Whakapaingia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_136:1">136:1</span> ¶ Whakawhetai ki a Ihowa, he pai hoki
ia: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:2">136:2</span> Whakawhetai ki te Atua o nga atua: he
mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:3">136:3</span> Whakawhetai ki te Ariki o nga ariki: he
mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:4">136:4</span> E mahi nei tona kotahi i nga merekara
nunui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:5">136:5</span> I tohunga rawa nei ki te hanga i nga
rangi: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:6">136:6</span> I whakatakoto nei i te whenua ki runga
ki nga wai: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:7">136:7</span> Ki te kaihanga i nga whakamarama nunui:
he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:8">136:8</span> I te ra hei tohutohu i te awatea: he
mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:9">136:9</span> I te marama me nga whetu hei tohutohu i
te po: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:10">136:10</span> ¶ Ki te kaipatu i Ihipa, ara i a
ratou matamua: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:11">136:11</span> A arahina mai ana a Iharaira i
waenganui i a ratou: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:12">136:12</span> Na te ringa kaha me te takakau maro:
he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:13">136:13</span> I tapahi nei i te Moana Whero a motu
rawa: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:14">136:14</span> A meinga ana a Iharaira kia haere ra
waenganui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:15">136:15</span> A hurihia ana a Parao me ana mano ki
te Moana Whero: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:16">136:16</span> I arahi nei i tana iwi ra te koraha:
he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:17">136:17</span> I patu nei i nga kingi nunui: he mau
tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:18">136:18</span> I whakamate nei i nga kingi rongo
nui: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:19">136:19</span> I a Hihona kingi o nga Amori: he mau
tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:20">136:20</span> I a Oka kingi o Pahana: he mau tonu
hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:21">136:21</span> A homai ana to ratou whenua hei
kainga pumau: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu;

<span id="an_136:22">136:22</span> Hei kainga pumau mo Iharaira, mo tana
pononga: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:23">136:23</span> ¶ I mahara nei ki a tatou i to tatou
itinga; he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu:

<span id="an_136:24">136:24</span> A whakaorangia ana tatou i o tatou
hoariri: he mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:25">136:25</span> Ko ia te kaihomai i te kai ma nga
kikokiko katoa: he mau tonu hoki tana inahi tohu.

<span id="an_136:26">136:26</span> Whakawhetai ki te Atua o te rangi: he
mau tonu hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_137:1">137:1</span> ¶ I te taha o nga wai o Papurona, noho
ana tatou i reira, ae, tangi ana tatou, ia tatou i mahara ai ki Hiona.

<span id="an_137:2">137:2</span> Whakairia ake e tatou a tatou hapa ki
runga ki nga wirou i waenganui o reira.

<span id="an_137:3">137:3</span> No te mea i tono i reira te hunga nana
tatou i herehere ki etahi waiata i a tatou, me te hunga nana tatou i
tukino i tono mai he hari i a tatou, i mea mai, Waiatatia mai ki a matou
tetahi o nga waiate o Hiona.

<span id="an_137:4">137:4</span> Me pehea matou ka waiata ai i te waiata
a Ihowa i te whenua tauhou?

<span id="an_137:5">137:5</span> Ki te wareware ahau ki a koe, e
Hiruharama, kia wareware toku ringa matau ki tana mahi.

<span id="an_137:6">137:6</span> Ki te kore ahau e mahara ki a koe, kia
piri toku arero ki toku ngao; ki te kore ahau e whakanui i Hiruharama ki
runga ake i taku mea i tino hari ai.

<span id="an_137:7">137:7</span> ¶ E Ihowa, maharatia nga tama a Eroma i
te ra o Hiruharama; ta ratou meatanga, Whakahoroa, whakahoroa, a taea
rawatia ano tona turanga.

<span id="an_137:8">137:8</span> E te tamahine o Papurona, meake nei
whakangaromia, ka hari te tangata e utua ai koe mo tau i mea ai ki a
matou.

<span id="an_137:9">137:9</span> Ka hari te tangata e hopu ana, e ta ana
i au mea nohinohi ki runga ki te kohatu.

<span id="an_138:1">138:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Ka whakapaua toku ngakau
ki te whakawhetai ki a koe: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe i te aroaro o
nga atua.

<span id="an_138:2">138:2</span> Ka koropiko atu ahau ki te ritenga o
tou temepara tapu, a ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa, mo tou aroha me tou
pono: kua whakanuia hoki e koe tau kupu ki runga ake i tou ingoa katoa.

<span id="an_138:3">138:3</span> I whakahoki kupu mai koe ki ahau i te
ra i karanga ai ahau: a whakahirihiritia ana e koe toku wairua ki te
kaha.

<span id="an_138:4">138:4</span> Ka whakamoemiti nga kingi katoa o te
whenua ki a koe, e Ihowa, kua rongo hoki ratou ki nga kupu a tou mangai.

<span id="an_138:5">138:5</span> Ae, e waiata ratou mo nga ara o Ihowa:
he nui hoki te kororia o Ihowa.

<span id="an_138:6">138:6</span> ¶ Ahakoa hoki kei runga rawa a Ihowa, e
titiro iho ana ano ia ki te hunga papaku: tena ko te tangata whakakake,
i tawhiti ano kua matauria e ia.

<span id="an_138:7">138:7</span> Ahakoa haere ahau i waenganui o te he,
mau ahau e whakahauora: ka totoro tou ringa ki te riri o oku hoa
whawhai, ma tou ringa matau ano ahau e whakaora.

<span id="an_138:8">138:8</span> Ma Ihowa e whakaoti aku mea: e Ihowa, e
mau ana tau mahi tohu ake ake; kaua e whakarerea nga mahi a ou ringa.

<span id="an_139:1">139:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He Himene
na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kua tirotirohia ahau e koe, kua mohiotia ano e koe.

<span id="an_139:2">139:2</span> E matau ana koe ki toku nohoanga iho,
ki toku whakatikanga ake; e mohio ana koe ki oku whakaaro i tawhiti.

<span id="an_139:3">139:3</span> E kitea putia ana e koe toku ara me
toku takotoranga iho; e matatau ana hoki koe ki oku ara katoa.

<span id="an_139:4">139:4</span> Kahore rawa hoki he kupu i toku arero,
i toe i a koe te mohio, e Ihowa.

<span id="an_139:5">139:5</span> Kua hanga a muri, a mua, oku e koe: kua
pa ano tou ringa ki ahau.

<span id="an_139:6">139:6</span> He mea whakamiharo rawa, kei tawhiti
atu hoki i ahau, tenei matauranga: kei runga noa atu, e kore e taea e
ahau.

<span id="an_139:7">139:7</span> ¶ Me haere ahau ki hea i tou wairua? Me
oma ranei ahau ki hea i tou aroaro?

<span id="an_139:8">139:8</span> Ki te kake ahau ki te rangi, kei reira
koe: ki te wharikitia e ahau toku moenga i roto i te reinga, kei reira
ano koe.

<span id="an_139:9">139:9</span> Ki te tango ahau ki nga pakau o te ata,
a ka noho ki nga topito o te moana;

<span id="an_139:10">139:10</span> Kei reira ano tou ringa hei arahi i
ahau, tou matau hei pupuru i ahau.

<span id="an_139:11">139:11</span> Ki te mea ahau, He pono, tera ahau e
hipokina e te pouri, a ko te marama i tetahi taha oku, i tetahi taha, ka
meinga he po;

<span id="an_139:12">139:12</span> Ahakoa te pouri kahore e huna mai i a
koe, engari ka marama te po ano ko te ao: ki a koe rite tahi te pouri me
te marama.

<span id="an_139:13">139:13</span> I a koe hoki oku whatumanawa: nau
hoki ahau i hipoki i roto i te kopu o toku whaea.

<span id="an_139:14">139:14</span> Ka whakawhetai ahau ki a koe; he mea
whakawehi, he mea whakamiharo toku hanganga; he mahi whakamiharo au
mahi, mohio rawa ano toku wairua ki tena.

<span id="an_139:15">139:15</span> Kihai i huna oku wahi i a koe, i ahau
e hanga ngarotia ana, e ata whakairohia ana i nga wahi hohonu rawa o te
whenua.

<span id="an_139:16">139:16</span> I kite ou kanohi i ahau, kahore ano
kia ahua noa: i tuhituhia katoatia ano hoki oku wahi ki tau pukapuka, i
nga rangi i whakaahua ai, i te mea kahore ano tetahi i oti noa.

<span id="an_139:17">139:17</span> ¶ Kia pehea mai hoki te matenui o ou
whakaaro ki ahau, e te Atua; koia ano te ranea, ina huihuia!

<span id="an_139:18">139:18</span> Ki te taua e ahau, maha atu i te
onepu: ka oho ake ahau, kei a koe tonu ahau.

<span id="an_139:19">139:19</span> He pono ka patua e koe, e te Atua, te
tangata kino: mawehe koia atu i ahau, e nga tangata toto.

<span id="an_139:20">139:20</span> He kino hoki a ratou kupu mou: e
whakahua noa ana ou hoariri i tou ingoa.

<span id="an_139:21">139:21</span> Kahore ianei ahau, e Ihowa, e kino ki
te hunga e kino ana ki a koe? e whakarihariha hoki ki te hunga e
whakatika ana ki a koe?

<span id="an_139:22">139:22</span> He tino kino taku kino ki a ratou:
waiho iho ratou e ahau hei hoariri moku.

<span id="an_139:23">139:23</span> Tirohia iho ahau, e te Atua, kia
matau hoki koe ki toku ngakau: whakamatautauria ahau, kia matau hoki koe
ki oku whakaaro:

<span id="an_139:24">139:24</span> Kia kite mehemea kei ahau tetahi ara
o te kino, ka arahi ai i ahau i te ara pumau.

<span id="an_140:1">140:1</span> ¶ Ki te tino kaiwhakatangi. He himene
na Rawiri. Whakaorangia ahau, e Ihowa, i te tangata kino: araia atu i
ahau te tangata tutu:

<span id="an_140:2">140:2</span> E whakaaro kino nei i o ratou ngakau: e
whakamine nei i a ratou i nga wa katoa ki te whawhai.

<span id="an_140:3">140:3</span> Kua whakakoia to ratou arero, ano he
nakahi: kei raro i o ratou ngutu te wai whakamate o te neke. (Hera.

<span id="an_140:4">140:4</span> Tiakina ahau, e Ihowa, i nga ringa o te
hunga kino: araia atu i ahau te tangata tutu, kua mea nei kia tutea oku
hikoinga.

<span id="an_140:5">140:5</span> Kua huna e te hunga whakakake te
mahanga moku, me nga aho; kua horahia e ratou he kupenga ki te taha o te
ara: kua whakapikoa e ratou he rore moku. (Hera.

<span id="an_140:6">140:6</span> I mea ahau ki a Ihowa, Ko koe toku
Atua: whakarongo, e Ihowa, ki toku reo inoi.

<span id="an_140:7">140:7</span> E Ihowa, e te Ariki, e te kaha o toku
whakaoranga, nau i hipoki toku upoko i te ra o te tatauranga.

<span id="an_140:8">140:8</span> ¶ Aua e whakaaetia, e Ihowa, nga hiahia
o te tangata kino: kei taea tona whakaaro koroke; kei whakakake ratou.
(Hera.

<span id="an_140:9">140:9</span> Tena ko te upoko o te hunga e whakapae
nei i ahau, kia hipokina ratou e te kino o o ratou ngutu.

<span id="an_140:10">140:10</span> Kia taka he waro mura ki runga ki a
ratou: kia panga ratou ki te ahi, ki roto ki nga poka hohonu, kei
whakatika ake ano ratou.

<span id="an_140:11">140:11</span> E kore te tangata korero kino e
whakapumautia ki runga ki te whenua: ma te kino e aruaru te tangata
tutu, kia turakina atu ia ki raro.

<span id="an_140:12">140:12</span> E matau ana ano ahau ma Ihowa e tohe
te whakawa a te tangata e tukinotia ana, te mea hoki e rite ana ma nga
rawakore.

<span id="an_140:13">140:13</span> He pono ka whakawhetai te hunga pai
ki tou ingoa: ka noho te hunga tika ki tou aroaro.

<span id="an_141:1">141:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa, kua
tangi nei ahau ki a koe; hohoro mai ki ahau: whakarongo ki toku reo ua
karanga ahau ki a koe.

<span id="an_141:2">141:2</span> Kia whakatikaia taku inoi ki tou
aroaro, hei whakakakara; te toronga atu hoki o oku ringa ano ko te
whakahere o te ahiahi.

<span id="an_141:3">141:3</span> Homai he kaitiaki mo toku mangai, e
Ihowa: tiakina te kuwaha o oku ngutu.

<span id="an_141:4">141:4</span> Kaua e whakaangahia toku ngakau ki te
mea kino, ki te mahi i nga mahi hianga i roto i nga kaimahi i te kino:
kaua ano ahau e kai i a ratou mea papai.

<span id="an_141:5">141:5</span> ¶ Ma te tangata tika ahau e patu: he
mahi aroha tena; mana ahau e riri; he hinu tena ki runga ki te upoko;
kaua ia e paopaongia e toku upoko: ahakoa hoki i roto i to ratou kino ka
inoi tonu ahau.

<span id="an_141:6">141:6</span> E turakina ana o ratou kaiwhakawa ki te
taha o te kohatu; a ka rongo ratou i aku kupu; he reka hoki.

<span id="an_141:7">141:7</span> Pera i tetahi e haehae ana, e wawahi
ana i te whenua, e titaritaria ana o matou wheua ki te waha o te reinga.

<span id="an_141:8">141:8</span> Otiia e tau ana oku kanohi, e Ihowa, e
te Ariki, ki a koe: ko koe toku whakawhirinakitanga; kaua toku wairua e
waiho pani.

<span id="an_141:9">141:9</span> Tiakina ahau kei mau i nga mahanga i
whakatakotoria e ratou moku, i nga rore hoki a nga kaimahi i te kino.

<span id="an_141:10">141:10</span> Kia taka te hunga kino ki roto ki a
ratou kupenga ano: ko ahau ia kia mawhiti.

<span id="an_142:1">142:1</span> ¶ He Makiri na Rawiri; he inoi i a ia i
roto i te ana. He karanga ta toku reo ki a Ihowa; he inoi ta toku reo ki
a Ihowa.

<span id="an_142:2">142:2</span> Horahia ana taku inoi ki tona aroaro;
whakaaturia ana e ahau toku mate ki tona aroaro.

<span id="an_142:3">142:3</span> I te ngaromanga o toku wairua i roto i
ahau i matau koe ki toku ara: kua whakatakotoria pukutia e ratou te
mahanga moku i te ara i haere ai ahau.

<span id="an_142:4">142:4</span> ¶ Titiro ki toku taha matau, kia kite;
kahore hoki tetahi tangata e mohio ana ki ahau; kahore he piringa moku;
kahore tetahi e mahara ana ki toku wairua.

<span id="an_142:5">142:5</span> I karanga ahau ki a koe, e Ihowa: i
mea, Ko koe toku piringa, toku wahi i te whenua o te hunga ora.

<span id="an_142:6">142:6</span> Tahuri mai ki taku karanga: kua
whakaititia rawatia hoki ahau: whakaorangia ahau i oku kaitukino: he
kaha rawa hoki ratou i ahau.

<span id="an_142:7">142:7</span> Whakaputaina toku wairua i te herehere,
kia whakamoemiti ai ahau ki tou ingoa: ka karapotia ahau e te hunga
tika; nou ka atawhai nei i ahau.

<span id="an_143:1">143:1</span> ¶ He himene na Rawiri. E Ihowa,
whakarongo ki taku inoi, kia titaha mai tou taringa ki aku inoi:
whakahokia mai he kupu ki ahau i runga i tou pono, i runga i tou tika.

<span id="an_143:2">143:2</span> A kaua e anga e whakawa ki tau pononga:
ki tau titiro hoki kahore tetahi mea ora e tika.

<span id="an_143:3">143:3</span> Kua tukinotia hoki toku wairua e te
hoariri; patua iho e ia toku ora ki raro ki te whenua: meinga ana ahau e
ia kia noho i nga wahi pouri, kia rite ki nga tupapaku onamata.

<span id="an_143:4">143:4</span> Na reira i ngaro ai toku wairua i roto
i ahau: moti rawa toku ngakau i roto i ahau.

<span id="an_143:5">143:5</span> E mahara ana ahau ki nga ra onamata; e
whakaaro ana ki au mahi katoa: e whakaaroaro ana ahau ki nga meatanga a
ou ringa.

<span id="an_143:6">143:6</span> Totoro tonu atu oku ringa ki a koe: e
hiainu ana toku wairua ki a koe, ano he whenua mauiui. (Hera.

<span id="an_143:7">143:7</span> ¶ Hohoro te whakahoki kupu mai ki ahau,
e Ihowa; ka hemo toku wairua: kei huna tou mata ki ahau; kei rite ahau
ki te hunga e heke ana ki te poka.

<span id="an_143:8">143:8</span> Meinga kia rongo ahau ki tou aroha i te
ata; e whakawhirinaki ana hoki ahau ki a koe: meinga kia matau ahau ki
te ara e haere ai ahau; kua ara nei hoki toku wairua ki a koe.

<span id="an_143:9">143:9</span> Whakaorangia ahau, e Ihowa, i oku
hoariri: ka kuhu nei ahau ki roto ki a koe.

<span id="an_143:10">143:10</span> Whakaakona ahau ki te mea i tau e pai
ai; ko koe hoki toku Atua: he pai tou wairua; arahina ahau ki te whenua
o te tika.

<span id="an_143:11">143:11</span> Whakahauorangia ahau, e Ihowa, he
whakaaro ki tou ingoa; whakaarohia tou tika, ka whakaputa ake i toku
wairua i roto i te pouri.

<span id="an_143:12">143:12</span> Aroha mai hoki, a huna oku hoariri:
whakangaromia katoatia ano nga kaitukino o toku wairua: he pononga hoki
ahau nau.

<span id="an_144:1">144:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri. Kia whakapaingia a Ihowa,
toku kamaka, e whakaako nei i oku ringa ki te whawhai, i oku maihao ki
te tatau;

<span id="an_144:2">144:2</span> Ko te atawhai moku, ko toku pa, ko toku
pourewa me toku kaiwhakaora; ko toku whakangungu rakau, ko taku e
whakawhirinaki ai; ko te kaipehi hoki o toku iwi ki raro i ahau.

<span id="an_144:3">144:3</span> E Ihowa, he aha te tangata i maharatia
ai ia e koe? Te tama ranei a te tangata i whakaaroa ai ia e koe?

<span id="an_144:4">144:4</span> Ko te rite o te tangata kei te mea
memeha noa: ona ra me te mea he atarangi e rere atu ana.

<span id="an_144:5">144:5</span> Whakapikoa iho ou rangi e Ihowa, a heke
iho: pa ki nga maunga, a ka pongere.

<span id="an_144:6">144:6</span> Kokiritia mai he uira hei whakamarara i
a ratou: koperea mai au pere, kia whati ai ratou.

<span id="an_144:7">144:7</span> Totoro iho tou ringa i runga: tangohia
ahau, whakaorangia ahau i nga wai nunui, i te ringa o nga tangata ke;

<span id="an_144:8">144:8</span> E korero teka nei to ratou mangai, a he
ringa matau teka to ratou ringa matau.

<span id="an_144:9">144:9</span> ¶ Ka waiatatia e ahau he waiata hou ki
a koe, e te Atua: ka himene atu ahau ki a koe i runga i te hatere aho
tekau.
