<span id="an_144:10">144:10</span> Ko ia te kaihomai i te whakaoranga ki
nga kingi, te kaiwhakaora i a Rawiri, i tana pononga, i te hoari
whakamate.

<span id="an_144:11">144:11</span> Tangohia ahau, whakaorangia hoki i
nga ringa o nga tangata ke, e korero teka nei o ratou mangai, a he ringa
matau teka to ratou ringa matau.

<span id="an_144:12">144:12</span> A, kia rite a matou tama i to ratou
taitamarikitanga ki nga mahuri e tupu ake ana; a matou tamahine hoki ki
nga kohatu kokonga, whakapaipai rawa, no te whare rangatira te tauira;

<span id="an_144:13">144:13</span> Kia ki a matou pakoro, mo te tiki noa
atu i tena mea, i tena mea: kia mano, kia tini nga hua o a matou hipi i
o matou parae;

<span id="an_144:14">144:14</span> Kia taimaha a matou kau i nga
pikaunga; kia kahore he pakarutanga mai ki roto, he whatinga atu hoki ki
waho, a kia kahore he aue i o matou huarahi;

<span id="an_144:15">144:15</span> Ka hari te iwi e pena ana: ae, ka
hari te iwi ko Ihowa nei to ratou Atua.

<span id="an_145:1">145:1</span> ¶ Na Rawiri, he whakamoemiti. Ka
whakanui ahau i a koe, e toku Atua, e te Kingi: ka whakapai ki tou ingoa
ake ake.

<span id="an_145:2">145:2</span> Ka whakapai ahau ki a koe i nga ra
katoa: ka whakamoemiti ki tou ingoa ake ake.

<span id="an_145:3">145:3</span> He nui a Ihowa, kia nui ano te
whakamoemiti ki a ia: e kore e taea tona nui te rapu.

<span id="an_145:4">145:4</span> Ma tetahi whakatupuranga e whakamoemiti
au mahi, tae noa atu ki tetahi whakatupuranga; e korero hoki au mahi
nunui.

<span id="an_145:5">145:5</span> Ka korerotia e ahau te kororia, te
honore o tou nui, me au mahi whakamiharo.

<span id="an_145:6">145:6</span> Ka korerotia ano e te tangata te kaha o
au mahi whakamataku: maku ano e korero tou nui.

<span id="an_145:7">145:7</span> Ka whakapuakina e ratou te mahara ki te
nui o tou pai: ka waiatatia ano tou tika.

<span id="an_145:8">145:8</span> He atawhai a Ihowa, he aroha: he puhoi
ki te riri, he nui tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_145:9">145:9</span> He pai a Ihowa ki nga mea katoa; kei
runga ano tona aroha i ana mahi katoa.

<span id="an_145:10">145:10</span> ¶ E whakamoemititia koe, e Ihowa, e
au mahi katoa: e whakapaingia e tou hunga tapu.

<span id="an_145:11">145:11</span> Ma ratou e korero te kororia o tou
kingitanga, e kauwhau hoki tou kaha;

<span id="an_145:12">145:12</span> Kia mohiotia ai e nga tama a te
tangata ana mahi nunui, me te kororia o te maruwehi o tona kingitanga.

<span id="an_145:13">145:13</span> He kingitanga mutungakore tou
kingitanga; kei nga whakatupuranga katoa tou rangatiratanga.

<span id="an_145:14">145:14</span> E tautokona ana e Ihowa te hunga
katoa e hinga ana: e whakaarahia ake ana hoki e ia te hunga katoa kua
whakapikoa iho.

<span id="an_145:15">145:15</span> E tatari ana ki a koe nga kanohi o te
katoa; a e hoatu ana e koe ki a ratou ta ratou kai i te wa e tika ai.

<span id="an_145:16">145:16</span> E whakatuwhera ana koe i tou ringa, a
makona iho i a koe te hiahia o nga mea ora katoa.

<span id="an_145:17">145:17</span> He tika nga ara katoa o Ihowa: he
tapu hoki ana mahi katoa.

<span id="an_145:18">145:18</span> E tata ana a Ihowa ki te hunga katoa
e karanga ana ki a ia: ki te hunga katoa e karanga pono ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_145:19">145:19</span> Ka whakamana e ia te hiahia o te
hunga e wehi ana i a ia: e whakarongo hoki ia ki ta ratou tangi, a ka
whakaora i a ratou.

<span id="an_145:20">145:20</span> Ko Ihowa hei tiaki i te hunga katoa e
aroha ana ki a ia: ko te hunga kino katoa ia e ngaro i a ia.

<span id="an_145:21">145:21</span> Ma toku mangai e korero te
whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa: kia whakapai ano hoki nga kikokiko katoa ki
tona ingoa tapu ake ake.

<span id="an_146:1">146:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. E toku
wairua, whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_146:2">146:2</span> I ahau e ora nei ka whakamoemiti ahau
ki a Ihowa; ka himene ahau ki toku Atua i ahau i te ao nei.

<span id="an_146:3">146:3</span> Kei whakawhirinaki ki nga rangatira, ki
te tama ranei a te tangata, kahore nei he awhina.

<span id="an_146:4">146:4</span> Ko te putanga atu o tona wairua, hoki
ana ia ki tona oneone; kore iho ona whakaaro i taua ra pu ano.

<span id="an_146:5">146:5</span> ¶ Ka hari te tangata ko te Atua nei o
Hakopa tona kaiawhina: ko tana e tumanako ai ko Ihowa, ko tona Atua;

<span id="an_146:6">146:6</span> Ko te kaihanga o te rangi, o te whenua,
o te moana, o nga mea katoa o reira; e pupuri nei i te pono ake ake;

<span id="an_146:7">146:7</span> E tohe nei i te whakawa a te hunga e
tukinotia ana: e whangai nei i te hunga mate hiakai: ko Ihowa hei wewete
i nga herehere:

<span id="an_146:8">146:8</span> Ko Ihowa hei whakatitiro i nga matapo:
ko Ihowa hei whakaara i te hunga kua whakapikoa iho: e aroha ana a Ihowa
ki te hunga tika.

<span id="an_146:9">146:9</span> Ko Ihowa hei tiaki i nga manene; ko ia
hei tautoko i te pani, i te pouaru: ko te ara ia o te hunga kino, ka
huripokitia e ia.

<span id="an_146:10">146:10</span> Ko Ihowa hei kingi ake ake, ae, ko
tou Atua, e Hiona, tae noa ki nga whakatupuranga katoa. Whakamoemititia
a Ihowa.

<span id="an_147:1">147:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa; he pai hoki
te himene ki to tatou Atua: ahuareka rawa, ataahua tonu te whakamoemiti.

<span id="an_147:2">147:2</span> Ko Ihowa hei hanga i Hiruharama: mana
hoki nga whati o Iharaira e kohikohi.

<span id="an_147:3">147:3</span> Ko ia hei rongoa i te hunga ngakau
maru: mana e takai o ratou wahi mamae.

<span id="an_147:4">147:4</span> E taua ana e ia nga whetu, te maha: e
huaina ana hoki e ia o ratou ingoa katoa.

<span id="an_147:5">147:5</span> He nui to tatou Ariki, he nui hoki tona
kaha: e kore e taea tona matauranga te whakaaro.

<span id="an_147:6">147:6</span> Ko Ihowa te kaitautoko mo te hunga
mahaki: ka turakina e ia te hunga kino ki te whenua.

<span id="an_147:7">147:7</span> Waiata, whakawhetai ki a Ihowa: himene
i runga i te hapa ki to tatou Atua:

<span id="an_147:8">147:8</span> Ko ia nei te kaiuwhi i te rangi ki nga
kapua, te kaihanga i te ua mo te whenua: e whakatupu ana ia i te
tarutaru ki runga ki nga maunga.

<span id="an_147:9">147:9</span> E homai ana e ia he kai ma te kirehe:
ma nga pi raweni hoki ina tangi.

<span id="an_147:10">147:10</span> E kore ia e ahuareka ki te kaha o te
hoiho: e kore ia e manako ki nga waewae o te tangata.

<span id="an_147:11">147:11</span> E manako ana a Ihowa ki te hunga e
wehi ana i a ia, ki te hunga e tumanako ana ki tona aroha.

<span id="an_147:12">147:12</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, e
Hiruharama: whakamoemititia tou Atua, e Hiona.

<span id="an_147:13">147:13</span> Nana nei hoki i whakakaha nga tutaki
o ou tatau: manaakitia ana e ia au tamariki i roto i a koe.

<span id="an_147:14">147:14</span> Nana ano i mau ai te rongo i roto i
ou rohe: nana koe i makona ai i te witi pai rawa.

<span id="an_147:15">147:15</span> E tukua ana e ia tana kupu ki te
whenua: tere rawa te rere o tana kupu.

<span id="an_147:16">147:16</span> E homai ana e ia te hukarere ano he
huruhuru hipi: e whakatitaritaria ana te haupapa ano he pungarehu.

<span id="an_147:17">147:17</span> Maka mai ana e ia tana hauhunga ano
he maramara: ko wai e tu i mua i tana matao?

<span id="an_147:18">147:18</span> E tukua ana e ia tana kupu, a
whakarewaina ana aua mea: ka meinga tana hau kia pupuhi, rere ana nga
wai.

<span id="an_147:19">147:19</span> E whakakitea ana e ia tana kupu ki a
Hakopa; ana tikanga, me ana whakaritenga ki a Iharaira.

<span id="an_147:20">147:20</span> Kahore i pera tana hanga ki tetahi
iwi; kihai ano ana whakaritenga i mohiotia e ratou. whakamoemititia a
Ihowa.

<span id="an_148:1">148:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.
Whakamoemititia a Ihowa i runga i nga rangi: whakamoemititia ia i nga
wahi tiketike.

<span id="an_148:2">148:2</span> Whakamoemititia ia, e ana anahera
katoa: whakamoemititia ia, e ana mano whaioio.

<span id="an_148:3">148:3</span> Whakamoemititia ia, e te ra, e te
marama: whakamoemititia ia, e nga whetu whakamarama katoa.

<span id="an_148:4">148:4</span> Whakamoemititia ia, e nga rangi o nga
rangi, e nga wai hoki o runga atu i nga rangi.

<span id="an_148:5">148:5</span> Kia whakamoemititia e ratou te ingoa o
Ihowa: nana hoki i whakahau, a kua hanga ratou.

<span id="an_148:6">148:6</span> Nana hoki aua mea i whakapumau ake ake:
i whakatakotoria e ia he tikanga e kore e taka.

<span id="an_148:7">148:7</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa, i runga i te
whenua, e nga tarakona, e nga rire katoa;

<span id="an_148:8">148:8</span> E te kapura, e te whatu; e te hukarere,
e te kohu; e te tupuhi, e mahi nei i tana kupu;

<span id="an_148:9">148:9</span> E nga maunga, e nga puke katoa; e nga
rakau hua, e nga hita katoa;

<span id="an_148:10">148:10</span> E nga kirehe, e nga kararehe katoa; e
nga mea ngokingoki, e nga manu whai pakau:

<span id="an_148:11">148:11</span> E nga kingi o te whenua, e nga iwi
katoa; e nga rangatira, e nga kaiwhakawa katoa o te whenua:

<span id="an_148:12">148:12</span> E nga taitama, e nga taitamahine; e
nga koroheke ratou ko nga tamariki:

<span id="an_148:13">148:13</span> Kia whakamoemititia e ratou te ingoa
o Ihowa: nona anake hoki te ingoa e nui ana; kei runga ake i te whenua,
i te rangi, tona kororia.

<span id="an_148:14">148:14</span> Ko ia hoki te kaiwhakaara o te haona
o tana iwi; e whakamoemititia ana e ana tangata tapu katoa; e nga tama a
Iharaira, e te iwi e tata ana ki a ia. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_149:1">149:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Waiatatia ki
a Ihowa he waiata hou, me te whakamoemiti ki a ia i te whakaminenga o te
hunga tapu.

<span id="an_149:2">149:2</span> Kia hari a Iharaira ki tona kaihanga:
kia koa nga tama a Hiona ki to ratou Kingi.

<span id="an_149:3">149:3</span> Kia whakamoemiti ratou ki tona ingoa me
te kanikani ano: kia himene ratou ki a ia i runga i te timipera, i te
hapa.

<span id="an_149:4">149:4</span> E manako ana hoki a Ihowa ki tana iwi:
mana e whakaataahua te hunga mahaki ki te whakaoranga.

<span id="an_149:5">149:5</span> Kia koa te hunga tapu i runga i te
kororia: kia hamama ratou i te hari i runga i o ratou moenga.

<span id="an_149:6">149:6</span> ¶ Kia whai whakamoemiti o ratou mangai
ki te Atua, kia whai hoari matarua to ratou ringa;

<span id="an_149:7">149:7</span> Hei rapu utu i nga tauiwi, hei whiu i
nga iwi;

<span id="an_149:8">149:8</span> Hei herehere i o ratou kingi ki te
makameka, i o ratou tangata nunui ki nga here rino;

<span id="an_149:9">149:9</span> Hei whakaputa ki a ratou i te
whakaritenga kua oti te tuhituhi: No tona hunga tapu katoa tenei honore.
Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

<span id="an_150:1">150:1</span> ¶ Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.
Whakamoemititia te Atua i tona wahi tapu: whakamoemititia ia i te
kikorangi o tona kaha.

<span id="an_150:2">150:2</span> Whakamoemititia ia mo ana mahi nunui:
kia rite ki te hira o tona nui te whakamoemiti ki a ia.

<span id="an_150:3">150:3</span> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te tangi o
te tetere: whakamoemititia ia i runga i te hatere, i te hapa.

<span id="an_150:4">150:4</span> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te
timipera, i te kanikani: whakamoemititia ia i runga i nga mea aho, i nga
okana.

<span id="an_150:5">150:5</span> Whakamoemititia ia i runga i te
himipora tangi nui: whakamoemititia ia i runga i te himipora tangi
tiori.

<span id="an_150:6">150:6</span> E nga mea katoa e whai manawa ana,
whakamoemititia a Ihowa. Whakamoemititia a Ihowa.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
